[1,i_1,ii]	ānandam ekam amṛtam ajam vijñānam akṣaram asarvam sarvam abhayam namasyāmaḥ prajāpatim vedānteṣu vipratipadyante vipaścitaḥ kecid aprāmāṇyam manyante ātmanaḥ pramāṇa antara siddha tve teṣām anuvādaka tvam asiddha tve saṃbandha agrahaṇāt apadārtha tve vākyasya aviṣaya tvāt pravṛtti nivṛtti anupadeśe ca apuruṣa artha tvāt anye tu pratipatti kartavya tā prāmāṇya vyājena aprāmāṇyam eva āhuḥ anye tu karma vidhi virodhāt pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt ca śruta artha parigrahe upacarita arthān manyante tad nirāsa artham ucyate ānandam iti parām ca devatām guṇa abhidhāna lakṣaṇayā stutyā kāya vāc manaḥ prahvatā lakṣaṇayā ca praṇatyā pūjayati prakaraṇa artham ca upakṣipati vipratipatti nirākaraṇa mukhena vedāntānām evaṃbhūte arthe prāmāṇya pratipādanāt yatas bhavati eṣaḥ api prakaraṇa arthaḥ 
[1,iii^1]	atra kecid ānanda ātmaka tve brahmaṇaḥ ānanda rāgāt mumukṣu pravṛttiḥ syāt rāga nibandhanā ca pravṛttiḥ saṃsāra bījam iti na muktaye syāt śāntasya dāntasya ca ātmani darśanam ucyate na ca ānanda anurāgāt pravartamānaḥ śāntaḥ bhavati tasmāt sakala duḥkha atige brahma tattve duḥkhebhyaḥ udvignaḥ sukhebhyaḥ ca vīta rāgaḥ pravartamānaḥ mucyate ānanda śrutayaḥ ca sakala duḥkha atikramam eva āhuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hi kṣudh duḥkha ādi nivṛttau sukha śabdaḥ sā eva ca sukham iti anye na ca āśma ādau prasaṅgaḥ pratyak vṛtteḥ upalabhyamānāyāḥ sukha tvāt tad viśiṣṭa ātma upalabdheḥ vā tān pratyāha ānandam iti 
[1,iii^2]	na tāvat duḥkha nivṛttiḥ eva sukham yugapad sukha duḥkhayoḥ darśanāt saṃtāpavataḥ śīta hrade nimagna ardha kāyasya atha sati api animagna ardha kāya duḥkhe itarasya abhāvāt sukham iti kumbhīpāke pacyamānasya naraka antara duḥkha abhāvāt sukhitva prasaṅgaḥ eka indriya dvāra duḥkhasya ca indriya antar dvāra duḥkha abhāvāt itas ca aduḥkhasya api viṣaya viśeṣa saṃparkāt saṃvedya āhlāda utpatteḥ yatra api duḥkha vigamaḥ tatra api na tanmātram eva sukham anna pāna viśeṣa upādānāt duḥkha vigamaḥ hi yaiḥ taiḥ anna pānaiḥ sidhyati na ca sa viśeṣavān yena tad viśeṣāya tad sādhana viśeṣaḥ apekṣyeta sukhe tu atiśayavat tvādi uktā tad sādhana atiśaya apekṣā 
[2,i^1]	yat api manyante yadā api na anyat duḥkham nivartyam tadā api kāmasya duḥkha ātmaka tvāt tad nibarhaṇa rūpam sukham tatra api akāmasya viṣaya viśeṣa upabhoge na sukhitā syāt bhavati ca madhya sthaḥ api ramaṇīya viṣaya saṃparke hlādavān syāt etat yatra eva kāmaḥ saḥ eva sukhayati viṣayaḥ na itaraḥ tasmāt kāma nivṛttya eva viṣayāḥ sukhayitāraḥ anyathā yaḥ ekasya sukhaḥ sa sarvasya syāt kāma nivṛttyā tu sukha tve yatra yasya kāmaḥ abhiruciḥ saḥ eva tasya sukhaḥ iti yujyate tatra akāmasya api viṣaya viśeṣa upabhogāt kāma abhivyaktau tad nivṛttau tad sukhitvam iti tat api asāram yatas viṣaya upabhogāḥ na avaśyam kāma nibarhaṇāḥ uktam hi na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati iti tathā bhoga abhyāsam anu vivardhante rāgāḥ kauśalāni ca indriyāṇām iti viṣaya doṣa darśanāt api ca kāma nivṛttiḥ tatra upabhoga tulyaḥ āhlādaḥ syāt 
[2,i^2]	samāne ca prārthita artha lābhe pramoda bhedaḥ na syāt kāma nivṛtteḥ aviśeṣāt syāt etat kāma atireke tad nivṛttau sukha atiśaya abhimānaḥ itaratra anyathā iti tat ca na kāma atirekāt prayasyantam avāptaḥ arthaḥ na tathā prīṇayati yathā prārthitaḥ vinā prayāsāt upanataḥ tathā hi kleśāt avāptaḥ ayam iti na tena tathā prīyate yathā anāśaṃsita upanatena kāma abhāva mātre ca sukhe akāmita viṣaya upabhoge na bhoga avasthāyāḥ pūrva apare avasthe bhidyeyātām kāma pradhvaṃse vā para avasthāḥ na bhidyeta bhoga avasthāyām prabuddha adhvasta kāmaḥ eva iti ced pūrvā parayoḥ api dvayoḥ avasthayoḥ tarhi sukhī itaratra duḥkhī iti anubhava viruddham āpadyeta aprāptaḥ ca smaraṇa viparivartī viṣayaḥ kāmasya udbodhakaḥ prāptaḥ nivartakaḥ prāptasya udbodha tve na tatas nivṛttiḥ syāt 
[3,i]	na ca yatra kāmaḥ tatra sukham manoratha śata arthitasya api upabhogena kasyacid duḥkhi tva darśanāt sukha pūrvakaḥ tu kāmaḥ anubhūta tad bhāve tad darśanāt yā api kācid ananubhūte api jāti viśeṣa bhājām kāma pravṛttiḥ sā api prāc bhavīya anubhava nibandhanā yathā ca kasyacid kvacid kāmaḥ jāti bheda ādi nimittaḥ tathā kiñcid kasyacid sukham iti na avyavasthā api ca kāma nivṛttya api kecid dūyante tad abhāve viṣaya upabhoga sāmarthya abhāvāt na tarhi nivṛtti kāmāḥ nivṛtti kāmā viṣayam prati tasya kutaścid nimittāt anupabhogya tvāt kim iti tarhi dūyante anubhūta carasya tad janmanaḥ sukhasya aprāpteḥ yathā pitta ādi upahata indriyāḥ viśiṣṭebhyaḥ anna pānebhyaḥ nivṛtti kāmāḥ tathā eva kāma nivṛttyā tapyante tatra anubhūta cara tad janma āhlāda vicchedāt na anyaḥ hetuḥ tasmāt pratyātma vedanīya sukha pratyākhyānam ayuktam sukha saṅgi jana upacchandanāya tu tatrabhavadbhiḥ varṇitam iti paśyāmaḥ tat evam duḥkha nivṛtteḥ anyat sukham sa ca ānanda śabdasya mukhyaḥ arthaḥ śabda pramāṇake ca yathāśabdam pratipattiḥ yuktā 
[3,ii]	na ca rāga nibandhanā tatra pravṛttiḥ na hi icchā mātram rāgaḥ avidyā kṣiptam abhūta guṇa abhiniveśam rāgam ācakṣate tattva darśana vaimalyāt tu tattve cetasaḥ prasādaḥ abhiruciḥ abhīcchā na rāga pakṣe vyavasthāpyate yathā saṃsāra asāra tā tattva darśana niṣpannaḥ na udvegaḥ tatas dveṣa pakṣe anyathā sarva duḥkha atige api tattve tad dveṣa nibandhanā pravṛttiḥ iti saṃsāra anubandhaḥ syāt api ca dṛṣṭa para utkarṣa rāgibhyaḥ api indriya jayaḥ upadiśyate sādhana tvena kāma ādi tyāga ātmakaḥ tathā iha api bhaviṣyati katham ca tatra samīhita itara viṣaya abhiṣvaṅga niṣedhaḥ sarva niṣedhe apravṛtti darśanāt tathā uttama sukha rāga āditarasmāt upanatāt api nivṛttiḥ tathā ca uktam kāma ātma tā na praśastā na ca eva iha asti akāma tā iti 
[3,iii^1]	syāt etat ānandaḥ ced brahmaṇi saṃvedyaḥ kartuḥ anyat karma iti dvaita prasaṅgaḥ kartṛ karma bhāvaḥ ca na kriyām karaṇam ca antareṇa yatas tatas ānandam brahma iti ca na syāt tadvat tayā vyapadeśe advitīyam iti na yujyate asaṃvedane san api asat kalpaḥ iti vyartham tad saṃkīrtanam puruṣa artha tvāya hi tad saṃkīrtanam asaṃvedyaḥ ca katham puruṣa arthaḥ ucyate phalavat kartṛ vat ca idam draṣṭavyam tathā hi pramāṇasya phalam artha antaram anartha antaram vā sarva parīkṣakaiḥ pratijñāyate prajñāyate ca na ca tat asaṃvedyam tad asaṃvedya tve sarva asaṃvedya tva prasaṅgāt tad kṛta tvāt saṃvedya bhāvasya bhāvānām na ca saṃvedyam phala antara anupalabdheḥ anavasthā prasaṅgāt ca 
[3,iii^2]	tasmāt saṃvedyam ātma prakāśa tvāt asaṃvedyam ca viṣaya vat karma bhāva abhāvāt yathā ca kartari ātmani asaṃvedye saṃvid eva na syāt na hi tadā evam bhavati mayā idam viditam iti na hi ātmā saṃvedyaḥ phale viṣaye ca anusaṃdhātum śakyaḥ ananusaṃdhāne ca sva para saṃvedyayoḥ kaḥ atiśayaḥ na ca saṃvedyaḥ karma tve kartuḥ vyatireka prasaṅgāt anātma tva prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt ātma prakāśa tā eva tasya saṃvedya tā tathā brahmaṇaḥ sva ātma prakāśasya ānanda svabhāvaḥ na saṃvedyaḥ karma tva abhāvāt na ca asaṃvedyaḥ sva prakāśa tvāt tat kena kam paśyet iti api niṣedhaḥ karma viṣayaḥ tathā hi sarva karma pratyasta maya hetukaḥ eva saḥ ucyate yadā asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt iti 
[4,i^1]	anye manyante dvividhāḥ dharmāḥ bhāva rūpāḥ abhāva rūpāḥ ca iti tatra abhāva rūpāḥ na advaitam vighnanti yathā ekam amṛtam ajam iti na hi bheda udaya vyayānām nivṛttiḥ kiñcid vastu yena dvaitam āvahet ānandaḥ ca yadi bhāvaḥ tasya dharmi tve vijñānam dharmaḥ syāt atha vijñānam dharmi rūpam ānandaḥ dharmaḥ na hi ekasya dve rūpe yujyete virodhāt tatra vijñānam ānandam brahma iti bhāva rūpayoḥ ānanda brahmaṇoḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedāt advaita vighātaḥ syāt etat dharmaḥ api dharmiṇaḥ na bhinnaḥ bhede gavāśva vat dharma dharmi bhāva anupapatteḥ 
[4,i^2]	tat asat abhede api dharmi rūpavat tad anupapatteḥ tasmāt kathañcid bhinnaḥ dharmaḥ tathā ca ātyantika bheda abhāva śrutiḥ ekam eva advitīyam iti na yujyate evam yaḥ api ekasya rūpa dvayam pratipadyate tasmāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ brahmaṇaḥ duḥkha abhāva upādhiḥ eva ānanda śabdaḥ yathā sthūla abhāva ādi upādhayaḥ asthūlam anaṇva hrasvam ityādayaḥ śabdāḥ na ca vijñāna ānandayoḥ eka tvam eva śabda dvaya prayoga vaiyarthyāt katham ca aparyāya śabda abhidheyaḥ eka tvam tasmāt duḥkha uparamaḥ eva ānanda śabdasya brahmaṇi arthaḥ iti 
[5,i^1]	atra ucyate viśiṣṭasya āhlāda ātmanaḥ prakāśasya cāndramasasya iva śabda dvayena pratipādanāt na doṣaḥ yathā ca prakṛṣṭaḥ prakāśaḥ savitā iti na ca prakṛṣṭa prakāśa śabdayoḥ paryāya tvam atha ca ekaḥ eva abhyām artha viśeṣaḥ pratipādyate prakāśa viśeṣaḥ na hi prakarṣaḥ anyaḥ prakāśa rūpāt sa vitari na prakāśa rūpaḥ vā prakarṣāt api tu prakāśa bhedaḥ śabda dvaya upāyaḥ pratīyate tathā vijñānam ānandam brahma iti ānanda bhedaḥ vijñāna bhedaḥ vā brahma rūpam iti śabda dvayena avagamyate parama tām api asya kecid sādhana pāratantrya lakṣaṇāyāḥ kṣayitā lakṣaṇāyāḥ ca duḥkha tāyāḥ abhāvāt manyante tat api yathāśabdam pratipatteḥ śabda pramāṇake arthe na anumanyante na hi svarūpataḥ para ma tā saṃbhave virodhi asaṃsargāt upacaritā sā yuktā bhavitum tasmāt ātma prakāśa prakṛṣṭa ātma svabhāvam eva brahma iti yuktam evam ca laukika ānandaḥ etasya mātrā iti yujyate avacchedāt duḥkha nivṛttau tu duryojam etat 
[5,i^2]	itas ca ānanda svabhāvaḥ ātmā para prema āspada tvāt śrūyate hi para prema āspada tvam tat etat preyaḥ putrāt iti pratīyate ca tathā hi sarvasya iyam ātma āśīḥ kṛmeḥ api mā na bhūvam bhūyāsam iti sā ca priye avakalpate premā ca sukha ātmani na duḥkhe na ubhaya rūpa rahite dveṣāt upekṣaṇāt ca anye tu suṣupte sukham aham asva apsam iti parāmarśāt ātmani sukha anubhavam āhuḥ na hi ananubhave parāmarśaḥ evam syāt suṣupta abhyupagamaḥ ca na ca anyathā anubhave sukham iti parāmarśaḥ na ca tatra ātmanaḥ anyat anubhavanīyam asti tathā ca aharahar brahma loka avāptiḥ śrūyate tatra anyaḥ āhuḥ duḥkha uparamāt api tathā parāmarśa siddheḥ na ekāntataḥ sukhitva siddhiḥ tān pratyāhuḥ anyathā abhāve avagate duḥkha uparama nimittaḥ sukha śabdaḥ iti yujyate anyathā mukhya artha tā eva yuktā tatra āhuḥ ubhayathā vyapadeśasya darśanāt upapatteḥ ca na vyapadeśa mātrāt artha siddhiḥ iti alam ati vistareṇa 
[6,i^1]	atra kecid bhoga vyavasthānāt mukta saṃsāri vibhāga upapatteḥ ca dṛś śakteḥ ca arthavat tvāt sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt dṛśyena ca draṣṭuḥ anumānāt dṛśyasya ca sukha duḥkha moha bheda vat śabda ādi vibhāga upalabdheḥ ekatva śrutiḥ jāti deśa kāla vibhāga abhāva nimitta upacārāt manyante ātmā eva idam sarvam iti ca tādarthya nimitta upacārāt tān pratyucyate ekam iti indraḥ māyābhiḥ puru rūpaḥ īyate iti vyaktam eva nānā rūpa avagamaḥ māyā nibandhanaḥ darśitaḥ tatra katham eka tvam upacaritam iti vaktum śakyam tathā vyaktaḥ nānā tva niṣedhaḥ na iha nānā asti kiñcanaḥ iti nānātva darśana nindā ca mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti iti bheda darśanasya ca abhāvaḥ bheda dṛṣṭiḥ iva bhramāt yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati iti iva śabdena prakāśitaḥ na upacaritaḥ eka tve avakalpate 
[6,i^2]	kāmam upacāra ādaḥ tu eka tvam na tu bhāvikasya nānātvasya nivṛttiḥ sā api upacāreṇa eva ucyate iti ced na prayojana abhāvāt sati nimitte prayojane ca upacāraḥ na ca nānā tva nivṛtti upacāre prayojanam paśyāmaḥ viparyayāt ca abhyudayāya niḥśreyasāya vā nānā tva nivṛttiḥ upacaryeta sā hi sādhya sādhana ādi vibhāgam nivartayantī sarvatra ca ātmā abhimānam āvirbhāvayantī tad virodhinī syāt tathā hi sarvatas nivṛttasya niḥśreyasam iti avisaṃvādaḥ tathā ekam eva advitīyam iti avadhāraṇa advitīya śabdābhyām tasya eva arthasya punar punar abhidhānāt sarva prakāra bheda nivṛtti para tā śruteḥ lakṣyate abhyāse hi bhūyas tvam arthasya bhavati yathā aho darśanīyā aho darśanīyāḥ iti na nyūna tvam api dūratas eva upacarita tvam 
[7,i^1]	yat tu bhoga vyavasthānāt iti tatra ucyate kalpitāt api bhedāt bhoga vyavasthā siddheḥ asāram etat tathā hi ekasmin api ātmani sarva gate śarīra parimāṇe aṇu parimāṇe vā kalpita bheda nibandhanā bhoga vyavasthā dṛśyate pāde me vedanā śirasi me vedanā iti na hi pādasya śirasaḥ vā vedanayā abhisaṃbandhaḥ ajña tvāt śarīra parimāṇa ātma vādinaḥ api na avayavāḥ eva vedanā bhājaḥ ātmanaḥ tad viraha prasaṅgāt syāt etat aikātmye tadvat eva deha antara bhoga anusandhānam syāt anyat idānīm etat asti tāvat bhoga vyavasthā api ca tatra api na pradeśaḥ pradeśa antara vedanām anusaṃdadhāti tathā iha api na jīvaḥ jīva antara vedanām anusaṃdadhāti iti samānam tathā maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādiṣu sukha ādīnām varṇa saṃsthāna bheda vyavasthānam upalabhyate bheda abhāve api 
[7,i^2]	evam ca mukta saṃsāri vibhāgaḥ api upapannaḥ tathā hi ekaḥ api ātmā pradeśaiḥ sukha duḥkha ādibhiḥ yujyamānaḥ tatra baddhaḥ iva itaratra muktaḥ iva ca gamyate yathā malīmase darpaṇa tale malīmasam mukham viśuddhe viśuddham darpaṇa rahitam ca gamyamānam tad upādhi doṣa asaṃpṛktam syāt etat kalpanā pratipattuḥ pratyayasya dharmaḥ na vastu vyavasthāpayitum alam na khalu pratipattuḥ pratyayam anu viparivartante vastūni na ca upacaritāt kāryam upapadyate na hi upacarita agni bhāvaḥ māṇavakaḥ dahati udāhṛtā tu vyavasthā satyam vibhramaḥ hi saḥ atra api vibhrama tvam na daṇḍa vāritam kalpitaḥ api ca ahidaṃśaḥ maraṇa kāryāya kalpate pratisūryakaḥ ca prakāśa kāryāya 
[7,ii^1]	yat api dṛśyena eva draṣṭuḥ anumānāt draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ bhedaḥ dṛśyasya ca sukha ādi bheda upalabdheḥ na anātvam iti tat api asat na draṣṭarya prakāśe yatas dṛśyasya siddhiḥ asti iti uktam dṛśya bheda upalabdhiḥ ca na asti pramāṇasya anavacchedaka tvāt iti vakṣyate dṛś śakteḥ ca arthavat tvam sva ātma upayogāt na ca sva ātmani vṛtti virodhaḥ pradīpa vat pramāṇa phala vat ca iti uktam api ca ekatvaḥ eva ayam draṣṭṛ dṛśya bhāvaḥ avakalpate draṣṭuḥ eva cit ātmanaḥ tathā tathā vipariṇāmāt vivartanāt vā nānātve tu vivitkasvabhāvayoḥ asaṃsṛṣṭa paraspara svarūpayoḥ asambaddhayoḥ kīdṛśaḥ draṣṭṛ dṛśya bhāvaḥ na hi cityā saṃsṛṣṭam cetitam iti yujyate ekāntaḥkaraṇa saṃkrāntau asti eva sambandhaḥ iti ced na citeḥ śuddha tvāt apariṇāmāda pratisaṃkramāt ca 
[7,ii^2]	dṛśyā buddhiḥ citi sannidheḥ tad chāyayā vivartate iti ced atha kā iyam tad śāyatā atada ātmanaḥ tad avabhāsaḥ na tarhi paramārthataḥ dṛśyam dṛśyate paramārthataḥ ca adṛśyamānam draṣṭṛ vī atiriktam asti iti durbhaṇam yaḥ api manyate dṛśya tayā eva dṛśyam vyavasthāpyate na sambandhena darśanam ca idam iti parāgrūpa viṣayam sa vaktavyaḥ satyam parāgrūpa viṣayam tat tu ekasya eva ātmanaḥ tathā tathā vipariṇāmāt vivartanāt vā darpaṇa talaḥ iva ātmanaḥ tathā hi darpaṇa tala stham ātmānam vibhaktam iva ātmanaḥ pratyeti citeḥ tu vibhaktam asaṃsṛṣṭam tayā ca iti atas iti duravagamam evam ca draṣṭuḥ avyatirekaḥ dṛśyasyāmnāyate ātmani vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti tasmāt suṣṭhu uktam ekam iti 
[8,i^1]	kṣaṇika jñāna ātma vādinaḥ tu sa vāsana kleśa samucchedāt jñāna uparama lakṣaṇām eva brahma prāptim āhuḥ tathā ca śrūyate na pretya saṃjñā asti iti anye tu samucchinna sakala vāsana tvāt vidhūta viṣaya ākāra upaplava viśuddha jñāna utpāda lakṣaṇām anādi nidhana tve hi na apaneyam na upaneyam vā kiñcid asti iti tad arthāni śāstrāṇi tad arthāḥ ca pravṛttayaḥ vyarthāḥ syuḥ tathā hi vidyā svabhāvam ced na kiñcid nivartavyam avāptavyam vā syāt avidyāyāḥ abhāvāt vidyāyāḥ ca bhāvāt avidyā svabhāvam ced tasya nitya tve pūrva svabhāva tyāgāt svabhāva antara anāpatteḥ ca evam ubhaya svabhāva tve api vidyāyāḥ prāpta tvāt avidyāyāḥ ca ucchettum aśakya tvāt tān pratyāha amṛtam ajam iti na ca śāstrāṇām mukti arthānām ca pravṛttīnām vaiyarthyam avidyāyāḥ nivartya tvāt sarva pravādeṣu ca anādiḥ api avidyā ucchedya abhyupagamyate 
[8,i^2]	na brūmaḥ anādeḥ na ucchedaḥ iti kim tu nityasya brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvasya atha avidyā na brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ artha antaram brahmaṇaḥ āpadyeta na vā syāt tatra kim nivartyam atha matam agrahaṇam avidyā sā katham artha antaram syāt na ca anivartyā sarva pramāṇa vyāpārāṇām agrahaṇa nivṛtti artha tvāt tat api ayuktam tattva agrahaṇa ātmikayā vidyayā nivartyate sā ca nityāḥ brahmaṇi na ca brahmaṇaḥ anyaḥ asti yasya tattva agrahaṇam brahmaṇi prayatnalabhyayā vidyayā nivartyeta brahmaṇi tu yugapad grahaṇa agrahaṇe vipratiṣiddhe avipratiṣedhe vā na kadācid avidyā nivartyeta yasya tu viparyaya grahaṇam avidyā tasya brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ ced sa nityaḥ katham nivartyeta asvabhāvaḥ ced artha antaram āpadyeta kasya ca tat iti vācyam brahmaṇaḥ anyasya abhāvāt brahmaṇaḥ eva iti ced vipratiṣedhaḥ tasya vidyā svarūpa tvāt avipratiṣedhe vā kena nivṛttiḥ 
[9,i^1]	atra ucyate na avidyā brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ na artha antaram na atyantam asatī na api satī evam eva iyam avidyā māyā mithyā avabhāsaḥ iti ucyate svabhāvaḥ ced kasyacid anyaḥ ananyaḥ vā parama arthaḥ eva iti na avidyā atyanta asattve kha puṣpa sadṛśī na vyavahāra aṅgam tasmāt anirvacanīyā sarva pravādibhiḥ ca ittham iyam āstheyā tathā hi śūnya vādinā sattve yathārtha darśanam na avidyā kha puṣpa tulya tve na vyavahāra aṅgam vijñāna mātra vādinaḥ api yathāvabhāsam jñāna sadbhāve na artha apahnavaḥ nīla pīta ādeḥ jñeya ākārasya bahis avabhāsān apahnavāt atyanta asattve bahis avabhāsa ayogāt kha puṣpa vat 
[9,i^2]	bāhya artha vādinām api anitya ādiṣu nitya ādi khyātayaḥ rajata ādi vibhrāntayaḥ ca avabhāsamāna rūpa sadbhāve na avidyā tvam aśnu vīran na atyanta asattve tad nibandhanaḥ kaścana vyavahāraḥ syāt syāt etat avabhāsamānam rūpam mā bhūt avabhāsaḥ tu san ā iva sa ca avidyā iti gīyate na etat sāram avabhāsamāne asati tad avabhāsaḥ api satyataḥ durnirūpaḥ avabhāsa mātram tu syāt tad avabhāsaḥ iti api bhrāntiḥ eva tasmāt na avidyā satī na api asati iti atas eva ca asyāḥ nivṛttiḥ adṛḍha svabhāvāyāḥ māyā mātra tvāt anyathā svabhāve dṛḍham vyavasthitāyāḥ katham anyathātvam svabhāva hānāt śūnya tve svayam nivṛtta tvāt evam ca na advaitahānam na nivartanīyasya abhāvaḥ vā 
[10,i]	yat tu kasya avidyā iti jīvānām iti brūmaḥ nanu na jīvāḥ brahmaṇaḥ bhidyante evam hi āha anena jīvena ātma anupraviśyaḥ iti satyam paramārthataḥ kalpanayā tu bhidyante kasya punar kalpanā bhedikā na tāvat brahmaṇaḥ tasya vidyā ātmanaḥ kalpanā śūnyatvāt na api jīvānām kalpanāyāḥ prāk tad abhāvāt itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt kalpanā adhīnaḥ hi jīva vibhāgaḥ jīva āśrayā kalpanā iti 
[10,ii^1]	atra kecid āhuḥ vastu siddhau eva doṣaḥ na asiddham vastu vastu antara niṣpattaye alam na māyā mātre na hi māyāyām kācid anupapattiḥ anupapadyamāna arthā eva hi māyā upapadyamāna artha tve yathārtha bhāvāt na māyā syāt anye tu anādi tvāt ubhayoḥ avidyā jīvayoḥ bīja aṅkura santānayoḥ iva na itaretara āśrayam aprakḷptim āvahati iti varṇayanti tathā ca uktam avidyā upādānava ādibhiḥ anādiḥ aprayojanā ca avidyā iti tatra anādi tvā anna itaretara āśraya tva doṣaḥ aprayojana tvāt na bheda prapañca sarga prayojana paryanuyoga avakāśaḥ yat eke paryanuyuñjate prayojanam anuddiśya na mandaḥ api pravartate iti tatra parasya brahmaṇaḥ prapañca sarga prayojanam vācyam na tāvat para anugrahaḥ prāk sargāt anugrāhyāṇām abhāvāt duḥkha uttara tvāt ca sargasya na ātma artha krīḍā ādiḥ āpta kāma tvāt iti tasya avidyā nibandhana tve sarge na avakāśaḥ na hi avidyā prayojanam apekṣya pravartate na hi gandharvanagara ādi vibhramāḥ samuddiṣṭa prayojanāḥ bhavanti 
[10,ii^2]	tathā puruṣasya viśuddhasya na aśuddhā vikṛtiḥ bhavet iti api prayuktam avidyā nibandhane sarga vibhāge api ca kṛtārthānām āpta kāmānām eva krīḍā ādi pravṛttiḥ ullāsāt prārthanā parikṛṣṭa cetasām tu rati virahiṇām anabhimatā eva krīḍā bhavati na ca vaiṣamyanaiḥ ghṛṇya doṣaḥ na hi māyākārasya vividham prapañcam darśayataḥ aṅga sākalya vaikalya vibhāgena rāga dveṣa vibhāgaḥ citrapusta ādi kṛtām vā vikala avikala ādi bhedena citrāṇi tāni tāni kurvatām bālānām ca mṛṇmaya ādibhiḥ pratikṛti bhedaiḥ vicitraiḥ krīḍatām na teṣu kiñcid vaiṣamyam nairghṛṇyam vā karma āśaya anurodhena ca vidadhataḥ vaicitryam na doṣaḥ iti ācāryāḥ na ca anīśvara tva doṣaḥ na hi sevā bheda anurodhena phala bheda pradaḥ prabhuḥ aprabhuḥ bhavati tathā śuddhasya api aśuddhaḥ vikāraḥ na hi prakṛti vikārayoḥ atyantam availakṣaṇyam prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ eva na syāt dravāṇām ca apām karaka ādiḥ kaṭhinaḥ vikāraḥ tathā acetanasya gomayasya cetanaḥ vṛścikaḥ ityādi bahuvidham prakṛti vikāra vailakṣaṇyam utprekṣitavyam iti alam ati prasaṅgena 
[11,i^1]	nanu jīvāḥ api brahma tattva avyatirekāt viśuddha svabhāvāḥ tat katham teṣu avidyā vakāśaḥ vārtam etat na ca tāvat bimbāt avadātāt pratibimbam kṛpāṇa ādiṣu bhinnam atha ca tatra śyāma tā ādiḥ aśuddhiḥ avakāśam labhate vibhramaḥ saḥ iti ced samānam etat jīvānām api aśuddhiḥ vibhramaḥ anyathā duravāpa eva viśuddhiḥ syāt iti uktam syāt etat kṛpāṇa ādayaḥ mukhe vibhrānti hetavaḥ tathā iha api vibhrama hetuḥ vācyaḥ anādau vibhrame hetu anveṣaṇam asāmpratam iva tathā ca svapna ādi vat avidyāyāḥ pravṛttiḥ tasya kiṅkṛtāḥ iti pratyuktam nanu svābhāvikyana ādiḥ avidyāḥ nirhetuḥ sā katham ucchidyeta sarva śāstrāṇi eva tāvat naisargikyāḥ avidyāyāḥ ucchedāya prasthitāni api ca pārthivānām aṇūnām śyāma tā anādiḥ pāka jena varṇena nivartyate 
[11,i^2]	nanu svābhāvikam api kiñcid vilakṣaṇa pratyaya upanipātāt nivartatām aikātmya vādinaḥ tu anāgantuka arthasya tad abhāvāt kutas nivṛttiḥ na khalu ātma svabhāvaḥ eva vidyā avidyā nivartikā avidyāyāḥ tayā saha vṛtteḥ avirodhāt virodhe vā nitya nivṛtteḥ nityam uktam jagat syāt na ca vidyā antaram āgantukam virodhi nivartakam aikātmya vāde vyatiriktasya tasya ayogāt āgantukasya brahma svabhāva tva anupapatteḥ ca tat uktam svābhāvikīm avidyām tu na ucchettum kaścid arhati vilakṣaṇa upapāte hi naśyet svābhāvikam kvacid na tu aikātmya abhyupāyānām hetuḥ asti vilakṣaṇaḥ iti atra ucyate uktam etat jīvānām avidyā kaluṣita tvam na brahmaṇaḥ tat hi sadā viśuddha nitya prakāśam anāgantuka artham anyathā brahma bhūyam gatasya api na avidyā nivarteta 
[11,i^3]	tatra anirmokṣaḥ atha brahma eva saṃsarati brahma eva mucyate eka m uktau sarva mukti prasaṅgaḥ yatas bheda darśanena brahma eva saṃsarati abheda darśanena ca mucyate teṣām ca nisarga ja avidyā kaluṣāṇām vilakṣaṇa pratyaya vidyā udayena upapadyate avidyā nivṛttiḥ na hi jīveṣu nisarga jāḥ vidyā asti avidyā eva hi naisargikī tasyāḥ āgantukyāḥ vidyayā pravilayaḥ avyatireke api ca brahmaṇaḥ jīvānām bimba pratibimba vat vidyā avidyā vyavasthā vyākhyātā kena punar upāyena avidyā nivartate śravaṇa manana dhyāna abhyāsaiḥ brahmacarya ādibhiḥ ca sādhana bhedaiḥ śāstra uktaiḥ katham yaḥ ayam śravaṇa manana pūrvakaḥ dhyāna abhyāsaḥ pratiṣiddha akhila bheda prapañce saḥ eṣa na iti na iti ātmani sa vyaktam eva bheda darśana pratiyogī tat nivartayati 
[11,i^4]	sa ca sāmānyena bheda darśanam pravilāpayan ātmanā api pravilīyate na ca śrotṛ śravaṇa śrotavya ādi vibhāga parihāṇyāḥ vibhāga antara nivṛtti viṣayāḥ śravaṇa ādayaḥ api tu sāmānyena tathā ca tasmin api pravilīne svacchaḥ pariśuddhaḥ asya ātmā prakāśate yathā rajaḥ samparka kaluṣitam udakam dravya viśeṣa cūrṇa rajaḥ prakṣiptam rajaḥ ntarāṇi saṃharat su ayam api saṃhriyamāṇam su acchām svarūpa avasthām upanayati evam eva śravaṇa ādibhiḥ bheda darśane pravilīyamāne viśeṣa abhāvāt tad gate ca bhede svacche pariśuddhe svarūpe jīvaḥ avatiṣṭhate avidyayā eva tu brahmaṇaḥ jīvaḥ vibhaktaḥ tad nivṛttau brahma svarūpam eva bhavati yathā ghaṭa ādi bhede tad ākāśam pariśuddham parama ākāśam eva bhavati syāt etat katham bhedena eva bhedaḥ pratisaṃhriyate 
[11,i^5]	bheda pratipakṣa tvāt yathā rajasā rajaḥ iti uktam vyaktam eva bheda atīta brahmaṇi śravaṇa manana dhyāna abhyāsānām bheda darśana pratipakṣa tvam avidyā anubandhe api yathā payaḥ payaḥ jarayati svayam ca jīryati yathā ca viṣam viṣa antaram śamayati svayam ca śāmyati yathā uktam vidyām ca avidyām ca yaḥ tad veda ubhayam saha avidyayā mṛtyum tīrtvā vidyayā amṛtam aśnute etat uktam bhavati vidyā avidye dve api upāya upeya bhāvāt sahite na avidyām antareṇa vidyā udayaḥ asti sādhyā tarhi tathā ca kṛtaka tvāt anitya tvam atas āha avidyayā mṛtyum iti eṣaḥ arthaḥ na avidyā vidyāyāḥ sādhanam kim tu avidyayā śravaṇa ādi lakṣaṇayā api avidyā eva nivartate mṛtyuḥ iti avidyā eva ucyate 
[11,i^6]	tasyām nivṛttāyām vidyā rūpa upalakṣitam amṛtam aśnute svarūpa avasthānam sphaṭika maṇiḥ iva upādhi āśraya nibandhana uparāga tyāgāt antareṇa prayatna antaram vidyā svarūpe avatiṣṭhate iti anyaḥ arthaḥ na avidyā vidyā rahitā asti tathā hi bheda darśanam api na prakāśa śūnyam tad abhāve na bhedaḥ prakāśeta tasmāt paraḥ eva prakāśaḥ tathā tathā prakāśate yathā uktam tam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti kim tu avidyā anubaddhaḥ yathā uktam sarvam darśanam anyūnam avikalpam vikalpitam iva tu ayam āntaraḥ puruṣaḥ abhimanyate tathā na vidyā aikātmya śravaṇa ādi lakṣaṇā vinā avidyayā śrotṛ śravaṇa ādi vibhāga anubaddha tvāt tatra avidyayā eva vidyā pratyāsannayā vibhāga darśanam avidyām tīrtvā vidyā lakṣaṇe nitye svarūpe avatiṣṭhate pratibimba kaluṣitam iva udakam tad nivṛttau 
[11,i^7]	syāt etat aikātmye vibhāgasya asatya tvāt tad adhiṣṭhāna śravaṇa ādayaḥ api asatyāḥ katham kasmaicid kāryāya syuḥ asatyāt ca satya pratipattiḥ mithyā eva yathā dhūmaḥ iti mithyā gṛhītāt bāṣpāt iti ucyate na ayam niyamaḥ asatyam na kasmaicid kāryāya bhavati iti bhavati hi māyā prīteḥ bhayasya ca nimittam asatyam ca satya pratipatteḥ yathā rekhā gavayaḥ lipi akṣarāṇi ca syāt etat svarūpeṇa idam satyam na śūnyam aikātmya vādinaḥ tu sva rūpeṇa api upāyānām asatya tā ucyate santu sva rūpeṇa satyāḥ yena tu rūpeṇa pratipādakāḥ tat asatyam kārya upayoga rahitā svarūpa satyatā vyarthā api ca abheda darśana upāyāḥ api na sva rūpeṇa mithyā yatas brahmā eva eṣām svarūpam tatra brahma eva avidyā anubaddham brahma prāpti upāyaḥ yathā rekhā ādayaḥ kakāraḥ ayam gavayaḥ ayam iti avidyamāna rūpeṇa eva varṇa ādīnām bodhakāḥ 
[11,i^8]	yaḥ api manyate na rekhā gavayaḥ gavayatvena gavaya antarāṇām pratipatti hetuḥ na rekhā varṇa tvena kim tu sādṛśyāt etad sadṛśaḥ gavayaḥ iti rekhā ca samayāt īdṛśīm rekhām dṛṣṭvā ayam varṇaḥ smartavyaḥ iti tasya loka virodhaḥ tathā hi bālāḥ hi rekhāsu varṇa tvena eva vyutpādyante loke abhedena ca vyapadeśaḥ ayam gavayaḥ iti ākhyātuḥ pratipattuḥ ca gavayaḥ ayam mayā dṛṣṭaḥ iti tathā asatyāt pratibimbāt ca adṛṣṭasya pratibimba hetoḥ viśiṣṭa deśa avasthasya anumānam na mṛṣā śabdāt ca nityāt asatya dīrgha ādi vibhāga bhājaḥ artha bheda pratipattiḥ na mithyā tathā mithyā ahi daṃśaḥ maraṇa hetuḥ tatas ca maraṇa mūrcchā ādi anumānam na vitatham kāla ādi bheda yuktāt satya ahi daṃśāt iva 
[14,i^1]	yasya eva kṣaṇika jñānam ātmā tasya eva tu upaneya apaneyā sambhavān mokṣa śostrāṇām mukti arthānām ca pravṛttīnām vaiyarthyam kṣaṇikasya svarasena eva nirvāṇāt anādheya atiśaya tvāt ca ekasmin kṣaṇe viśeṣa aviśeṣa vibhāga abhāvāt kṣaṇasya abhedya tvāt yadi matam santatau upaneyam apaneyam ca samasti iti tat asat kartā bhoktā ca saṃsārī na ca santatiḥ avastu tvāt kartrī bhoktrī vā katham vāsataḥ mukti bandhau atha matam na atyantam asatī santatiḥ na api satī kalpanayā tu satī tad vimokṣāya śāstrāṇi pravṛttayaḥ ca iti kalpitaḥ tarhi saṃsarati vimucyate ca kalpita viṣayau ca saṃsāra vimokṣau api kalpitau eva tat etat asmābhiḥ ucyamānam kim na bhavataḥ abhimatam uktam etat kalpita viṣayau eva saṃsāra mokṣau na parasmin parama arthe api ca abhyupagamya api kṣaṇikam vijñānam anādinidhanāyāḥ eva santateḥ mukti saṃsārau abhyupetau tathā hi santateḥ anādi tvāt saṃsārasya avastu tvāt ca na utpādaḥ na ucchedaḥ avastu tvāt antyakṣaṇa anupapatteḥ ca 
[14,i^2]	sa hi antyaḥ kṣaṇaḥ kiñcid kāryam ārabheta vā na vā ārambhe na antyaḥ iti tad abhāva at na ucchedaḥ anārambhe sarva śakti virahāt asat lakṣaṇāt tasya asattvam tasmin asati sarve api anena eva krameṇa asantaḥ santāninaḥ syuḥ tad abhāve santānaḥ eva na asti kasya ucchedaḥ atha ārabhate eva kāryam antyaḥ santāna antare sārvajñe sati hetu phala bhāve katham santāna antaram na hetu phala bhāvāt anyat eka santateḥ vyavasthāpakam na hetu phala bhāva mātrāt eka santati vyavasthā api tu upādāna hetu phala bhāvāt na ca sārvajñasya jñānasya cara makṣaṇaḥ upādānam ālambana pratyayaḥ hi saḥ samanantara pratyayaḥ ca upādānam sva santati patita samanantara pratyaya janyam ca sārvajñam jñānam ālambana pratyayaḥ asya cara makṣaṇaḥ yadi tulya jātīyam upādānam na mukta citta sārvajña jñānayoḥ tulya jātīya tā na asti yaḥ api manyate vilakṣaṇa kārye santati ucchedaḥ iti tasya rūpa jñāna prabandhe viṣaya antara vijñānāt nirvāṇa prasaṅgaḥ katham cit tulya tā āyām anirvāṇam iti alam ati prasaṅgena 
[15,i^1]	kecid tu vijñāna guṇam avijñāna svabhāvam ātma tattvam icchantaḥ samutkhāta sakala viśeṣa guṇe svarūpe tasya sthitim brahma prāptim āhuḥ sā hi tasya avasthā deha indriya ādi upādhibhiḥ akṛta avacchedāḥ bṛhatī brahma iti gīyate jñāna svabhāva tve ca sarva gatasya deha indriya nirapekṣasya nitya tvāt jñāna svarūpasya sannihita vividha jñeya bhedasya bṛhattaraḥ saṃsāraḥ syāt atha na vijānāti kiñcid na tarhi jñāna svarūpaḥ sa karmakaḥ hi jānātyarthaḥ na asati karma sambandhe yujyate tān pratyāha vijñānam iti kutas śrūyate hi satyam jñānam anantam brahma vijñānam ānandam ityādi na ca ukta doṣaḥ 
[15,i^2]	yathā dāhakaḥ api vahniḥ upanītam dāhyam dahati na anupanītam adāhyam ca yathā ca sphaṭika darpaṇa ādayaḥ su acchāḥ prakāśa svabhāvāḥ api yat eva upanidhīyate yogyam ca tad chāyā āpattyā tat eva darśayanti evam ayam puruṣaḥ bhoga āyatana śarīra sthaḥ bhoga sādhana indriya upanītān śabda ādīn bhuṅkte tad chāyā āpattyā nitya caitanyaḥ api atas ca na sarvasya sarva darśi tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca muktau bāhya viṣaya upabhogaḥ syāt etat sarva gatasya sarvam eva viṣaya tvena vartate tatra kim upaneyam ucyate yasya api ajñasya ātmanaḥ jñānam manaḥ saṃyoga ādi janyam tasya api sarva manobhiḥ sarva ātmanām saṃyogāt katham upabhoga vyavasthā 
[15,i^3]	manaḥ saṃyoga mukhena sarve hi tad viṣayāḥ viṣaya tve asya vartante atha asya karma nibandhana tvāt upabhogasya karma nimittā vyavasthā sā citi rūpa ātma vādinaḥ api na daṇḍa vāritā api ca asya abheda darśana pariniṣpattyā sarvasmin ātma bhāvam āpanne dṛśya abhāvāt eva na darśanam dṛś svabhāvasya api dagdhuḥ iva vahneḥ dāhya abhāvāt na dāhaḥ prakāśasya iva ca prakāśya abhāvāt na prakāśaka tā tat uktam na hi draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ vidyate avināśi tvāt na tu tat dvitīyam asti tatas anyat vibhaktam yat paśyet yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt ityādi vijñāna ādi viśeṣa guṇa nivṛtti lakṣaṇā ca muktiḥ uccheda pakṣāt na bhidyate 
[15,i^4]	na hi sataḥ api ātyantikaḥ darśana abhāvaḥ abhāvāt viśiṣyate kaḥ ca sarvatas preyasaḥ ātmanaḥ abhāvam abhikāṅkṣeditya puruṣa arthaḥ mokṣaḥ syāt syāt etat vividha duḥkha upaśama tvāt ātma ucchedaḥ api puruṣeṇa arthyate dṛśyante hi tīvra pāpa roga grastāḥ sva ucchedāya yatamānāḥ satyam pravṛddha gada unmūlita nikhila sukhāḥ duḥkha mayīm iva mūrtim udvahantaḥ na tu evam saṃsāriṇaḥ vividha vicitra deva ādi ānanda bhāginaḥ tatra yathā vividha duḥkha uparama tvāt puruṣa artha tvam tathā vividha sukha uparama tvāt apuruṣa artha tvam api yasya tu nirmṛṣṭa nikhila duḥkha anuṣaṅgā parama ānanda saṃvedanā avasthā tasya eva aikāntikam puruṣa artha tvam iti alam ati prasaṅgena 
[16,i^1]	akṣaram iti śabda ātma tām āha viśeṣeṇa sāmānyasya lakṣaṇāt apariṇāmi tvam vā pariṇāme pūrva dharma nivṛtteḥ kṣaraṇasya bhāvāt tad vyudāsena katham tāvat śabda ātma tā param ca aparam ca brahma yadā uṅkāraḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ na ca idam abhidheya apekṣam kāra pratyaya antasya śabda svarūpa paratvāt avarṇāt api varṇa samudāyāt paraḥ kāra pratyayaḥ dṛśyate eva kāraḥ kimarthaḥ kimarthaḥ cakāraḥ iti nanu idam anyathā eva vyācakṣate sarva viśeṣa atigasya brahmaṇaḥ upāsitum aśakyatvāt pratīkā upadeśaḥ ayam asmin ālambane brahma upāsitavyam yathā devatāyāḥ sākṣāt pūjā sambhavāt tad lāñchane dāruṇī aśmani vā pūjā vidhānam tat buddhyā tathā dhyātā devatā sā prasīdati iti 
[16,i^2]	anena vā abhidhānena tat dhyeyam praṇavasya tad abhidhāna tvāt ucyate om iti ātmānam dhyāyatha om iti yuñjīta iti yatra yoga aṅga tā śrūyate tatra evam yatra tu yuñjīta iti ādeḥ aśravaṇāt tādātmyaḥ eva paryavasyati vākyam tatra na ittham yathā om iti brahma om iti idam sarvam iti atra hi sarva vāc anugamena tad atyāgāt oṅkāraḥ vācaḥ tattvam iti darśayitvā vāc rūpa atyāgāt ca rūpa prapañcasya oṅkāraḥ eva idam sarvam iti upasaṃharati yatra api etena eva param puruṣam abhidhyāyītaḥ iti śravaṇam tat api sarva ātma bhāva pratipādana pūrvakam na ca sarva ātma bhāvaḥ aupacārikaḥ stuti arthaḥ iti yuktam mukhya artha tve api avirodhāt 
[16,i^3]	sarvasya hi pratyakṣa ādi anavaseyam śāstra gamyam idam rūpam na viruddhyate na hi pramāṇa antareṇa anavagamaḥ pramāṇa antarasya viṣayam apaharati tasmāt vidvān iti ca sārvātma vidaḥ eva tena dhyāna upadeśaḥ na ca tad anyatas tasmāt anantaram eva vākyam tatra paryavasitam tatas adhigata sārvātmyasya sataḥ dhyāna upadeśaḥ atha vā vāc eva viśvā bhuvanāni jajñe vāc eva idam bubhuje vāc uvācaḥ iti ādau vācaḥ sārvātmyam śrūyate tathā vāc sūkte vācaḥ sarva ātma tvam sarva īśitvam ca pradarśitam aham rudrebhiḥ vasubhiḥ carāmi iti vācā eva yathā ātmani pratibuddhena vāmadevena aham manuḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca iti api ca prakṛti rūpa anvitāḥ vikārāḥ vāgrūpa anvitam ca jagat 
[16,i^4]	atas vācaḥ vipariṇāmaḥ vivartaḥ vā avasīyate katham tad anugamaḥ tad uparāga vijñāna vedanīya tvāt tathā hi dhūmāt atra agniḥ iti pratipatteḥ vyadhikaraṇa tayā vyaktam vailakṣaṇyam śabdāt artha avagamasya saṃvedyate sarveṇa itas ca etat evam yaḥ tu śabdayoḥ viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa bhāvaḥ avagamyate nīlam utpalam iti artha gataḥ eva asau anyathā yathā ūrdhva tve kāka nilayanāt sthāṇuḥ iti paraspara vyavacchinnābhyām arthābhyām artha antara pratītiḥ tathā syāt api ca dhūmaḥ iva śabde pratipatti hetau na tādrūpyeṇa niścayaḥ syāt na ca dhūmāt pramāṇa antarāt vā agnau niścayaḥ dhūma rūpa anukārī bhavati bhavati tu pramāṇa antarāt api artheṣu niścayaḥ śabda rūpa parāmarśī 
[16,i^5]	tad darśanāt śabdāt api pratipattau tathā pratipattiḥ na tu ānantarya nimittā bhrāntiḥ iti adhyavasyāmaḥ bālānām api ca yeyam anya parihāreṇa stana ādau pravṛttiḥ sā naḥ idam iti aniścinvatām bhavitum arhati na aniścite sthāṇau puruṣe vā anyatara nibandhanā pravṛttiḥ na ca niścayaḥ śabda anurāga śūnyaḥ iti teṣām api pūrva janma śabda bhāvanā bhājām vāc rūpa uparaktam eva jñānam niścīyate tathā ca tad rūpa upagrāhyam jagat tat vivartaḥ iti pratīmaḥ api ca santi arthāḥ vyāvahārikāḥ yeṣām na śabda vivartāt anyat tattvam tad sāmānyāt itare api tathā avasātavyāḥ yathā kuryāt na kuryāt iti vidhi niṣedhau vākya arthaḥ samūhaḥ asantaḥ ca alāta cakra śaśa viṣāṇa ādayaḥ 
[16,i^6]	tatra na tāvat vidhi niṣedhau bhūte pravṛtti nivṛttī na ca vartamāne na bhaviṣyantyau apākṣīt pacati pakṣyati iti aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt kārye iti ced na kāla traya atirekeṇa kāryatvasya anirūpaṇāt tasmāt pravṛtti nivṛtti anuguṇam avastukam pratibhā mātram vidhi niṣedhaḥ ca syātām na ca anālambanā jñāna svabhāva tvāt pratibhā yuktā na ca sā śabda rūpa parāmarśa vikalā tasmāt pravṛtti nivṛttyā anuguṇyena śabda tattvam eva tathā tathā avabhāsate iti sāmpratam evam vākya arthaḥ saṃsargaḥ na saṃsargi vyatirekeṇa kaścid na saṃsargya saṃsargi rūpa atiriktaḥ na jñeya śūnyam jñānam na vikalpa pratyayaḥ vāc rūpa uparāga rahitaḥ iti vāc tattvam eva tathā tathā vivartate iti nyāyyam evam samūhe vanāt au asatsu ca alāta cakra ādiṣu yojanīyam 
[16,i^7]	api ca yadi api ṣaḍja ādiṣu gavā ādiṣu ca prāk śabdāt jñānam asti tathā api na tādṛś yādṛś śabda niveśāt uttarasmin kāle aviviktā hi prāk pratipattiḥ sphuṭatarā vivekavatī paścāt tathā ca gopāla avi pāla ādayaḥ viveka jñāna siddhaye saṃjñām niveśayanti evam ca śabda saṃsparśe arthe bodha utkarṣa darśanāt tad pratihāre ca saṃcetitānām api asaṃcetita kalpa tvāt pathi gacchataḥ tṛṇa ādīnām apakarṣāt vāc rūpa adhīnam eva citaḥ citi tvam vāc śaktiḥ eva vā citiḥ tad pratisaṃhāre api sūkṣmā vāc śaktiḥ iti eke sarvathā vāc rūpa adhīnaḥ jñeya bodhaḥ iti sarvam jñeyam vā ac rūpa anvitam gamyate iti tad vikāraḥ tad vivartaḥ vā mṛdaḥ iva ghaṭa ādayaḥ candramasaḥ iva jala taraṅga candramasaḥ iti 
[16,i^8]	anye tu mṛd ādi dṛṣṭānta darśanāt pariṇāmi tām brahmaṇaḥ manyante tat apākriyate akṣaram iti kutas dhruvaḥ nityaḥ iti tatra tatra śruteḥ atha matam pariṇāmi tve api tattva avighātāt na nityatā vyāhanyate yathā uktam yasmin vikriyamāṇe api tattvam na vihanyate tat api nityam iti satyam tathā api tu yat viśuddham ātma rūpam tasya abhāvāt sarva ātmanā pariṇatau anitya tvam eka deśa pariṇatau sāvayava tvāt nitya tvam eka tvam ca vyāhanyete tat etat viśuddha tvam nitya tvam eka tvam ca ākāśa kalpe brahmaṇi avakalpate kalpita avacchede akalpita avacchedam api ākāśam anavacchinnam asti eva atha kalpita eka deśa pariṇāmaḥ sa kalpanayā eva iti suṣṭhu uktam akṣaram iti 
[19,i]	kecid sarva gandhaḥ sarva rasaḥ iti ādi śruteḥ sarva ātma tām brahmaṇaḥ upāgaman evam ca viṣaya upabhoga upapatteḥ prakāśa svabhāvasya ātmanaḥ viṣayāḥ yuktam yat prakāśeran anya tve tu jaḍānām prakāśanam asambhāvanīyam iti tān pratyāha asarvam iti kutas asthūlam anaṇva hrasvam iti sarva bheda uparāga pratiṣedhāt sarva bheda aviyogāt ca anirmokṣaḥ na hi svabhāvāt viyojayitum vastu śakyam vahniḥ iva auṣṇyāt atha api kathañcid viyojyeta tathā api bheda prapañca prabandhasya anucchedāt viyoga abhāvāt nitya saṃsāritā syāt sarvathā aśanāyā pipāsā ādi prapañcaḥ asya ātmā tad prapañcasya ca ucchedaḥ na iṣyate tatra ekātmya vādinaḥ anirmokṣaḥ ātma bheda vādinaḥ tu kasyacid ucchinnaḥ kasyacid na iti mukta saṃsāri vibhāgaḥ tasmāt na prapañca ātmakam brahma avidyā vikrīḍitam eva prapañcaḥ iti sāmpratam 
[20,i^1]	yadi tarhi avidyā krīḍitam eva prapañcaḥ prapañca śūnya tā tarhi parama arthaḥ sā eva astu brahma parama artha tvāt tathā ca prapañca niṣedhena eva tad rūpam śrāvyate saḥ eṣa na iti na iti asthūlam anaṇva hrasvam iti ca tatra āha sarvam iti etat uktam bhavati brahmaṇaḥ na sarva ātma tā sarvam tu brahma ātmakam brahma rūpeṇa rūpavat na tu śūnyam eva nitya mukti prasaṅgena tad artha upadeśa pravṛtti vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt nitya mukti tve api avidyā nibandhanaḥ saṃsāraḥ iti ced yadi grahaṇa abhāvaḥ avidyā katham tarhi tad nibandhanaḥ saṃsāraḥ 
[20,i^2]	muktau api tasya tulya tvāt tadvat eva na kiñcid prakāśeta atha ayathārtha grahaṇam avidyā na tarhi sarva śūnyatā tena idam pūrṇam puruṣeṇa sarvam iti śruteḥ ātmā eva idam sarvam iti ca sarvasmin ātma upadeśāt katham asataḥ sajjāyeta iti ca svayam śūnyatāyāḥ niṣedhāt bhāvaḥ hi yathāvat aprakāśamānaḥ adhyasta avidyamāna rūpaḥ prakāśate śūnye tu kva adhyāsaḥ kim prakāśa tām iti nirbīja tā eva syāt vijñānam ānandam iti rūpa upadeśāt ca na sarva abhāva mātram brahma api tu sarvasya ātmā iti 
[20,ii]	kecid tu kevalasya sukhasya adarśanāt duḥkha āvinā abhāvāt na asti avasthā duḥkha saṃsparśa viviktā iti manyante na hi kaścid jantuḥ sukhī ā iva upalabhyate duḥkhī ā iva vā duḥkhavataḥ eva tu sukham sukha tve avatiṣṭhate tāpavataḥ eva candana saṃsparśaḥ sukham tatra āha abhayam iti sarva bhaya vinirmuktā hi brahma avasthā na ca atra alpīyān api kleśaḥ asakṛt abhaya śruteḥ abhayam vai brahma ityādi tathā hi na svābhāvikam bhayam brahmaṇi ānanda rūpeṇa virodhāt na āgantukam hetumat dvitīya abhāvāt tat uktam dvitīyāt vai bhayam bhavati iti na ca duḥkha nivṛtti rūpam sukham yena duḥkhitasya eva sukham sukha tve avatiṣṭheta iti prapañcitam etat purastāt 
[21,i^1]	aparaḥ prakāraḥ iha kecid muktā abhimatānām api punarāvṛtti bhayam manyante iha hi vijñāna ātmānaḥ brahmaṇaḥ vibhaktāḥ syuḥ avibhaktā vā svatas brahmaṇā eva vā vibhajyeran bhoga artham krīḍā artham vibhūti khyāpana artham vā svabhāvāt vā avidyā nibandhanaḥ vā tad vibhāgaḥ vijñāna ātmānaḥ eva vā brahma śabda abhidheyāḥ na anyat brahma teṣām karma avidyā nibandhanaḥ saṃsāraḥ draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ paraspara yogya tā nibandhanaḥ vā tatra yogyatā nibandhana tve yogyatāyāḥ anapāyāt punarāvṛtti bhayam apracyutam atha kṛta kārya tvāt na punarāvṛttiḥ sakṛt śabda ādi upalabdhau na punar tad upalabdhiḥ syāt atha ananta vikārā prakṛtiḥ sarva ātmanā upalabdhau nivartate avikṛta rūpa antara upalabdhaye ca pravartate eva 
[21,i^2]	ānantyāt eva tarhi na sarva ātmanā upalabdhiḥ saṃbhavati iti guṇa puruṣa anyatā khyātimataḥ api punarāvṛttiḥ saṃbhāvyeta avidyā pūrva karma nibandhana tve api anādau saṃsāre ananta tvāt karmaṇā ām aniyata vipāka kāla tvāt ca pratisarga avasthāyāḥ iva mukti avasthāyāḥ api pratyudāvṛtti bhayam na vyāvartate avidyā nibandhana tve api tasyāḥ nirhetu tvāt niṣprayojana tvāt ca pravṛtteḥ tathā eva punar punar pravṛttiḥ kena vāryate tathā ca suṣupte brahma prāpteḥ pratyudāvṛttiḥ dṛśyate svatantre tu brahmaṇi vibhaktānām jīvānām deha indriya upabhoga hetau avibhaktānām vā vibhajya bhoga ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ na punar deha ādi bhedaḥ na sambhāvyate svatantraḥ hi krīḍayā svātantrya khyāpanena vā svabhāvena vā punar badhnīyāt laukikaḥ iva īśvaraḥ 
[21,i^3]	atha eṣa karma apekṣaḥ na karmasu asya svātantryam tathā api karmaṇām ānantyāt vipāka kāla niyama abhāvāt ca kalpa śata atikrame api prāpta vipāka kālebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ punar bandhaḥ sambhāvyate yatas na eka bhavikaḥ karma āśayaḥ na hi asya prāyaṇam eva abhivyañjakam api tu deśa kāla ādayaḥ api tathā hi ekasmin api dehe krameṇa karma phala bhogaḥ dṛśyate viruddha jāti bhoga nimittānām ca karmaṇām yugapad āvāpa gamana anupapatteḥ garbha mṛtyūnām ca akarmaṇām vimukti prasaṅgāt tatra ucyate abhayam iti parā hi iyam kṣema prāptiḥ śrūyate na asyām punar saṃsāra bhayam asti na tāvat karma nimittaḥ punar saṃsāraḥ vidyayā prāyaścittena iva akṛta bhogānām anantānām api karmaṇām prakṣayāt 
[21,i^4]	uktam hi jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā iti tathā kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi iti athavā vidyayā avidyā nivṛttau pravilīnaḥ eva kartṛ karma phala pravibhāgaḥ tasya kutas sambhavaḥ na api avidyā nimittaḥ tad pravṛtti hetoḥ abhāvāt anādiḥ hi avidyā anādi tvāt eva na hetum apekṣate prāgabhāve hi hetu vyāpāraḥ asati prāgabhāve kadā hetuḥ vyāpriyeta na hi sataḥ hetu kṛtyam asti vidyayā tu ucchinnā prāc asatī pravartamānā na akasmāt pravartitum arhati suṣupte tu vikṣepa mātram nivṛttam tad saṃskāraḥ agrahaṇam ca na eva nivṛtte anyathā na turīyāt bhidyeta vikṣepa mātra abhāvāt tu brahma prāpti abhidhānam tasmāt suṣṭhu uktam abhayam iti 
[22,i^1]	kena punar pramāṇena asya arthasya samadhigamaḥ na tāvat pratyakṣeṇa tasya etat viparīta bheda viṣaya tvāt na api anumānena tad pūrvaka tvāt na upamānena sādṛśya viṣaya tvāt tasya ca bheda adhiṣṭhāna tvāt arthāpattiḥ tu viparyaye na bhedam antareṇa kaścid vyavahāraḥ upapadyate yatas abhedaḥ api hi pramātṛ ādi vibhāgāt ṛte duravagamaḥ abhāvaḥ api na bhāva rūpa tattva avagamāya alam na api prapañca abhāva avagamāya pratyakṣa ādiṣu satsu tad asaṃbhavāt āgamaḥ api na tāvat āpta praṇetṛkaḥ atra kramate pramāṇa antara adhigata gocara tvāt na api svatantraḥ vidhi niṣedha rūpa tvāt tayoḥ ca sthite tattve asaṃbhavāt na api tad anapekṣam vyavasthita vastu viṣayam eva prāmāṇyam bhūta anuvāda tve pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt lokāt ca śabda sāmarthya adhigamaḥ tatra kārya para tayā eva kārya an vayiṣu artheṣu padāni prayujyante tathā arthavat tvāt na hi pravṛtti nivṛtti śūnyasya vacasaḥ kaścid arthaḥ api ca na bhūta anuvādāt vacasaḥ sambandha anugamaḥ api tu pravartakāt 
[22,i^2]	pravṛttyā hi anumāya artha pratyayam tatra śabdasya sāmarthya pratītiḥ tathā ca na pravṛtti sambandha rahiteṣu artheṣu śabdānām śaktiḥ gamyate tathā satya nava gata sāmarthyāḥ śabdāḥ bhūte arthe katham tad avagamayeyuḥ api ca pramāṇa antara avasitaḥ ced saḥ arthaḥ na śabdasya tatra prāmāṇyam atha anavasitaḥ natarām apadārtha tve vākya viṣaya tva asambhavāt padārthaḥ eva hi viśiṣṭa tayā vākya arthībhavati atyanta aparidṛṣṭaḥ tu padāt anavagamyamānaḥ padārtha saṃsarga ātmake vākya arthe na guṇa tvena pradhāna tvena vā anupraveśam arhati api ca pralīna nikhila avacchedam tattvam agocaraḥ eva pratipatteḥ sarvā hi pratipattiḥ evam na evam iti vyavacchedena pravartate anyathā na kaścid pratipannaḥ syāt sarva viśeṣa pratyasta maye tu katham pratipattiḥ syāt iti atra āha āmnāyataḥ prasiddhim ca kavayaḥ asya pracakṣate bheda prapañca vilaya dvāreṇa ca nirūpaṇām 
[23,i^1]	bhūta artha vādi tve api apauruṣeyasya na sa apekṣa tvam iti vakṣyate na ca kārya niṣṭhāni eva loke vacāṃsi tathā hi priya ākhyānāni diṣṭyā vardhase putraḥ te jātaḥ iti na pravṛttaye nivṛttaye vā dṛśyante ca sukha utpādana prayojanāni na ca sukhī bhavaḥ iti tatra pravṛttiḥ upadiśyate vastu sāmarthyāt eva tad siddheḥ upadeśasya anapekṣaṇāt atha matam asti tāvat tatra pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ vacasaḥ ca tatra tātparyam satyam utpattyā tātparyam na pratipattyā pratipattiḥ tu bhūta artha niṣṭhā eva na ca bhūta artha paryavasitasya eva śabdasya prayojanavat tve pravṛtti avadhiḥ vyāpāraḥ kalpayitum śakyate api ca upāye vā apravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ pravartyate ajñāta upāya tvāt vā upeye prāc apravṛttaḥ upāya prajñāpana dvāreṇa tatra iha na tāvat upāye putra janmani tasya niṣpanna tvāt na upeye sukhe tad artha vyāpāra antara abhāvāt 
[23,i^2]	tathā durjana vacanāni apriya ākhyānāni viṣāda prayojanāni na pravṛttim nivṛttim vā upadiśanti pūrveṇa eva nyāyena tathā rajju veṣṭitasya sarpa veṣṭitam ātmānam manyamānasya bhaya nivṛttaye tattva ākhyānam dṛśyate na tu tatra mā bhaiṣīḥ iti niyogaḥ tatra hi niyogaḥ bhavati yatra niyoga artham pratibudhya puruṣaḥ buddhi pūrvam niyoga sāmarthyāt icchayā vā punar pravartate nivartate vā iha tu tattva pratipatti mātrāt niyoga icchā anapekṣasya hetu abhāvāt eva tasya bhaya nivṛttiḥ na ca bhaya nivṛttau puruṣa artha tvāt svayaṃpravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ niyojyaḥ na api tad upāye tattva pratipattau rajjuḥ na sarpaḥ iti śabdāt eva tad utpatteḥ śabda artha pratipatti uttara kālasya ca vyāpārasya vidhi nibandhana tvāt tathā dūra deśa vṛttānta ākhyānāni pṛṣṭavatām kutūhalinām autsukya nivṛtti arthāni bhūta artha paryavasitāni na hānāya upādānāya vā 
[24,i^1]	yatra api bhūta artha pratipattau hānam upādānam vā saṃbhavati eṣa pratirodha kavān adhvā nidhimān eṣa bhū bhāgaḥ iti tatra api hāna upādānayoḥ śabdaḥ vyāpriyate bhūta artha upakṣayāt śabdāt bhūtam artham pratipadya tasya pramāṇa antara avagatām upakāra hetu tām apakāra hetu tām vā saṃsmṛtya icchayā pravartate dveṣeṇa nivartate vā nanu prayoktā buddhi pūrva kārī śrotuḥ pravṛtti artham nivṛtti artham vā vacanam prayuṅkte tathā ca pravṛtti nivṛtti paryavasitam eva idam hi tatra prayoktavyam na prayujyate na gantavyam anena adhvanā tathā gṛhāṇa itas nidhim iti na etat sāram bhūta artha paryavasitasya api vacasaḥ bhūta artha avagama mukhena pravṛtti nivṛtti aṅga bhāvaḥ yatas na vyāhanyate pratyakṣa ādīnām iva 
[24,i^2]	bhūta artha pramā pari samāpta vyāpṛtayaḥ pratyakṣa ādayaḥ mātrayā api agocarīkṛta pravṛtti nivṛttayaḥ na pravṛtti nivṛtti aṅga bhāvam jahati tathā śabdaḥ api iti na kiñcid praduṣyati prayoktṛ abhisaṃhite pravṛtti nivṛttī iti ced na prayoktṛ abhisaṃdhānāt śabda artha tvam api tu sāmarthyāt anyathā nidhi prāpti dvārikā nānāvidha puruṣa artha avāptiḥ api tasya abhisaṃhitā iti śabda arthaḥ syāt yadā ca pravṛttim nivṛttim vā abhisaṃdhāya kiñcid pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ jijñāsyate tadā abhisaṃhite api pravṛtti nivṛttī na pratyakṣa ādi prameye tadā abhisaṃhite api pravṛtti nivṛttī na śabda arthau itas ca etat evam yat kasyacid upādāna buddhiḥ anyasya upekṣā śabda artha tve hi sarveṣām upādāna buddhiḥ eva syāt 
[25,i]	na ca pravartaka vākya vyavahārāt eva sambandha avagamaḥ yena pravṛtti parata eva avagamyeta anyathā api darśanāt devadattaḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyām odanam pacati iti avyutpanna kāṣṭha śabda arthaḥ vyutpanna itara padārthaḥ vyutpanna vibhakti arthaḥ ca yat pacati arthe karaṇam paśyati tasya kāṣṭha prātipadikā artha tām pratipadyate tathā harṣa viṣāda āśvāsa prayojanebhyaḥ tattva ākhyānebhyaḥ harṣa ādi nimitteṣu bhavati vyutpattiḥ yathā eva hi pravṛtti viśeṣa darśanāt viśiṣṭa pravṛtti pratyayaḥ tad nimitta pratyayaḥ vā anumīyate hetu antara abhāvāt śabda anantaryāt śabdasya tatra sāmarthyam kalpyate tathā harṣa ādi upalabdheḥ harṣa ādi nimitta pratyaya anumānam śabda anantaryāt ca śabdasya tatra sāmarthya kalpanā pramāṇa antareṇa ca putra janmanaḥ harṣa nimittasya tasya avagata tvāt anyasya abhāvāt putraḥ te jātaḥ iti idam vākyam āptena tatra putra janmani prayuktam iti pratipadyate putra janma eva ca asmāt vākyāt anena pratītam iti avadhārayati tat evam prayoga pratyayābhyām asmin arthe vākyasya sāmarthyam pratipadyate 
[25,ii^1]	bhavatu vā loke sarva vacasām pravartaka tā tatas ca sambandha avagamaḥ tathā api idam vicāryam kim vidhāyaka pada vyatirekiṇām padānām sva artha mātra para tā āhosvit kārya artha saṃsarga para tā uta padārtha mātra saṃsarga para tā iti tatra sva artha mātra paryavasāne vākya artha pratyaya abhāvaḥ prayoga vaiyarthyam ca syāt tasmāt anya artha vyatiṣaṅga para tā tāvatā prayoga pratyayayoḥ upapattau na viśeṣa vyatiṣaṅge pramāṇam asti yaḥ hi viśeṣa vyatiṣaṅgam kalpayati kalpayati asau artha antara vyatiṣaṅgam tathā ca vinā api kāryeṇa padārthānām paraspara saṃsargāt viśiṣṭa bhūta artha pratyaya siddhiḥ avaśyam ca etat evam vijñeyam anyathā loke vivakṣā para tvāt padārtha anvayasya tad abhāvāt vede veda artha pratītiḥ na syāt 
[25,ii^2]	api ca sarveṣām kārya anvayitve parasparam padārthānām anabhisambandhaḥ tatra na viśiṣṭa padārtha viṣayaḥ niyogaḥ pratīyeta eka padārtha sādhyaḥ eva syāt atha na viniyoga pratyarthī niyogaḥ viśiṣṭa viṣaya tvāt pūrvaḥ tarhi viniyogaḥ paścāt niyogaḥ kim atas asti niyoga atirikta artha anvaye api padasya sāmarthyam niyoga anapekṣam ca paraspara anvitānām iyoga anvayāt na ca niyoga ākāṅkṣā nibandhanaḥ saṃsargaḥ iti pratipādayiṣyate anadhigatam api ramāṇa antareṇa anadhigata sambandham ca sva śabdena śakyam śabdena nirūpayitum viśeṣa pratiṣedha mukhena viśeṣa śabdānām nañaḥ ca yathāyatham arthaiḥ vidita saṅgati tvāt tathā ca ittham eva tat upadiśyate asthūlam iti sarva viśeṣa atigam etat kathayati bheda prapañca vilaya dvāreṇa iti etat ca vakṣyate iti 
[26,i]	anyaḥ arthaḥ yat uktam pratyasta mita sakala viśeṣam tattvam pratipatteḥ eva aviṣayaḥ iti tatra ucyate viśeṣa nivṛttyā eva tad śabdena buddhau nidhīyate suvarṇa tattva vat na hi suvarṇa tattvam piṇḍa rucaka ādi saṃsthāna bheda upaplava rahitam dṛśyate na ca te eva suvarṇa tattvam tad parityāge api bhāvāt saṃsthāna antare atha ca adṛṣṭa saṃsthāna bheda upaplava vivekam api buddhyā bheda apoha dvāreṇa svayam pratīyate parasmai ca pratipādyate saḥ eṣa pratipatti kramaḥ śrutyā eva darśitaḥ saḥ eṣa na iti na iti iti tathā anyaiḥ satyam ākṛti saṃhāre yat ante vyavatiṣṭhate tathā aparaiḥ adhyāra upa apavādābhyām niṣprapañcam prapañcyate iti 
[26,ii^1]	idam idānīm vicāryate kim kṛtsnaḥ āmnāyaḥ bheda prapañca vilaya mukhena brahma nirūpayati āhosvit kaścid asya eka deśaḥ tatra kecid āhuḥ sarvatra eva āmnāye kvacid kasyacid bhedasya pravilayaḥ gamyate yathā svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti śarīra ātma bhāvasya pravilayaḥ atra hi deha vyatirikta svarga upabhoga samarthaḥ adhikārī gamyate tena deha ātma bhāva pravilayaḥ tathā go dohanena paśu kāmasya praṇayet iti adhikṛta adhikārāt adhikāri bheda pravilayaḥ tathā vidhi niṣedha codanāsu api naisargikīṇām rāga ādi nibandhanānām pravṛttīnām pravilayaḥ 
[26,ii^2]	niṣedheṣu sākṣāt vidhiṣu pravṛtti antar niyogena loke api anabhipretāt pathaḥ sākṣāt vā nivāraṇam pathi antara upadeśena vā evam ca rāga ādi nibandhana naisargika pravṛtti bheda vilaya dvāreṇa dṛṣṭena eva karma vidhayaḥ ātma jñāna adhikāra upayoginaḥ tathā hi śāntasya dāntasya samāhitasya ca ātmani darśanam upadiśyate śakyam ca na hi viṣayaiḥ ākṛṣyamāṇaḥ tad upāya pravṛtti kṛta cetāḥ śaknoti ātmani samādhātum naisargikībhyaḥ tu pravṛttibhyaḥ uparataḥ niyata mānasaḥ ātma darśanena adhikriyate sāmarthyāt 
[27,i_27,ii]	anye manyante anavāpta kāmaḥ kāma upahata manāḥ na parama advaita darśana yogyaḥ karmabhiḥ tu kṛta kāma nibarhaṇaḥ sahasra saṃvatsara paryantaiḥ prājāpatyāt padāt parama advaitam ātmānam pratipadyate iti ubhayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ anayoḥ kṛtsnaḥ āmnāya ātma jñāna eka paryavasāyī anyeṣām darśanam pṛthakkāryāḥ eva santaḥ karma vidhayaḥ ātma jñāna adhikāram avatārayanti puruṣam anapākṛta ṛṇa trayasya tatra anadhikārāt ṛṇāni trīṇi apākṛtya manaḥ mokṣe niveśayet iti 
[27,iii_28,iii]	anye tu saṃyoga pṛthaktvena sarva karmaṇām eva ātma jñāna adhikāra anupraveśam āhuḥ vividiṣanti yajñena iti śruteḥ yena kenacana yajeta api darvīhomena anupahata manāḥ eva bhavati iti ca anye tu puruṣa saṃskāra tayā ātma jñāna adhikāra saṃsparśam karmaṇām varṇayanti mahāyajñaiḥ ca yajñaiḥ ca brāhmī iyam kriyate tanuḥ yasya ete catvāriṃśat saṃskārāḥ aṣṭau ātma guṇāḥ iti ca anye tu etat eva viparītam varṇayanti ātma jñānam eva kartṛ saṃskāra tayā karma adhikāra anupraveśī iti anye tu paraspara virodhinoḥ karma ātma jñānayoḥ dvaitādvaita viṣaya tvena asaṃbandhaḥ eva iti manyante 
[28,iv^1]	tatra na tāvat prathamaḥ kalpaḥ na hi karma ādi vidhayaḥ sva vākya samadhigata svarga ādi kāryāḥ kārya antaram apekṣante na api ātma jñāna vidhiḥ yathā udita brahmacarya ādi sādhana nirākāṅkṣaḥ karma vidhīn apekṣate tatra kutas eka adhikāra tvam yadi manyeta anavagata kāryāḥ eva karma ādi vidhayaḥ svarga ādīnām guṇa tvena saṃbandhāt iti svarga kāma adhikaraṇam asmai vyācakṣīta api ca sarva vidhi niṣedhānām nāma rūpa pravilaya kārya apavargi tve jantūnām abhyudaya vinipātāḥ akarma nimittāḥ ākasmikāḥ syuḥ tathā apavargaḥ api syāt iti vaiyarthyam śāstrasya api atha svarga ādi kārya dvāreṇa karma vidhīnām jñāna adhikāra anupraveśitā mārga grāma gamana upadeśānām iva abhimata nagara gamana upadeśa anupraveśi tvam 
[28,iv^2]	tat asat yuktam mārga grāma prāpteḥ anabhimata deśa prāpti upadeśa anupraveśi tvam na hi mārga grāma upadeśeṣu puruṣa artha prāptiḥ atas sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt yatra puruṣa artha prāptiḥ tam anupraviśanti na tu evam karma vidhiṣu puruṣa arthasya alābhaḥ svarga ādīnām puruṣeṇa arthyamāna tvāt tatra ca nairākāṅkṣye katham anya anupraveśaḥ atha matam yadā upacchandya nīyate uttarottara grāma guṇa upadarśanena abhipretam deśam tadā pūrva grāma upadeśāḥ prāpta abhimata kāryāḥ upadeśa antara anupraveśinaḥ ca iti yuktam tatra api pramāṇa antareṇa vaktuḥ abhiprāya adhigamāt 
[28,iv^3]	pramāṇa antareṇa hi tatra idam adhigatam etad deśa prāpta avidamasya samīhitam vaktuḥ saṃpadyate tasmāt idam asya vivakṣitam iti na tu śabda vṛtti mātra anusāreṇa itas ca etat evam yat pratigrāmam vaktuḥ śrotuḥ ca satyām artha prāptau pramāṇa antareṇa anadhigate para deśa prāpti abhiprāye pūrva upadeśān pūrva arthān eva pārśva sthāḥ pratipattāraḥ pratipadyante para deśa upadeśam ca sva artha niṣṭham yadi api vastu sthityā pūrva upadeśa arthāḥ para upakāriṇaḥ tathā api na śabdasya tātparyam dravya arjana ādi vidheḥ iva kratu vidhi artha upakāre api śabda vṛtta anusāreṇa ca iha tātparyam pramāṇa antara abhāvāt iti 
[28,iv^4]	api ca adhva grāma upadeśānām tad paratva adhyavasāyena eva tatra gamanam artha prāptiḥ ca tatra para deśa prāpti para tāyām tu na niyogataḥ tatra gamanam mārga antareṇa api tad prāpteḥ vivakṣita tvāt gacchet na ca niyogataḥ artha prāptiḥ anya pareṣu prayojana śruteḥ api artha vāda tvāt tat iha yadi vidhi niṣedhāḥ kārya antara parāḥ na svarga ādi kāryāḥ na khalu svarga ādi kāryam prayāja ādi kārya tulyam yena kārya antaram anupatet katham ca dṛṣṭena eva ātma jñāna adhikāra upakāriṇaḥ iti vaktavyam yadi tāvat rāga ādi ākṣipta dṛṣṭa artha pravṛtti nirodhena bhavatu pratiṣedhānām evaṃbhāvaḥ karma vidhayaḥ tu katham nirundhanti iti vācyam 
[28,iv^5]	na hi te parisaṃkhyāyakāḥ na ca niyāmakāḥ atyantam aprāpta artha tvāt prāpta arthaḥ hi vidhiḥ anya nivṛtti phalaḥ vijñāyate na ca tulya kārya tvena virodhena nivṛttiḥ aniyata kāla phalāḥ hi naiyogikyaḥ pravṛttayaḥ adṛṣṭa arthāḥ dṛṣṭa arthāḥ tu rāga ādi ākṣiptāḥ svābhāvikyaḥ na ca sa aṅgrahaṇyāḥ sevāyāḥ ca grāma upāya tve kaścid virodhaḥ etāvati pramāṇa tvāt śāstrasya tatra yugapad krameṇa vā phala bhūma arthinaḥ sevāsa aṅgrahaṇyau anutiṣṭhataḥ kaḥ virodhaḥ api ca sakala dṛṣṭa artha pravṛtti nirodhe niyoga niṣṭhāḥ api pravṛttayaḥ nirudhyeran anārjita dhanasya sādhana vikalasya tāsām asambhavāt 
[28,iv^6]	api ca tulye kāma upāya tve dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa artha pravṛttyoḥ na na viśeṣaḥ rāga ādi ākṣipta tve tathā hi svarga kāmaḥ iti rāga ādi ākṣipta pravṛtti anuvādena viśeṣa vidhānam tathā ca prapañca abhiniveśe tulye kena viśeṣeṇa eka ātma anuguṇyam bhajate tad virodhinī aparā kāma ākṣepaḥ hi aviśiṣṭaḥ manasaḥ atha kāma upāya tvam eva na manyeta varṇitam āka smika tvam uktaḥ ca nyāyaḥ pratyuddhriyeta tulya kārya nibandhana tvāt ca virodha ādyāḥ nirodha āśaṅkā sā dūratas nirasta avakāśā syāt atha kāma prāptyā karma vidhayaḥ kāmān pravilāpayantaḥ jñāna adhikāra anuguṇāḥ yathā uktam yadā sarve pramucyate kāmāḥ ye asya hṛdi śritāḥ 
[28,iv^7]	atha martyaḥ amṛtaḥ bhavati atra brahma samaśnute iti tat api asat yatas na kāma prāptyā kāma pravilayaḥ api tu doṣa paribhāvanā abhuvā prasaṅkhyānena kalayā api ced kāmaiḥ manaḥ saṃspṛśyate hriyate eva hāribhiḥ uktam hi na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati bhoga abhyāsam anu vivardhante rāgāḥ kauśalāni ca indriyāṇām iti ca anupāya tvāt api tāvat ayam kāmebhyaḥ vinivarteta nikhila kleśa upaśama rūpam ca ātma jñānam saṃśrayeta karma vidhi nidarśita vividha upāyaḥ tu tān eva prakṛta hāriṇaḥ bhogān abhiniviśeta tad pravilaya rūpāca ātma jñānāt udvijeta 
[28,iv^8_30,i]	śrutaḥ api hi ātmani ānandaḥ ananubhūtaḥ na anubhūta viṣaya nibandhana ānanda abhilāṣam mandīkartum api utsahate prāk eva ucchettum tasmāt prasaṃkhyānam eva ekaḥ kāma nibarhaṇa upāyaḥ karma vidhayaḥ tu viparyaya hetavaḥ yat api sarvatra eva āmnāye kvacid kasyacid bhedasya vilayaḥ yathā svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti śarīra ātma tva pravilayaḥ iti tat api asat anidaṃpara tvāt na hi idam vacanam deha vyatirikta ātma tattva avabodha param atha anya parāt api arthāt evam avasīyate iti tat api hastini dṛṣṭe tad padena tasya anumānam iva sākṣāt hi asthūlam iti upakramya deha indriya vilayaḥ darśitaḥ arthāt ca kāma ādi grantheḥ kāṭhinyam vaidikam syāt iti dvitīyaḥ api kalpaḥ varṇitāt eva kāmānām kāma nibarhaṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt sva kārya nirākāṅkṣāṇām ca anya anupraveśe pramāṇa bhāvāt asamañjasaḥ eka adhikāra tve tu samuccayaḥ sarva karmaṇām syāt sa ca aśakyaḥ iti 
[31,i^1]	ye api viparyayeṇa jñāna karmaṇoḥ eka adhikāra tvam āhuḥ taiḥ api jñānasya karma sambandhe pramāṇam vaktavyam na tāvat brīhīn prokṣati iti yathā tatra hi prakaraṇāt prakṛta karma apūrva lakṣaṇa aparaḥ brīhi śabdaḥ sva svarūpaḥ ānarthakyāt prakṛta apūrva sambandham bodhayati na api yathā yasya parṇa mayī juhūḥ bhavati iti tatra hi juhvādi avyabhicarita karma sambandham asati api prakaraṇe karma upasthāpayati tatra vākyena eva sambandhaḥ ātma jñānam tu na prakaraṇe śrutam na api ātma avyabhicarita karma sambandhaḥ tena asya karma sambandhaḥ durvacaḥ tathā ca ajñāte pārārthye yā nāma phala śrutiḥ na sārtha vādinī bhavati iti pṛthak adhikāra tvam 
[31,i^2]	atha matam vartamāna apadeśāt na sa punar āvartate iti kāma upabandha abhāvāt phalam vipariṇamayya kalpayitavyam tat ca tadākāṅkṣāyām satyām na tu dṛṣṭe sati tad ākāṅkṣā asti ca ātma jñāna vidheḥ dṛṣṭa phalam deha antara upabhogya phaleṣu karmasu pravṛttiḥ tasmāt svādhyāya adhyayana vidhi vat ātma jñāna vidhiḥ svādhyāya adhyayana vidhiḥ hi dṛṣṭa karma avabodha nirākāṅkṣaḥ na artha vādataḥ phalam prārthayate tathā ātma jñāna vidhiḥ api iti na adhikāra antaram tat api asat yatas ayam anyaḥ eva aupaniṣadaḥ puruṣaḥ vedānteṣu jijñāsyate na ca tat jñānam karma pravṛtti hetuḥ na hi tasya kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tve 
[31,i^3]	evam hi āha na tat aśnāti kiñcana anaśnan anyaḥ abhicākaśīti iti yaḥ tu karmaṇām kartā bhoktā ca saḥ eva sarva pratyakṣa siddhaḥ na śabda prameyaḥ nanu jīva paramātmanoḥ eka tvam eva evam hi āha anena jīvena ātmanā iti satyam tasya eva tu jīvasya evam avidyā anubandham pratyakṣa avaseyam rūpam tat ca karma pravṛtti hetuḥ na ca tat śabdam apekṣate yat tu svayaṃprakāśam sarva vibhāga śūnyam tat śabdāt jñātum iṣyate tat ca karma pravṛtti virodhi tat jñānasya katham karma pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭam prayojanam syāt tathā hi brahma ānandam ekam advayam ātmānam vijānataḥ kim artham katham vā pravṛttiḥ syāt āpta kāma tvāt sādhana ādi upāya abhāvāt ca 
[31,i^4]	syāt etat aupaniṣada puruṣa jñānam eva karma aṅga tvena coditam yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaniṣadā tat eva vīryavattaram bhavati iti tathā yaḥ vai etat akṣaram gārgya viditvā asmin loke juhoti iti upakramya yāga ādi phalasya antavat tā darśanena brahma vidyāyāḥ tādarthyam darśitam tam vidyā karmaṇī samanvārabhete iti ca vidyā karmaṇoḥ sāhityam darśitam pūrvam tāvat prakṛta udgītha viṣayam om iti etat akṣara mudgītham iti upakramāt pareṇa api karma nindayā akṣara jñāna stutiḥ vidyā karmaṇoḥ ca samanvārambhaḥ bhedena vidyāvantam vidyā anvārabhate karmavantam karma iti tasmāt evam api na karma jñānayoḥ eka adhikāra tvam iti 
[32,i^1]	ye api virodhāt asambandhaḥ eva karma jñānayoḥ dvaita viṣayam karma advaita viṣayam jñānam iti manyante teṣām anutpādaḥ eva advaita jñānasya prasajyate pramāṇa ādi vibhāgā dvaita pratipattyoḥ virodhāt atha upāya upeyayoḥ ayaugapadyāt avirodhaḥ pralīyate eva advaita pratipattau sarvaḥ vibhāgaḥ na ca virodhaḥ anupāya tvam vā upāyasya pūrva kāla tvāt tadā ca tasya apralīna tvāt bhedaḥ eva ca abheda pratipattau upāyaḥ na tarhi karmabhiḥ api virodhaḥ upāya tvāt eva syāt etat asādhya tvāt brahmaṇaḥ na karmaṇām upayogaḥ vidyate śrūyate ca na asti akṛtaḥ kṛtena iti 
[32,i^2]	na ca jñāna utpattau upayogaḥ jñānasya pramāṇa adhīna tvāt na ca jñāna saha kārīṇi karmāṇi jñānasya sādhya antara abhāvāt na tasya mokṣaḥ sādhyaḥ anitya tva prasaṅgāt atha bandha hetu vicchedaḥ sādhyaḥ iti tasmin vicchinne tad abhāvāt mucyate kaḥ punar bandha hetuḥ anādya vidyā na tarhi pṛthak ta d vicchedaḥ sādhyaḥ yatas vidyā udayaḥ eva avidyā vyāvṛttiḥ syāt etat bhavatu agrahaṇa lakṣaṇa avidyā vyāvṛttiḥ vidyā utpādaḥ yatas bhāvaḥ eva abhāva vyāvṛttiḥ na ca vidyā utpādaḥ eva viparyāsa jñāna vyāvṛttiḥ na khalu bhāva antaram bhāva antara vyāvṛttiḥ na ca paraspara abhāva ātmānaḥ bhāvāḥ abhāva tva prasaṅgāt 
[32,i^3]	yadi manyeta tattva agrahaṇa nimittaḥ viparyāsaḥ nimitta nivṛttau svayam eva nivartiṣyate tat ca na na khalva grahaṇam abhāvaḥ kasyacid nimittam mūrcchā ādiṣu prasaṅgāt kim tarhi nimittam anādiḥ aprayojanā ca avidyā iti uktam tatra ca hetu anuyogaḥ niravakāśaḥ viparyāsa tad saṃskārayoḥ ca paraspara hetu phala bhāvena vyavasthānāt na doṣaḥ atas viparyaya jñānasya nivṛttiḥ vidyayā sādhyeti tatra jñānasya sahakāri apekṣā syāt etat ca vārtam na khalu śuktikā ādiṣu viparyāsa purassaram samupajāta samyak jñānāḥ tad nivṛttaye pṛthak prayatante sahakāri vā anyat apekṣante 
[32,i^4]	yatas virodhi bhāva antara utpādaḥ eva pūrva pradhvaṃsaḥ na śūnyam anyathā na pradhvaṃsaḥ hetumān syāt virodhinī ca vidyā viparyaya jñānasya tad utpattau viparyāsaḥ naṣṭaḥ eva bhavati atha ucyeta karmāṇi bandha hetavaḥ tad kṣayaḥ jñānāt sahakāri savyapekṣāt iti tat ca pramṛṣṭa aśeṣa viśeṣa viśuddha jñāna udaye kutas sambhavaḥ tathā ca viparyāsa saṃśayābhyām tulya vat prasaṃkhyātāni karmāṇi bhidyante hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare iti atha vijñāna vaimalyāya anya apekṣā sā api mudhā saṃśaya viparyāsayoḥ jñāna malayoḥ pramāṇa uttha vijñāne asaṃbhavāt 
[32,i^5]	atha matam śābda jñānāt anyat api pratyakṣam jñānam iṣyate vigalita vibhāga udgrāham sarva vikalpa atītam tasya hi brahma gocaraḥ na śābdasya vibhakta padārtha saṃsarga udgrāhiṇaḥ tad utpattau karma upāsana ādi apekṣā iti kaḥ punar asya viśeṣaḥ yena tat arthyate spaṣṭa ābha tvam na tasya upayogaḥ jñānam hi jñeya abhivyāptaye śābda jñāne ca utpannaḥ āptam eva jñeyam pramiteḥ pratyakṣa paratvāt tatra ca nairākāṅkṣyāt tad arthyate iti ced etat adhigate prameye kim anyat ākāṅkṣyeta pramāṇa antaram iti ced na prameya siddhi artha tvāt tad ākāṅkṣāyāḥ punar siddhi artham iti ced na pūrvasmāt api asakṛt tad siddheḥ 
[32,i^6]	siddhasya ca siddhi apekṣāyām na hetuḥ asti upāya antara sadbhāvaḥ ced upāya antaram tarhi apekṣeta prameye tu naiḥ ākāṅkṣyam eva prīti viśeṣaḥ ced sa pūrva pramāṇa jāt api darśanāt sidhyati na tad siddhi artham pramāṇa antaram pratyakṣa dṛṣṭam api itaraiḥ tad sambhavāt jijñāsyeta viśeṣa abhāvāt niścāyaka tvam itareṣām api pramāṇa bhāvāt hāna ādi yogya viṣayam pratyakṣam sannikṛṣṭa artha tvāt na itarāṇi iti ced sannikarṣa hetuḥ tarhi apekṣya tām na pramāṇam siddha tvāt pramāyāḥ prakṛte ca prameye na eṣa viśeṣaḥ asti sāmānya viṣayāḥ śabda ādayaḥ viśeṣa viṣayam pratyakṣam iti ced anadhigataḥ eva tarhi śabdena pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ 
[32,i^7]	bāḍham uktam etat na śābdasya jñānasya viṣayaḥ brahma iti yadi tarhi na śabdena adhigatam brahma katham tasmin upāsanā pravartatām na ca anyasmin upāsyamāne anyat sākṣāt bhavati kasya ca rūpasya sākṣātkaraṇāya yajña ādi vidhānam śabda upadarśita niratiśaya ānanda apahata pāpma ādi rūpa brahma svabhāvasya ātmanaḥ sākṣātkaraṇāya yajña ādi vidhiḥ upapadyate avidita puruṣa artha rūpe tad viparīta rūpe nirvicikitsāt pramāṇāt prakaṭa tām prāpte na aparam apekṣyam asti nanu avagate api tat tvam asi iti śabdāt brahma ātma bhāve prāk iva sāṃsārika dharma darśāt tad nivṛttaye bhavati anya apekṣā na etat sāram 
[32,i^8]	katham khalu avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ vidita ātma yāthātathyaḥ mithyā darśana nimittaiḥ dharmaiḥ yujyate śrūyate ca brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati iti na ca brahmaṇi apahata pāpmani teṣām avakāśaḥ tathā ātmānam ced vijānīyāt ayam asmi iti pūruṣaḥ kim icchan kasya kāmāya śarīram anusañjvaret tathā aśarīram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti mithyā abhimāna nimittaḥ śarīra sambandhaḥ tasmin yāthātathya darśanāt nivṛtte aśarīra tvam tatra priya apriyayoḥ asambandhaḥ ākhyāyate tasmāt na avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ prāk iva sāṃsārika dharma bhāj yaḥ tu tathā na asau avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ iti 
[35,i^1]	atra ucyate niścite api pramāṇāt tattve sarvatra mithyā avabhāsāḥ nivartante hetu viśeṣāt anuvartante api yathā dvi candra diś viparyāsa ādayaḥ āpta vacana viniścita diś candra tattvānām tathā nirvicikitsā dāmnāyāt avagata ātma tattvasya anādi mithyā darśana abhyāsa upacita bala vat saṃskāra sāmarthyāt mithyā avabhāsa anuvṛttiḥ tad nivṛttaye asti anyat apekṣyam tat ca tattva darśana abhyāsaḥ loka siddhaḥ yajña ādayaḥ ca śabda pramāṇakāḥ abhyāsaḥ hi saṃskāram draḍhayan pūrva saṃskāram pratibadhya sva kāryam santanoti yajña ādayaḥ ca kena api adṛṣṭena prakāreṇa 
[35,i^2]	śreyaḥ paripanthi kaluṣa nibarhaṇa dvāreṇa iti anye nityānām karmaṇām durita kṣaya artha tvāt syāt etat anuvartantām mithyā avabhāsāḥ pramāṇāt tu niścayaḥ yathātattvam yathā niścayam ca vyavahāraḥ tasmānāvagata ātma tattvasya kācana śubha aśubhā vā pravṛttiḥ upapadyate ucyate jāte api tattva darśane anāhite ca paṭau saṃskāre draḍhiyasi ca mithyā darśana je saṃskāre niścayāḥ api mithyā arthāḥ bhavanti yathā diś mūḍhasya ananusaṃhita āpta vacasaḥ prāk iva pravṛtti darśanāt tathā pramita rajju bhāvāyāḥ api rajjvāḥ pramāṇa an anusandhāne sarpa bhrāntyā bhaya darśanam 
[35,i^3]	tasmāt jāte api pramāṇāt tattva darśane anādi mithyā darśana abhyāsa pariniṣpannasya draḍhīyasaḥ saṃskārasya abhibhavāya ucchedāya vā tattva darśana abhyāsam manyante tathā ca mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti ucyate śama dama brahmacarya yajña ādi sādhana vidhānam ca anyathā kaḥ tad upadeśa arthaḥ syāt etat brahmacarya ādi sādhana karaṇāt eva āmnāyāt tattva vijñānam tat asat śabda mātrāt pratipatteḥ utpatteḥ na hi prāk sādhana viśeṣebhyaḥ tattva pratipatti paraḥ āmnāyaḥ avācakaḥ na api aniścāyakaḥ aśeṣa āśaṅkā nirmokṣāt anyathā tad upadiṣṭeṣu sādhaneṣu api durlabhā pratipattiḥ 
[35,i^4]	api ca anyathā niścaye api raṅga gatāḥ bharata ādayaḥ mithyā avabhāsena śoka bhaya ādi hetavaḥ niścite api guḍasya mādhurye tatra mithyā tikta avabhāsaḥ avitathaḥ iva duḥkhayati avitathasya iva tasya api dhūtkṛtya tyāgāt tasmāt tad nivṛttaye viniścita brahma ātma bhāvena api sādhanāni apekṣyāṇi yathā eva pramāṇāt tattva abhivyaktau na mukteḥ kārya tā tathā abhivyakti viśeṣe api sādhanebhyaḥ śrutayaḥ tu abhyāsa pariniṣpatti avasthā viṣayāḥ śabda sādhana jñāna apekṣāḥ vā bhavantu tad hetu tvāt uttarasya iti alam ati vistareṇa 
[36,i]	yat api pṛthakkāryāḥ eva karma vidhayaḥ jñāna adhikāram avatārayanti apākṛta ṛṇa trayasya tatra adhikārāt tat api na niyogataḥ āśrama vikalpasya smaraṇāt tassya āśrama vikalpam eke yam icchet tamavaset iti yadi vā itarathāḥ brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet iti śravaṇāt etat ha sma vai tat pūrve vidvāṃsaḥ agnihotram na juhavāñcakrire tathā kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥ tathā kimarthāḥ vayam adhyeṣyāmahe kimarthāḥ vayam yakṣyāmahe iti karma tyāga darśanāt pratipannaga arhasthyasya ātma vidyayā eva kṛtakṛtya tām manvānasya ṛṇa apākaraṇam pratyanādṛtasya vihita akaraṇa nimittasya pāpmanaḥ vidyā udaya pratibandhṛ tvam darśayati ṛṇāni trīṇi apākṛtya iti 
[36,ii]	idam tu yuktam kārya antara nirākāṅkṣāṇām api karmaṇām saṃyoga pṛthaktvāt tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣanti yajñena iti vidyā aṅga bhāvaḥ saḥ api utpatti artha tayā na prayāja ādi vat kāya upayogena vidyāyāḥ kārya antara abhāvāt saṃskāra pakṣaḥ vā smṛteḥ saṃskṛtasya hi vidyā utpatteḥ tat uktam vihita tvāt ca āśrama karmā api iti 
[36,iii]	nanu dṛṣṭa utpāyaḥ eva vidyā utpādaḥ tatra dṛṣṭā eva iti kartavya tāpekṣya tām śama dama ādi sādhana viśeṣaḥ citta vikṣepasya vihantrī sama hita cittasya ābhasataḥ jñāna prasāda utpatteḥ na tu yajña ādayaḥ taiḥ vinā api abhyāsena tad sambhavāt satyam tathā ca ūrdhvaretasām ca āśramiṇām vinā api taiḥ viśuddha vidyā udayaḥ iṣyate kim tu kāla kṛtaḥ viśeṣaḥ sādhana viśeṣāt hi sā kṣipram kṣiprataram ca vyajyate tad abhāve cireṇa ciratareṇa ca tat uktam sarva apekṣā ca yajña ādi śruteḥ aśva vat eṣaḥ arthaḥ yajñena dānena iti śravaṇāt karmāṇi apekṣyante vidyāyām abhyāsa labhyāyām api yathā antareṇa api aśvam grāma prāptau siddyantyām śaighryāya akleśāya vā aśvaḥ apekṣyate 
[37,i^1]	nanu vidyā rūpam brahmā eva na vidyā brahmaṇaḥ anyā tat ca nityam akāryam tatra katham kiñcid apekṣyeta ucyate yathā upadhāna tirohita rūpa sphaṭika maṇiḥ upadha avakarṣaṇam svarūpa abhivyaktaye apekṣate tathā iha api draṣṭavyam na hi sphaṭika maṇeḥ pūrva rūpam vinaṣṭam upadhāna sannidheḥ tad apagame vā anyat utpannam na hi akasmāt aneka visabhā ga kṣaṇa vyavahitasya pūrva sabhā ga kṣaṇasya utpattiḥ sambhavati na hi agni vigame aṅgārebhyaḥ punar kāṣṭha santati pravṛttiḥ tasmāt yathā eva akāryam sphaṭika rūpam upadhāna avakarṣaṇam apekṣate tathā ātma rūpam api syat etat jñānam tatra sa apekṣam tat ca sphaṭikāt bhinnam kāryam 
[37,i^2_37,ii]	puruṣa prayatnaḥ hi tatra jñāna arthaḥ kim punar jñānam sva rūpeṇa eva arthitam āhosvit artha svabhāva siddhaye na tāvat svarūpeṇa arthena vyavahārat na vijñāna mātra nibandhanaḥ vyavahāraḥ mithyājñānena api prasaṅgāt atha artha svabhāya jñānam arthyeta tad arthaḥ vyāpāraḥ tena arthitaḥ bhavati na ca jñānāt arthe kaścid vikāraḥ tayoḥ asaṃbandhāt yogya deśa tāyāḥ sarvatra bhāvāt sarva pratipattṛṇām ca vidita tva prasaṅgāt dhvasta anāgateṣu ca tad asaṃbhavāt tasmāt yathā atirohitam api tirohitam iva abhivyajyate iva prayatna apekṣam tathā ātma tattvam api atirohitam tirohitam iva prayatnāt abhivyajyate iva iti puṣkalam saṃhṛta akhila bhedaḥ atas sāmānya ātmā sa varṇitaḥ hema iva pārihārya ādi bheda saṃhāra sūcitam 
[37,iii]	yatas ca viśeṣa pratyasta mukhena tad nirūpaṇam atas anyaiḥ brahma vidyā abhiyuktaiḥ sāmānya rūpam brahma nirūpitam saḥ eva mahān ajaḥ ātmā sattā lakṣaṇaḥ tathā sattā eva sarva bheda yoniḥ prakṛtiḥ parāḥ iti yathā suvarṇa tattvam kaṭaka aṅgulīya ādi viśeṣa upasaṃhāreṇa nirūpyamāṇam tat sāmānyam iti ye vā nirviśeṣam na sāmānyam bhavet śaśa viṣāṇa vat iti abhāvam āhuḥ tān pratyucyate saṃhṛta akhila bhedaḥ iti yadi tāvat asāmānya tvam sādhyate siddha sādhanam viśeṣāṇām abhāve keṣām tad sāmanyam sāmanyam tu uktam brahma vādibhiḥ viśeṣa pratyasta mukhena nirūpaṇāt upacārataḥ atha abhāvaḥ eva sādhyaḥ viśeṣaiḥ eva asya nirviśeṣaiḥ vyabhicāraḥ iti 
[39,i_39,ii]	nanu pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ vyāvṛttānām bhāva svabhāvānām avagamāt na ekasmin advaye śabdaḥ pramāṇam pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt grāva plavana ādi arthavacaḥ vat ucyate āhuḥ vidhātṛ pratyakṣam na niṣeddhṛ vipaścitaḥ na ekatve āgamaḥ tena pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate nanu pramāṇa antara paratantrāṇām puruṣa vacasām tad virodha ādi uktam apramāṇa tvam svatantrasya tvāmnāyasya anapekṣita pramāṇa antara pravṛtteḥ tad virodhe api kasmāt apramāṇa tvam āmnāya virodhāt eva tu pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇa tāyāḥ kim iti na cyavante tulye anapekṣa tve na viśeṣa hetuḥ asti tatra vṛthā pramāṇa antara virodha parihāra pariśramaḥ iti 
[39,iii^1]	tatra kecid āhuḥ pratyakṣa ādi virodhe āmnāyasya daurbalyam sa apekṣa tvat tathā hi svarūpa siddhi artham eva tāvat pratyakṣa ādīni āmnāyaḥ apekṣate tathā ca teṣām prāmāṇyam anumantavyam tad apabādhane svarūpasya eva tāvat asiddheḥ na tu evam āmnāye pratyakṣa ādīnām kācid apekṣā dṛṣṭa vyabhicāra tvāt ca śabdasya pratyakṣasya ca adṛṣṭa vyabhicārāt api ca sa avakāśa anavakāśayoḥ anavakāśam balavat anavakāśāḥ ca pratyakṣa ādayaḥ sa avakāśaḥ tu śabdaḥ gauṇena arthena tathā hi śakyam eka tvam abheda śrutīnām upacaritam avakāśaḥ varṇayitum avivakṣita arthānām vā vedāntānām japa upayogaḥ avakāśaḥ upaniṣadaḥ vedāntāḥ iti varṇitam 
[39,iii^2]	kim ca vyākula tvāt āmnāyasya avyākula tvāt pratyakṣa ādīnām karma vidhayaḥ hi bheda āśrayāḥ abheda āśrayāḥ ca vedāntāḥ paraspara parāhatā asati api pramāṇa antara virodhe durlabha prāmāṇyāḥ kim punar avyāhata pratiṣṭhita prāmāṇya ādi virodhe tasmāt idam avirodhāya prayatyate iti mukhya tvāt ca mukhyāḥ hi pratyakṣa ādayaḥ jātasya jantoḥ apara kāle āmnāyaḥ sa taiḥ pratiṣṭhita arthaiḥ apahṛta viṣayaḥ kalpanīya arthaḥ bādhyate tad anusāreṇa vā artha kalpanām arhati arthataḥ api ca mukhya tā pratyakṣa ādīnām pada padārtha vibhāga adhīnaḥ āmnāya artha paricchedaḥ sa ca pratyakṣa ādiṣu āpatate atas avirodhāya prayatyate iti 
[40,i_40,ii^1]	anye manyante tulya bala tve api pratyakṣa ādīnām āmnāyasya ca vastuni vikalpa anupapatteḥ virodhe saṃśayaḥ syāt tena avirodhaḥ upapādyate iti anyat darśanam āmnāyaḥ eva balavān tad virodhe paurvāparye pūrva daurbalyam prakṛti vat pūrva ābādhena na utpattiḥ uttarasya hi sidhyati iti tathā hi sarvasya nisarga jaḥ pratyakṣa ādi nibandhanaḥ kila vibhakta vastu paricchedaḥ tad apekṣaḥ tu tad pūrvakaḥ anisarga jaḥ kasyacid eva agantuḥ advaita avagamaḥ sa pūrvam anupamṛdya udetum aśaknuvan tad apabādha ātmā udīyate itas ca saṃbhavat vicitra vibhrama hetu tvāt pratyakṣa ādīnām vigalita nikhila doṣa āśaṅka tvāt ca āmnāyasya puruṣa āśrayāṇām hi doṣāṇām śabde puruṣa abhāve asaṃbhavāt 
[40,ii^2]	śakyaḥ hi āmnāyāt eva anādiḥ avidyā saṃskāraḥ vibhrama hetuḥ pratyakṣa ādiṣu saṃbhāvayitum niścetum ca deha ātmā abhimānaḥ iva na tu evam apauruṣeye śabde kācid doṣa āśaṅkā satyām vā pramāṇam eva na syāt pratyakṣa ādīnām tu vyāvahārikam prāmāṇyam avidyā saṃskārasya sthemnā vyavahāra viparyaya abhāvāt yatra ca vyavahāra viparyayaḥ na tatra prāmāṇyam śabde tu saṃbhāvita doṣe na tattva āvedanena prāmāṇyam na vyavahāra aviparyayeṇa adṛṣṭa artha tvāt doṣebhyaḥ vyavahāra visaṃvādi jñāna darśanāt ca pratyakṣa ādīnām tu vyavahāre saṃvādāt na śakyate vyavahāra visaṃvādi jñāna hetuḥ doṣaḥ kalpayitum 
[40,ii^3]	vyavahāra viparyayāt hi sa kalpyeta tattva darśanasya tu vedānta janmanaḥ pratipakṣa tvāt tattva pratihati mātra hetuḥ eva anādiḥ avidya anubandhaḥ kalpyate tatas doṣa anubandhaḥ prāmāṇyam ca iti na virodhaḥ śabdaḥ tu saṃbhāvita doṣaḥ durlabha prāmāṇyaḥ eva syāt dṛśyate hi doṣebhyaḥ vyavahāra visaṃvādi jñāna utpattiḥ tatra doṣa āśaṅkayā vyavahāra visaṃvādasya śaṅkita tvāt tattva pratighātasya ca na tattva āvedana lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam na vyavahāra avisaṃvāda lakṣaṇam iti tasmāt śabdasya prāmāṇya abhyupagame pramāṇa antara virodhe api tasya eva balavat tvam iti sāṃpratam 
[40,ii^4]	yat tu pratyakṣa ādi apekṣaṇāt iti tatra ucyate na pramitau apekṣāvattā śabdasya pratyakṣa ādiṣu kim tu svarūpa siddhau anyathā pramāṇam eva na syāt tathā ca sva kārye apekṣa tvāt na pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ hīyate pratyakṣa ādayaḥ pi svarūpa siddhau na anya anapekṣāḥ kārye hi sa apekṣa tvam sāmarthyam apakarṣati iti yat tu eteṣām prāmāṇyam anumātavyam iti kaḥ vā anyathā āha vyavahāra avisaṃvādi lakṣaṇam tu tat na tattva āvedana lakṣaṇam vyāvahārika prāmāṇya upetebhyaḥ pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ siddhāt āmnāyāt tattva darśanam tad virodhāt teṣu tattva darśana aṃśam eva apabādhate na vyavahāra avisaṃvāda aṃśam 
[40,ii^5]	dṛṣṭam ca hetu tvena apekṣitāyāḥ api pūrvasyāḥ pratipatteḥ parasyāḥ pratipatteḥ balīyaḥ tvam yathā dūra stheṣu vanaspatiṣu hasti pratipattibhyaḥ vanaspati pratipatteḥ apekṣitāḥ hi hasti pratipattayaḥ vyakta vanaspati pratipattyā hetu tvena na tasyāḥ indriya artha saṃnikarṣa mātrāt janma āpāte abhāvāt na ca deśa viśeṣāt tad deśa sthasya eva utpatteḥ tasmāt puras vartiṣu vanaspatiṣu praṇihita manasaḥ prācya viparyāsa anugatam ati saṃskāra saciva indriya ādi saṃyoga kāritā sā iti mantavyam evam eka ādi saṃkhyā buddhi apāyāḥ viṃśati ādi buddhayaḥ api udāhāryāḥ 
[40,ii^6]	evam ca yat eke varṇayanti svayam eva vyāhatā vedānta artha pratipattiḥ nābhedaḥ bhedam antareṇa śakyaḥ avasātum bheda upāyāḥ hi tasya pratipattiḥ tatra abhedaḥ samākṣipta bhedaḥ eva pratāyate iti vyāghātaḥ tad apāstam yatas upāyam ākṣipati pratipattiḥ na upāyasya paramārtha tām mithyājñānāt api tattva pratipatteḥ vyāvahārikam ca bhedasya satya tvam iṣṭam eva iti vyabhicāra darśanam ca duṣṭa hetu janmanoḥ śabda pratyakṣayoḥ samānam itarayoḥ api tulyam avyabhicāri tvam tathā anavakāśa tvam api yadi khalu ekam advayam vedānta arthaḥ kaḥ teṣām anyaḥ avakāśaḥ 
[40,ii^7]	atha aupacārika tvam eka tvam tad arthaḥ avivakṣita artha tā vā japa upayoginām tatra virodhaḥ eva na asti iti bala abala cintā na avatarati tat kutas sa avakāśa tvena daurbalyam katham ca mukhyam artham ati laṅghya upacaritaḥ avakāśaḥ katham vautpattike śabdasya artham prati śeṣa bhāve dṛṣṭaḥ hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam aviśiṣṭaḥ tu vākya arthaḥ iti ca avivakṣita artha tā pramāṇa antara virodhāt iti ced vārtam etat na pramāṇasya pramāṇa antara apekṣam prāmāṇyam yena tad virodhe svarasam jahyāt tad apekṣa tve hi tad anuguṇa tayā varteta nirapekṣasya kaḥ pramāṇa antara anusaraṇe hetuḥ 
[40,ii^8]	laukikāḥ tu śabdāḥ pramāṇa antara apekṣam sva artham abhidadhati iti yuktā teṣām tad anusāriṇī vṛttiḥ tulye tu anapekṣa tve kim iti na viparyayaḥ ubhayoḥ vā vyāghātāt aprāmāṇyam paurvāparye pūrva daurbalyam iti vā rajata jñānasya iva pūrvasya bādhaḥ na khalu rajata jñāna virodhāt śukti jñānam anya viṣayam aviṣayam vā katham tarhi vede guṇa vādaḥ yatra śrautaiḥ arthaiḥ pramāṇa artha niṣpatteḥ asambhavaḥ tatra dvitīyasyāḥ api vṛtteḥ śabdānām pravṛtti darśanāt tayā pramāṇa viṣaya lābhaḥ yatra tu śabdāḥ svarasena labhante viṣayam tatra na pramāṇa antara virodhāt apāvartante na hi eṣām pramāṇa antara nibandhanaḥ arthaḥ yena tad vaśāt apāvarteran 
[42,i^1]	atha matam ubhaya anugrahāt evam kalpyate evam hi śabdaḥ pratyakṣa ādayaḥ ca anugṛhītāḥ bhavanti anyathā pratyakṣa ādayaḥ atyantam apabādhitāḥ syuḥ na etat sāram pramāṇa sāmarthya anusāreṇa prameye kācid kalpanā syāt pramāṇe tu svarasa siddham parityajya kalpanāyām na nibandhanam asti tasmāt pramāṇa anusāreṇa vikalpa samuccaya vyavasthāḥ kalpyante na ubhaya anugrahāt na ubhayam anugṛhītavyam iti pramāṇam asti te eva pramāṇe iti ced yadi matam na pramāṇasya pramāṇa antarāt anugrāhya tvam api tu svatas eva pramāṇa tvāt eva hi tasya tena artha vyavasthāpanā yathā tarhi tatas arthaḥ avagamyate tathā vyavasthāpanīyaḥ evam tat anugṛhītam bhavati anyathā bādhitam syāt apramāṇikā ca artha vyavasthā tatas svarasena apratīteḥ anyasya ca abhāvāt itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt ca 
[42,i^2]	prāmāṇyāt siddhāt artha antare pratītiḥ prāmāṇya ani athā anupapattyā kalpanīyā tad pratīteḥ ca prāmāṇyam sva rasalabhye tu arthe pratītitaḥ eva prāmāṇyam iti na itaretara āśraya tā tasmāt virodhe bādhaḥ eva pūrvasya pramāṇa anusārī tathā pratīteḥ na uttarasya viṣaya antara kalpanā na khalu rajata jñāna anugrahāya śukti śakala jñānasya gocaraḥ aparaḥ kalpyate na ca pratyakṣa ādīnām ananya gati tvāt anavakāśa tvam yā khalu rajata ādi vibhramāṇām gatiḥ sā teṣām api yadi teṣām upacaritaḥ kalpitaḥ vā viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām api tathā atha asattvāt tasya āviṣayāḥ avidyamāna arthāḥ pratyakṣa ādayaḥ api evam tasmāt avivakṣita artha tvam upacarita artha tvam vā gatiḥ ubhayoḥ aviśiṣṭā etena idam api parākṛtam yat āhuḥ śabdasya pramāṇa antara virodhe dṛṣṭam upacarita artha tvam avivakṣita artha tvam vā loke tasmāt pratyakṣa ādi virodhe vedāntānām tathā abhāvaḥ iti pratyakṣa ādiṣu api tathā darśanāt iti 
[43,i]	yat tu mukhya tvāt pratiṣṭhita arthaiḥ apahata viṣayaḥ āmnāya iti atas eva bādhakaḥ śukti jñāna vat na ca tad anusāreṇa artha kalpanām arhati anapekṣa tvāt na tad adhīnam asya pramāṇa tvam na taiḥ saṃbhūyakāri tvam nāmnā ayasya pratyakṣa ādīnām ca eka vākya bhāvaḥ paraspara anapekṣaḥ hi ubhayatra buddhi utpādaḥ tatra para balīyaḥ tvam nyāyyam yathā uktam pūrvāt para balīyaḥ tvam tatra nāma pratīyatām anyonya nirapekṣāṇām yatra janma dhiyām bhavet 
[43,ii^1]	yatra tu eka vākya tayā saṃbhūyakāri tvam tatra anupajāta virodhitayā sva rasa vṛttyā mukhye sthite prathamayā vṛttyā tad eka vākya tvam pratipattum aśaknuvanti tad apekṣita artha samarpaṇa anupapatteḥ para padāni dvitīyayā vṛttyā pūrva apekṣitam artham samarpayanti eka vākyatā sāmarthyāt iti mukhya balīyaḥ tvam yat tu vyākula tvāt iti tatra ucyate syāt vyākula tvam yadi karma vidhayaḥ bheda pratipādana parāḥ syuḥ te tu siddham bhedam upāśritya idam anena ittham sādhayet iti puruṣa hita anuśāsana pradhānāḥ syāt etat
