[43,ii^2]	asati bhede aṃśa traya pratyasta mayāt kutas hita anuśāsanam ucyate yathā khalu śyena ādiṣu na hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtāni iti pratiṣedhāt sādhya aṃśa pratyasta maye api anuśāsanam evam sarvatra sarva aṃśa pratyasta maye api tathā hi niṣiddha anartha udayā katham hiṃsā sādhyā syāt atha bhavati kasya cit tīvra krodha ākrānta svānta tayā samuddhata dhvānta tiraskṛta viveka vijñānasya anartham api artha tvena paśyataḥ śāstra upadeśam atikrāmataḥ tathā jyotiṣṭoma ādiṣu nisarga ja avidyā upadarśitāḥ apratibuddhānām trayaḥ api aṃśāḥ tān upāśritya teṣām anuśāsanam 
[43,ii^3]	pratibuddhāḥ tu karma vidhibhiḥ na anuśiṣyante yathā śyena ādi vidhibhiḥ apajita krodha arātayaḥ tat evam vyavahāra siddha bheda āśrayeṣu karma vidhiṣu yadi api bheda pratītiḥ asti tathā api teṣām atatparatvāt na tatra prāmāṇyam vṛttānteṣu iva arthavāda padānām tathā ca kutas taiḥ veda antānām parāhatiḥ vedāntaiḥ vā teṣām api ca pratyakṣa ādiṣu eva parāhatiḥ upalabhyate bādhya bādhaka bhāva darśanāt rajata śukti śakala ādi jñāneṣu bheda abheda pratīteḥ ca sarvatra tat evam balavat tve api āmnāyasya yaḥ nāma manda dhīḥ laukika vacasām pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ upacarita artha tva darśanāt loka vat vede api śabda vṛttam iti manyate yaḥ vā nirūḍha nibiḍa tayā bheda darśana andhakārasya pratyakṣa ādīnām eva balavat tvam manyate loka vacasām ca taiḥ bādha darśanāt tad pratibodhanāya virodhaḥ nirasyate na hi yaḥ nāma manda viṣeṇa vṛścikena daṣṭaḥ mriyate na asau na cikitsyate iti 
[44,i]	tatra pratyakṣe trayaḥ kalpāḥ vastu svarūpa vidhiḥ vastu antarasya vyavacchedaḥ ubhayam vetti ubhayasmin api traividhyam yaugapadyam vyavaccheda pūrvakaḥ vidhiḥ vidhi pūrvakaḥ vyavacchedaḥ iti tatra vastu antara vyavacchede ubhayasmin vā bhedaḥ pratyakṣa gocaraḥ iti bhavati virodhaḥ sva rūpa vidhi mātre tu kasyacid vyavacchedena śūnye na bhedaḥ pramāṇa arthaḥ na hi vyavacchedāt ṛte bheda siddhiḥ vidhi mātra vyāpāram ca pratyakṣam atas na virodhaḥ katham iti ucyate labdha rūpe kvacid kiñcittādṛś eva niṣidhyate vidhānam antareṇa atas na viṣedhasya saṃbhavaḥ 
[44,ii^1]	na tāvat vyavaccheda mātram pratyakṣa vyāpāraḥ na yugapad ubhayam na vyavaccheda pūrvakam vidhānam yatas siddhe viṣaye siddha rūpam eva niṣidhyate na idam iha na ayamayam iti siddhe bhū tale siddhaḥ ghaṭaḥ gavi vai aśvaḥ na pratiṣedhyāt pratiṣedha viṣayāt ca vinā pratiṣedhaḥ avakalpate katham tarhi atyanta asatām pradhāna kha puṣpa ādīnām pratiṣedhaḥ na hi tatra kvacid deśe kāle vā niṣedhaḥ ātyantika tvāt na api kutaścid siddhi atyanta asattvāt tatra kecid āhuḥ kha puṣpa ādiṣu tāvat siddheṣu kha ādiṣu tadvidhāḥ puṣpa ādayaḥ niṣidhyante pradhānam na asti iti jagat kāraṇe sukha duḥkha moha ātma tā vibhakta kārya tva ādīni nivāryante 
[44,ii^2_45,i]	anye tu kutaścid nimittāt buddhau labdha rūpāṇām bahis niṣedhaḥ kriyate iti varṇayanti anyathā daiva niṣiddhe kaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ aprāpta rūpe prāpta rūpe vā katham atyantāya pratiṣedhaḥ api ca anapekṣita viṣaya niṣedhye vyavacchede śūnyatā pramāṇa arthaḥ syāt na bhedaḥ sarvasya sarvatra aviśeṣeṇa niṣedhāt yaḥ tu bhedāya vyavacchedaḥ sa bhedyayoḥ siddhim apekṣate na ca sā vidhāna ādṛtaḥ iti prāk vidhānam eṣitavyam vidhi pūrvakaḥ eva ca niṣedhaḥ aṅgīkriyate iti na api vidhi pūvakaḥ vyavacchedaḥ yatas kramaḥ saṃgacchate yuktyā na eka vijñāna karmaṇoḥ na saṃnihita jam tat ca tad anyāmarśi jāyate 
[45,ii^1]	na khalu eka pramāṇa jñāna vyāpārau santau vidhi vyavacchedau kramavantau yujyete kṣaṇika tvāt kramavatoḥ hi vyāpārayoḥ paścāt tanaḥ na tad vyāpāraḥ syāt vyavadhānāt api ca janma eva buddheḥ vyāpāraḥ artha avagraha rūpāyāḥ sā ced arha vidhāna rūpa udayā vidheḥ eva asyāḥ vyāpāraḥ yaugapadyasya niṣedhāt utpannāyāḥ ca punar anutpatteḥ api ca saṃnihita artha ālambanam pratyakṣam na asaṃnihitam artham avabhāsayitum arhati na ca anavabhāsamāna rūpam vyavacchettum paryāpnoti anavabhāsamāne hi tatra vyavacchedye vyavaccheda mātram syāt na vyavacchedaḥ kasyacid sarvasya vā syāt tasmāt na anavabhāsamāne vyavacchedye vyavacchedaḥ na ca saṃnihita artha avalambane pratyakṣe asaṃnihita avabhāsaḥ yuktaḥ katham idānīm bādhakam pratyakṣam tatra hi pūrva artha niṣedha puraḥsaraḥ anya vidhiḥ eka jñāne abhyupeyate asaṃnihita niṣedhya avabhāsaḥ ca tasmāt na eṣa niyamaḥ yatas pūrvaḥ niṣedhaḥ eka jñāna vyāpāre ca kramaḥ pratyakṣeṇa ca asaṃnihita artha avabhāsaḥ 
[45,ii^2]	na etat sāram tatra api pūrva vijñāna vihite rajata ādau idam iti ca saṃnihita artha sāmānye niṣedhaḥ vidhi pūrvaḥ eva śuktikā vidhiḥ tu virodhi niṣedha pūrvaḥ ucyate vidhi pūrva tā ca niyamena niṣedhasya ucyate na vidheḥ niṣedha pūrvaka tā niṣidhyate na ca tatra eka jñānasya krama vat vyāpāra tā ubhaya rūpasya utpatteḥ pūrva jñāna prāpita tvāt ca viṣaya vyavacchedyayoḥ na asaṃbhavaḥ pūrva jñāna avabhāsite ca vyavacchedye vyavacchedasya vṛtteḥ na asaṃnihita artha avabhāsa prasaṅgaḥ pūrva apekṣasya tasya utpatteḥ pūrva apekṣayā eva ca tat dvi rūpam udeti anyathā eka rūpam eva udīyāt api ca sarva vyavacchedān apākurvataḥ kaḥ vyavacchedaḥ abhimataḥ yena pratyavasthīyeta siddhaḥ sa lokaḥ iti ced ayam vā kim na loka siddhaḥ na aśvaḥ gauḥ na gauḥ aśvaḥ iti 
[46,i]	yat tu matam eka vidhiḥ eva anya vyavacchedaḥ tathā hi darśanam yathā eva tad ākāratayā tad rūpam vidadhāti tathā tad eka ākāra pratiniyamāt tat eva na anyat iti anyat vyavacchinatti tad sāmarthya prabhāvitau ca idam na idam iti vikalpau bhāva abhāva vyavahāram pravartayataḥ na hi eka ākāra pratiniyatāt ananya saṃsargiṇaḥ jñānāt anyaḥ anya vyavacchedaḥ tatra ucyate vidhānam eva na ekasya vyavacchedaḥ anya gocaraḥ mā sma bhūt aviśeṣeṇa mā na bhūt eka dhī juṣām 
[46,ii^1]	na eka pratiniyamaḥ anya abhāva niścaya nimittam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpti asya itarasya ca aviśeṣeṇa vyavaccheda prasaṅgāt tad pratiniyamaḥ hi tatas anyasya asaṃsargaḥ tathā ca asaṃsargāt vyavacchede tasya dṛśya adṛśyayoḥ aviśeṣāt ubhayoḥ vyavacchedaḥ syāt atha matam bhavati eva tathā hi yāvantaḥ asya anātmāna stān aviśeṣeṇa tad ātma niyamāt darśanam apākaroti tathā ca na asya anyaḥ ātmānaḥ tad deśa kālāḥ tu bhaveyuḥ rūpa ādi vat avirodhāt tatra upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ viśeṣaḥ tad deśa kāla vyavaccheda avadhāraṇāya saṃbhavati hi anupalabhyaḥ tad deśa kālaḥ anātma anupalabhyamānaḥ api anya upalabdhau itara vat anyathā na tulya upalambha yogyatas syāt 
[46,ii^2]	satyam asti ayam vibhāgaḥ na tu idānīm darśana pratiniyamasya sāmarthyam tathā hi pratiniyatam api tatra deśe kāle ca rūpe darśanam tayoḥ yathā rūpa vidhi mātra upakṣayāt na rasam vyavacchinatti tathā bhū bhāga darśana niyamaḥ api bhū bhāga vidhi mātra vyāpāra tvāt na ghaṭadṛśyam api vyavacchindyāt vyavacchede vā sarvasya vyavacchedaḥ tasmāt dṛśya vyavacchede api hetu antaram upāsyam na darśana pratiniyama mātram tathā ca ātmā antara vyavacchedaḥ api na tatas siddhim upāśnute kāmam vidheḥ vidheyā sattva vyavaccheda rūpa tvāt tad abhāvaḥ vyavacchidyeta na ātma antara sat tā tad deśa kālayoḥ iva anupalabhya sattā na ekasya bahavaḥ ātmānaḥ iti ced anyatas tarhi virodhāt vyavacchedaḥ na darśana niyamāt asati ca vyavacchede kutas bahu tvam kutas vā virodhaḥ itaretara āśrayam vā tasmāt na eka vidhiḥ anya vyavacchedaḥ api ca eka niyamāt anya vyavacchede citra ādiṣu nīla ādīnām eka darśana bhājām bhedaḥ na sidhyet eka jñāna saṃsargāt ekatra jñānasya aniyamāt 
[47,i^1]	nanu prakṛtyā eva bhinnāḥ bhāvāḥ tān tadvidhān vidadhat eva darśanam parasparataḥ vyāvartayati na hi vyāvṛttiḥ anyā vyāvṛttimataḥ tatra vyāvṛttimat vidhau sā api vidhīyate eva yat prakṛtiḥ khalu yaḥ padārthaḥ sa tayā eva prakṛtyāḥ vidheyaḥ anyathā na tasya vidhiḥ syāt vyāvṛtta svabhāvāḥ ca bhāvāḥ yathāyatham darśaneṣu nirbhāsante tasmāt tathā eva vidhīyante iti atra api asaṃspṛṣṭa nirbhāsanāt asaṃspṛṣṭa svabhāva tve dṛśyayoḥ aviśeṣeṇa vyavacchedaḥ tad avasthaḥ api ca na bhedaḥ vastunaḥ rūpam tad abhāva prasaṅgataḥ arūpeṇa ca bhinna tvam vastunaḥ na avakalpate 
[47,i^2]	na vyāvṛttiḥ vastu svabhāvaḥ sā khalu eka aneka adhiṣṭhānā pratijñāyate prajñāyate ca tathā ca tasyāḥ ekasyāḥ aneka vṛtteḥ vastu svabhāva tve vastūnām api bhedaḥ na syāt na ekasmāt abhinna svabhāvam bhinnam yujyate tadvat eva atha mā bhūt eṣa doṣaḥ iti artha antaram eva vyāvṛttiḥ āsthīyate tathā api vyāvṛtteḥ a rūpa tvāt svarūpeṇa na bhāvāḥ vyāvṛttāḥ syuḥ aparaḥ kalpaḥ bhedaḥ parasparān ātma svabhāvaḥ sa ced vastunaḥ svabhāvaḥ vastūnām abhāva prasaṅgaḥ abhāva ātmaka tva pratijñānāt aparaḥ prakāraḥ bhedaḥ ced vastunaḥ svabhāvaḥ na ekam kiñcana vastu syāt bhedena ekatvasya virodhāt 
[47,i^3]	paramāṇuḥ api bhedāt aneka ātmakaḥ iti na ekaḥ tathā ca tat samuccaya rūpaḥ anekaḥ api asya ātmā na avakalpate tatra ekatva aneka tvayoḥ anupapatteḥ tṛtīya prakāra asaṃbhavāt ca vastunaḥ niḥsvabhāva tva prasaṅgaḥ anyā vyākhyā dvitīya ardhasya vyatireka avyatireka vikalpe pratyavatiṣṭhate vastu gataḥ eṣa vibhāgaḥ tad svabhāva tvam anya tvam ca iti na avastuni vikalpa viracita śarīre bhede avatāram arhati tathā hi tattva anya tva abhyām anirvacanīyaḥ anādi vikalpa vāsanā upādāna vikalpa paridarśita śarīraḥ ayam asmāt bhinnaḥ ayamanayoḥ bhedaḥ iti vyavahāram pravartayati na bhedaḥ nāma kiñcid vastu yasya tattvam anya tvam vā kiñcid vicāryeta 
[47,i^4_48,i]	tatra idam punar upatiṣṭhate arūpeṇa ca bhinna tvam vastunaḥ na avakalpate yadi tarhi arūpaḥ niḥsvabhāvaḥ bhedaḥ na hi vastu sthityā asti vikalpaiḥ eva kevalam upadarśyate na tarhi vastunaḥ bhinna tvam paramārthataḥ bheda abhāvāt na hi kalpitena svabhāvena pāramārthikī tadvat tā yujyate kalpitā eva syāt tat etat asmābhiḥ ucyamānam kim iti bhavān na anumanyate vayam api etat eva brūmaḥ na bhedaḥ bhāvataḥ asti anādya vidyā vilasitam etat iti yat uktam bheda ātma tve vastunaḥ eka vastu abhāvaḥ tad bhāvāditarasya api iti vastu abhāvaḥ tatra āhuḥ para apekṣam vastunaḥ bheda svabhāvam brūmaḥ na ātma apekṣam yena virodhāt eka vastu abhāvaḥ syāt sva rūpeṇa tu ekam vastu para apekṣayā bhinnam iti tatra ucyate pauruṣeyīm apekṣām ca na hi vastu anuvartate 
[48,ii^1]	na apekṣā nāma kaścid vastu dharmaḥ yena vastūni vyavasthāpyeran na khalu sva hetu prāpita udayeṣu svabhāva vyavasthiteṣu vastuṣu svabhāva sthitaye vastu antara apekṣā yujyate tatra puruṣa pratyaya dharmaḥ ayam na ca puruṣa pratyaya anuvidhāyīni vastūni sva hetubhyaḥ sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ atas na tad anusāreṇa vastu rūpam vyavatiṣṭhate vyavasthita vastu svarūpa anusāreṇa eva tasya vyavasthā nyāyyā tad pūrvaka tvāt paraspara apekṣāyām ca vastu svabhāva sthitau itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt athavā yat uktam ekasmāt bhedāt avyatiredāt vastunaḥ bheda abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti tatra āhuḥ na bhedaḥ ekaḥ rūpa virodhāt eka tve ca tad nimittam vastūnām eka tvam syāt tasmāt pratibhāvam bhedaḥ bhidyate katham tarhi aneka āśraya tvam 
[48,ii^2]	apekṣātaḥ tathā hi pratiyogi apekṣam tasya svarūpam vyavasthitam tathā ca yathāyatham bhedaiḥ pratiyogi apekṣaiḥ ātma bhūtaiḥ bhinnāḥ sarve bhāvāḥ iti tatra ucyate pauruṣeyīm iti puruṣaḥ hi ekam artham gṛhītvā param apekṣate kārya artham sva hetubhyaḥ tu pratilabdha avikala svabhāvānām bhāvānām bhāva antareṣu kimartha apekṣā nanu svabhāva sthitaye nānāvidhāḥ hi bhāva svabhāvāḥ tatra kaścid pratiyogi apekṣayā eva vyavatiṣṭhate vastu tattve yathā ayam eva bhedaḥ na tarhi hetubhyaḥ bhāvasya avikala ātma lābhaḥ bheda ākhyasya rūpasya pratiyogi apekṣa tvāt hetu antarāt ca pratiyoginaḥ saṃpadyamānaḥ paścāt bhedaḥ na svabhāvaḥ syāt 
[49,i^1]	syāt etat avikala rūpaḥ eva bhāvaḥ hetubhyaḥ jāyate tatra bheda ākhyam rūpam pratiyogi apekṣam na anapekṣam kadācid ittasya tadvidha tvāt tena tadvidhena eva saha jāyate iti na vikala rūpa prādurbhāvaḥ tatra ucyate bhavatu tadvidhasya prādurbhāvaḥ apekṣā arthaḥ tu vaktavyaḥ yasya hi yatra kiñcid āyatate tat tat apekṣate iti ucyate na anyaḥ viśeṣaḥ sa apekṣa nirapekṣayoḥ vyapasthāpakaḥ nirūpyate tatra na tāvat utpattiḥ pratiyoginī āyatate sva hetubhyaḥ avikalasya utpatteḥ na artha kriyā tad asaṃnidhāne api tasya artha kriyā darśanāt 
[49,i^2]	pratītiḥ ced tathā hi na anapekṣya pratiyoginam bhedaḥ pratīyate iti na tarhi bheda svabhāvaḥ sa apekṣaḥ tasmin avasthite vastu sthiti uttara kālā pratītiḥ artha antaram eva pratiyoginam apekṣate yathā vyavasthita anapekṣa svabhāvāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi apekṣāyām pratītau na sa apekṣa svabhāvāḥ kathyate itaretara āśrayāt ca na pratītiḥ api paraspara āyattau akalpate na ca vastu mātrāt anavagṛhīta bhedāt bheda siddhiḥ ekasmin api tad prasaṅgāt tasmāt pauruṣeyīm apekṣāyām na vastu anuvarttate atas na vastu svabhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[50,i_50,iii]	anyā vyākhyā na bhedaḥ vastunaḥ rūpam āpekṣikaḥ hi pratīyate na ca apekṣāyām puruṣa pratyayam vastu anuvartate vyavasthita vastu pūrvaka tvāt iti katham tarhi pitṛ ādayaḥ na hi te apekṣayā vinā na ca khapuṣpa gandharvanagara ādi tulyāḥ avisaṃvādi vyavahāra aṅga tayā loka siddha tvāt ucyate bhedaḥ api evam kim na loka siddhaḥ api ca pitṛ ādi viṣaye apekṣā janana ādi prabhāvitā eka kriyā viśeṣeṇa vyapekṣā hrasva dīrghayoḥ 
[50,iv]	vyavasthite eva janya janaka śaktī pitṛ putra śabdayoḥ abhidheye te tu samāna janana vyāpāra viṣaye tau āskandataḥ svabhāva bhedāt atas yena samāna tvam tatra apekṣā etat uktam bhavati śabda arthaḥ tatra sa apekṣaḥ na vastu apekṣā hetuḥ ca tatra sādhāraṇī kriyā vidyate vyavasthitayoḥ api vastunoḥ bhāva bhede tu ayam vastu tattva gataḥ vicāraḥ na ca apekṣā hetuḥ kaścid upalabhyate hrasva dīrghayoḥ api eka jātīyāyām kriyāyām deśa vyāptau nyūna adhika bhāvāt evam draṣṭavyam 
[50,v^1]	yadi tarhi kārya bhedāt api apekṣā hanta artha kriyā bhedāt eva bhāvānām paraspara apekṣaḥ bhedaḥ setsyati kim ca asatyām api darśanāt bheda siddhau vidhi mātra vyāpāra tvāt kārya bhedāt eva kāraṇa bhedam anumimīmahe na ekatve kārya bhedaḥ kalpate kāraṇa svabhāva apekṣa tvāt kārya bhedasya tat jananaḥ ca id asya svabhāvaḥ na anya jananaḥ tasmāt kārya antarasya anyatas janma iti tat idam bhedena eva bheda prasādhanam na ati caturaśram api ca artha kriyā kṛte bhede rūpa bhedaḥ na labhyate dāha pāka vibhāgena kṛśānuḥ na hi bhedavān na artha kriyā bhedāt bhāvānām paraspara apekṣaḥ rūpa bhedaḥ pratīyate na api anumātum śakyate vyapadeśa bheda mātram tu syāt ekasmin api vahnau dāha pāka ādi kārya bheda dṛṣṭeḥ atha matam rūpa ādi samūhaḥ vahniḥ tatra rūpāt prakāśaḥ sparśāt dāha iti 
[50,v^2]	kāmam dāha pākau tu sparśāt eva tau ca loke pratīti bhedau sati api saṃyogi dravya vikriyā sāmānye karma ca ekam saṃyoga vibhāga saṃskārāṇām hetuḥ ātmā ca icchā ādīnām sattva ādayaḥ ca pratyekam abhedāt lāghava prakāśa ādīnām rūpa ādayaḥ jñāna viśeṣāṇām sajātī yakṣaṇānām ca iti utprekṣitavyam nanu na artha kriyā bheda mātrāt bhedam brūmaḥ api tu tatra asaṃbhāvinyāḥ adṛṣṭāyāḥ yathā cakṣuṣi sati api adṛṣṭāyāḥ ca badhire tatra asaṃbhāvinyāḥ śabda buddheḥ indriya bhedaḥ paraspara asaṃbhavi kāryāḥ ca prāyeṇa bhāvāḥ anya kāryasya anyatra adarśanāt atha kārya asaṃbhavaḥ katham pratyetavyaḥ nanu uktam tatra adarśanāt na tarhi asaṃbhavaḥ yasya khalva dvayam jagat tasya kārya jātam ekatra eva dṛśyate iti katham adarśanam tatra siddhe bhede tatra adarśanam tatra adarśanāt ca bheda siddhiḥ iti ita retara āśrayāt na bheda anumānam 
[50,v^3]	atha matam adṛṣṭasya darśanāt iti tat asat ekasmāt api kramavatām kāryāṇām darśanāt syāt etat ekāntataḥ abhede kārya darśana adarśane na yukte viśeṣa abhāvāt na tarhi kārya bhedaḥ abhedam apabādhate tad anupamardena viśeṣa mātra anumānam syāt tat ca kalpanā viṣayam na eva avajānīmahe vastu sataḥ tasya ayogāt tattva anya tvayoḥ asaṃbhavāt yaḥ tu kṣaṇika vādī tattvam eva viśeṣasya na manyate tasya asati kāraṇa svabhāva abhede katham tulya svabhāva kārya utpādaḥ atha niranvaya vināśānām api kalpanā viṣayāt abhedāt kāryasya tulya tā hanta tarhi bhedāt eva kalpanā viṣayāt kārya bheda siddheḥ mudhā kāraṇa bheda kalpanā atha kārya abhede na kāraṇa svabhāva abhedaḥ apekṣyeta bhinna svabhāvebhyaḥ sahakāribhyaḥ eka kārya utpatteḥ yathā cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ rūpa vijñānasya 
[50,v^4]	yathā tarhi kārya svabhāva abhedāya na kāraṇa svabhāva abhedaḥ apekṣyate tathā tad bhedāya kāraṇa bhedaḥ api na apekṣitavyaḥ api ca aneka kāraṇa janye api ekasmin kārye kāraṇa vyāpāra viṣaya bhedaḥ tena eva varṇitaḥ yathā rūpa jñānasya cakṣuṣaḥ rūpa grahaṇa niyamaḥ samanantara jñānāt upalambha ātma tā viṣayāt tat ākāra tā iti yadi ca kārya tulya tvam na hetu sāmya kṛtam na kāryāt hetu anumānam syāt bhinna jātīyāt api tulya jātīya utpatti saṃbhavāt hetu abhedaḥ ced na kārya abhedaḥ upayujyate kaḥ tulya jātīyāt vijātīyasya janma nivārayet tatra yathā vyāvahārikāt abhedāt kārya abhedaḥ tathā vyāvahārikāt bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ iti na viśeṣaḥ syāt etat kalpitaḥ ced bhedaḥ kārya bhedāya prabhuḥ na tarhi kalpitaḥ na hi anyat parama artha satas lakṣaṇam artha kriyā sāmarthyāt tulyam idam abhede api 
[52,i^1]	yaḥ api manyate yugapad viruddha artha kriyā darśanāt bheda a agatiḥ tathā hi janana maraṇa vṛddhi kṣaya sthāna gamana śoka harṣa ādi vividha viruddha dharma samupetam ekadā viśvam upalabhyate tad bheda vat iti gamyate tasya api idam eva uttaram āvṛttyā dāha pāka vibhāgena iti katham idam tāvat ayam praṣṭavyaḥ kaḥ viruddha arthaḥ yadi ekatra asaṃbhavaḥ saḥ asiddhaḥ atha paraspara vyavacchinna ātma tā janana ādayaḥ ca paraspara rūpa nivṛtti ātmānaḥ iti na tarhi atas bheda siddhiḥ ekasmin api vahnau dagdhṛ tva paktṛ tva darśanāt na hi paraspara vyavacchedam antareṇa nānātvam dharmāṇām tatas ced bhedaḥ na aneka dharmakam ekam kiñcid syāt atha paraspara abhāva ātma tā eva virodhaḥ na ekasmin saḥ eva bhavati na ca bhavati iti tatas bheda avasāyaḥ tat asat na hi evam dharmau eva kutas tayoḥ virodhāt bheda avagatiḥ 
[52,i^2]	kha puṣpa ādiṣu ca ubhaya abhāvāt ubhaya prasaṅgaḥ atha vadhya ghātaka bhāvaḥ virodhaḥ harṣaḥ śokam hanti śokaḥ ca tam evam itareṣu api tatra api na ajātaḥ ekaḥ anyam nāśayati na anya adhikaraṇam tasmāt eka adhikaraṇaḥ bhūtvā nāśayati iti vācyam evam ca tayoḥ eka adhikaraṇa tva darśanāt na tad darśanena adhikaraṇa bheda anumānam avyabhicāram atha bhāva rūpa tad vyavaccheda ātmānaḥ dharmāḥ virodhinaḥ nitya tva anitya tva mūrta tva amūrta tva ādayaḥ tad saṃbandhāt bheda gatiḥ tat api na yatas na avaśyam yaḥ yatra bhavati sa tam vyāpnoti na hi ratha ādayaḥ tad saṃyoga ādayaḥ vā nabhaḥ vyaśnuvate anyān vā saṃyoginaḥ pṛthivī ādīn avacchinna tvāt evam avacchinnāḥ dharmāḥ anavacchinnam anantam artham āśrayantaḥ api na vyaśnuvate atas na ekasmin api bhāva abhāva virodhaḥ 
[53,i^1]	yaḥ tu manyeta artha kriyā bhedaḥ artha kriyā vyavasthā tatas bheda adhigamaḥ eka tve hi na vyavasthā yujyate tathā ca payasaḥ api tailam tilebhyaḥ ca dadhi syāt tathā ekasmin jāyamāne sarvam jāyeta naśyati ca naśyet anyathā bhedaḥ eva śabda antareṇa uktaḥ syāt tat uktam saha utpatti vināśau sarvam ca sarvatra upayujyeta iti tasya āpi idam eva uttaram dāha pāka vibhāgena iti yadi kārya nānā tvam vyavasthā na tayā tilānām payasaḥ ca bhedam pratipadyate atha payasaḥ dadhnaḥ janma na anyatas iti vyavasthā na anya tvam siddhayā vyavasthayā pramitsitam tad lakṣaṇam anupraveṣṭum arhati tasyāḥ asiddhi prasaṅgāt tasmāt dadhi janana śaktiḥ tad abhāvaḥ ca vyavasthā tatas bhedaḥ na hi eka viṣayaḥ ekasya śakti aśaktī yujyete iti sa ca ayam virodhi dharma yogaḥ bheda hetuḥ anantaram eva nirāsi 
[53,i^2]	yathā khalu dīrgha kālāḥ padārthāḥ mita kālaiḥ dharmaiḥ saṃbadhyamānāḥ tad dharmāṇaḥ atad dharmāṇaḥ ca na virodha pada bhājaḥ tathā parimita deśaiḥ vipula deśāḥ anantāḥ ca katham anantasya antavān dharmaḥ iti ced vyatireke anivarcanīya tve vā na asti asaṃbhāvanā avakāśaḥ avyatireke api dīrgha kālasya iva mita kālaḥ yaḥ api dīrgha kālam artham na pratipadyate tam prati idam punar paṭhitavyam dāha pāka vibhāgena iti ekaḥ api vahniḥ kiñcid eva dahati pacati ca tathā ca dāhakaḥ ca ādāhakaḥ ca na bhidyate tathā na dāha antarāṇi pāka antarāṇi vā karoti tasmin eva dāhye pākye ca tathā bīja ādayaḥ pratyekam samarthāḥ api na aṅkura antarāṇi janayanti na api sāmagrī tathā ca janakatvam ajanaka tvam iti 
[53,i^3]	atha ekasmin eva janaka śaktiḥ anyam pradhvastam āgāminam vā ekam kim na janayati atha tatra eva eṣām sāmarthyam na anyatra tulya jātīye api kutas tasya eva utpatteḥ kārya gamya tvāt ca sāmarthyasya tathā ca na śaktiḥ aśaktiḥ ca iti virodhaḥ abhede api tarhi payasaḥ tilānām dadhnaḥ anutpattau na virodhaḥ tathā hi yasya tāvat dadhnaḥ payasaḥ janma na tasya tilebhyaḥ anutpattiḥ yena śakti aśakti virodhāt bhedaḥ syāt kutas tilānām payasaḥ abhedāt atha dadhi antarasya anutpatteḥ virodhaḥ tat ca na anyatra aśakteḥ tatra eva śakteḥ bīja ādīnām iva na hi samartham iti eva kāraṇam sarvam tulya jātīyam janayati ekasmāt eva sarva tulya jātīya kārya utpatti prasaṅgāt atha matam artha kriyāsu bhedena viniyogāt bheda madhyavasyāmaḥ 
[53,i^4_54,i]	dadhne hi payaḥ viniyujyate na sikatā iti tat api anaikāntikam eka tve api bhedena viniyoga darśanāt tat eva artha vastu sahakāri sametam viniyujyate na kevalam atha matam bhinnam eva tat sahakāri sannidhāna upādhi bhedāt aupādhikaḥ tarhi pratyaya mātra niveśī bhedaḥ na paramārthataḥ tathābhūtaḥ ca bhāva bhedaḥ hi anujñāyate eva yaḥ api kṣaṇika tvena bhedam āha tasya api bhedasya tulya tvāt sarvam sarvatra viniyujyate na vā kiñcid kvacid adṛṣṭa sāmarthya tvāt atha kalpanā viṣayāt abhedāt tad siddhiḥ parasya api tādṛśāt bhedāt iti na viśeṣaḥ iti uktam yaḥ api ekasya ubhayam pratijānīte bhedam abhedam ca tena ekatra api viruddha dharma āveśam abhyupayatā durlabhaḥ eva dadhnaḥ janakatvā janaka tvābhyām tila payasoḥ vibhāgaḥ iti tat evam ekasya eva eṣa mahimā bheda saṃpādana asahaḥ vahneḥ iva yadā bhāva bheda kalpaḥ tadā mudhā 
[54,ii^1]	ekatra kriyā bheda upalabdheḥ asaṃbhavasya ca asiddheḥ adṛṣṭa darśanasya ca abheda bādhane sāmarthya abhāvāt viśeṣa mātra hetu tvāt tasya ca tattva anya tvābhyām anirvācyasya kalpanā āspada tvāt abhedāt iva ca tādṛśāt kārya abhedasya bhedāt api tadvidhāt bhedasya upapatteḥ virodhasya ca anaikāntika tvāt asiddha tvāt vā vyavasthāyāḥ ca viniyoga bhedasya ca anaikāntika tvāt abhedāt iva ca kalpitāt bhedāt tad siddheḥ bheda abhedayoḥ ca ekatra samavāye śakti aśaktyoḥ viniyoga aviniyogayoḥ ca eka samavāya saṃbhavāt ekasya eva eṣa kaḥ api acintyaḥ sāmarthya atiśayaḥ nikhila bheda prapañca saṃpādanāyai prabhuḥ pāvakasya iva pāka ploṣa ādi pravibhāga nimittam yadā upapadyate tadā bheda kalpanamakāraṇam ekasmāt api tad siddheḥ iti pūrva upasaṃhāraḥ tat etat ṛcā abhyanūktam etāvān asya mahimā iti 
[54,ii^2]	etat parimāṇam asya sāmarthyam yat ekaḥ api sahasra śīrṣā iti yat bhūtam yat ca bhavyam iti pūrvarc dvaya nirdiṣṭa vividha viruddha abhimata dharma kārya vyavahāra āśrayaḥ katham iti atas pratyakṣa abhimatāt puruṣaḥ eva idam sarvam iti vā adṛṣṭa nirdiṣṭāt uta amṛta tvasya iti vā deva manuṣya loka bhedena prapañcāt ekā ekasmāt samastāt ca vṛddhataraḥ puruṣaḥ tena asmin parimitānām viruddha abhimatānām api anante na samāveśaḥ na yujyate tat eva jyāyaḥ tvam darśayati pādaḥ asya viśvā iti kṛtsnaḥ api tāvat bhūta prapañcaḥ asya kanīyān bhāgaḥ iti kim punar pratyekam tathā hi tripād iva aparimitam anantam maraṇa ādi bhūta prapañca dharma śūnyam rūpam divi pradyota avasthāyām vartate pramoda avasthāyām vā sūrya maṇḍale dyusthāne vā tatra hi tad upāsyam tat hi tasya upalabdhi sthānam iti tatra iti ucyate 
[55,i]	aparaḥ kalpaḥ kalpite api kārya bheda ādi avasthāyāḥ vā kāraṇa bhede kim iti na kārya antaram kim iti vā na saṃkaraḥ viparītā vā vyavasthā bhede api payasaḥ tilebhyaḥ eva tailam na sikatābhyaḥ bhinā api ca eka kāryāḥ cakṣuḥ āloka ādayaḥ śara śṛṅga ādayaḥ ca bhede api ca tilebhyaḥ tailam payasaḥ dadhi na tu payasaḥ tailam tilebhyaḥ dadhi yadi matam acintyebhyaḥ bhāva sāmarthyebhyaḥ acintya anupapattitaḥ bhāva sāmarthyāni kasmāt katham iti kārya darśana unneya vyavasthāni tebhyaḥ kāryasya bhedaḥ vyavasthā na viparyayaḥ ca iti yadi evam ekasya eva saḥ astu sāmarthya atiśayaḥ yat anekam vyavasthitam aviparītam ca kāryam tanmātreṇa tad siddheḥ aprāmāṇikāḥ bhāvānām bhāva kalpanā iti 
[55,ii]	syāt etat vahneḥ api śakti bheda nibandhanaḥ kārya bhedaḥ tat na ekasmāt anekam kāryam tatra yadi vahniḥ api kāraṇam katham na ekasmāt anekam kāryam atha śaktīnām eva kāraṇa tvam abhipraiti tatra ucyate yathā eva bhinna śaktīnām abhinnam rūpam āśrayaḥ tathā nānā kriyā hetu rūpam kim na abhyupeyate 
[56,i^1]	ekasya aneka kārya yoga virodhāt śakti bhedaḥ kalpyate yadi ca ekasya aneka saṃbandha virodhaḥ katham nānā bhūtābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ ekaḥ saṃbadhyate tatra yathā ekasya artha svabhāvasya nānā śakti yogaḥ tathā nānā kārya yogaḥ api kim na anujñāyate atha nānā kārya yoge virodhaḥ na nānā śakti yoge viśeṣa hetuḥ vācyaḥ api ca śaktīnām avyatirekāt ekam aneka ātmakam iṣṭam tatra ekatvam sva āśraya samavāyinā aneka tvena ca virudhyate kārya gatena tu āśraya antara samavāyinā virudhyate iti subhāṣitam atha artha antara tvam eva śaktīnām āśraya arthaḥ vācyaḥ 
[56,i^2]	saṃśleṣaḥ ced na bhinna tve rūpa avibhāga lakṣaṇaḥ saṃśleṣaḥ bhedaḥ eva na syāt na nairantaryam tad śakti dravya saṃyuktasya dravya antarasya api tad śakti tva prasaṅgāt na hi dravyasya anantaram tat śakteḥ vyavahitam bhavati na hi cakṣuḥ dravyasya anantaram rūpasya na anantaram vibhu tvāt ca ākāśa ādīnām sarva artha śakti vyavadhāna abhāvāt sarva śakti prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt upakāra viśeṣāt kutaścit āśrayaḥ tatra yathā bhinnāsu śaktiṣu tad bhedāt upakārān bhinnān ekaḥ artha svabhāvaḥ karoti tathā kāryāṇi api iti kasmāt na iṣyate evam tāvat na anumāne api bheda adhigamaḥ na artha āpattyā ca 
[56,ii^1]	ye tu manyante satyam etat na pratyakṣam bheda adhigamāya alam itaretara abhāva aṃśaḥ hi bhāvānām bhedaḥ na saḥ akṣa gocaraḥ bhāva aṃśena eva saṃyogaḥ yogya tvāt indriyasya hi tathā ca na liṅga gamyaḥ api adṛṣṭa saṃgati tvāt arthāpattiḥ api kārya vyavasthā hetukā syāt sā asiddhe bhede vyavasthāyāḥ eva anupapatteḥ tatra ayuktā tasmāt sat upalambha hetubhyaḥ pramāṇa antaram eva abhāvāya upāsanīyam vidhāyakāt vā pramāṇa antaram eva vyavacchedakam abhāva ākhyam tad nibandhanā hi bhāvānām asaṃkīrṇa tā yat avocan vastu asaṃkara siddhiḥ ca tad prāmāṇya samāśrayā iti tān pratyucyate anyonya saṃśrayāt bhedaḥ na pramā antara sādhanaḥ 
[56,ii^2]	na asmin ayam na ayamayam iti bhedāt vinā na dhīḥ na khalu yat vyavacchidyate yatas ca vyavacchidyate tayoḥ apratipattau vyavaccheda gatiḥ na anapekṣita viṣaya niṣedhyaḥ niṣedhaḥ asti san vā śūnyatām āpādayet na bhedam iti uktam teṣām api vacaḥ gṛhītvā vastu sadbhāvam smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam mānasam na astita ajñānam jāyate akṣa anapekṣayā tayoḥ ca pratipattiḥ yadi na asaṃkīrṇa svabhāvayoḥ api tu vastu mātra tvena vyavacchedya vyavaccheda a adhi vibhāga abhāvāt na niṣedha saṃbhavaḥ artha mātre hi avibhāge viṣaya tvena apekṣite na niṣedhyam niṣedhya tvena apekṣite na viṣaya viśeṣaḥ tatra atyantāya niṣedhaḥ syāt sa ca na siddha tvena asiddhatvena vā yujyate iti uktam 
[56,ii^3]	kasyacid tāvat kutaścid bheda pratipattau sarvasya sarvatas bheda gatiḥ syāt aviśeṣāt tasmāt anena asaṃkīrṇa svabhāvena bhinnau eva pratipadya viṣaya niṣedhyau na idam iha na ayamayam iti vyavacchedaḥ pratipattavyaḥ saṃbhavān niyamāt ca na ca anyathā pratiyogi tvam sāmānya upalabdhau ca sthāṇau puruṣasya abhāva pratipatti abhāvāt tathā ca siddha viṣaya niṣedhya aṅgīkaraṇena vyavaccheda mātra vidhāyinya bhāva pratipattiḥ pratyātmam upalakṣyate tathā ca itaretara āśraya tvam asaṃkara pūrvam abhāva jñānam tatas ca asaṃkara siddhiḥ iti api ca na pramāṇa anutpāda mātrāt abhāva jñānam suṣupta ādau anutpatteḥ tasmāt satsu pramāṇa kāraṇeṣu pramāṇān utpādaḥ abhāva jñāna hetuḥ iṣṭaḥ 
[56,ii^4]	na ca tasya svarūpa bhedaḥ kaścid yena sāmarthya atiśayāt cakṣuḥ ādi vat bodhakaḥ kim tu na antarīyaka tvāt na antareṇa prameya abhāvam satsu pramāṇa hetuṣu pramāṇa an utpādaḥ asatsu tu sati api prameye tad abhāvāt syāt iti tathā ca liṅga vat jñāna apekṣaḥ pratipatteḥ janakaḥ sa ca yadi vastu antara jñānam na asiddhe vastu bhede sidhyati jñeya bheda anumeyaḥ hi jñeya anumeyānām jñānānām bhedaḥ tathā ca vastu bheda siddhi pūrvikā eva abhāvāt bhedau agatiḥ iti itaretara āśraya tvam atha ātmanaḥ apariṇāmaḥ na sa stimita avasthā sarva apratipattau kasyacid abhāvasya anavagateḥ tasmāt sati api vastu antara jñāna rūpa pariṇāme tad jñāna rūpa pariṇāma abhāvaḥ abhāva jñāna hetuḥ na ca eṣa viśeṣaḥ prāk vastu bheda siddheḥ sidhyati iti tat eva itaretara āśraya tvam 
[58,i_58,iii]	ye tu āhuḥ darśanāt eva bhāvānām bhedaḥ sidhyati tathā hi nirvikalpasya pratyakṣasya sāmānya viṣaya tvam apākurvata uktam tat ayuktam pratidravyam bhinna rūpa upalambhanāt iti yaḥ tu saṃyogāt samavāyāt vā saṃkaraḥ saḥ abhāva ākhyena pramāṇena apanīyate iti te prāk eva pratyuktāḥ ye api vidhāyaka pratyakṣa puraḥsaram pratyakṣa antaram eva vastu grahaṇa pratiyogi smaraṇa iti kartavyatā anugṛhīta akṣa pratilabdha janma vyavacchedakam manyante yathā eva sa vikalpasya vastu grahaṇasya paścāt janma śabda smaraṇa vyavadhiḥ ca na ca anaindriyaka tvam itikartavya tā viśeṣa anugṛhītāt indriyāt tad utpatteḥ evam na asti iti api jñānasya iti bruvantaḥ tān pratīdam eva vaktavyam anyonya saṃśrayāt bhedaḥ na pramā antara sādhanaḥ pratyakṣa antara sādhanaḥ iti arthaḥ ayam asau na bhavati iti jñānam pratyakṣam vā pramāṇa antaram vā sarvathā viṣaya niṣedhya vibhāgāt ṛte na niṣedha saṃbhavaḥ iti kim ca mīyamāna eka rūpeṣu na niṣedhaḥ avakāśavān 
[58,iv^1]	api ca sat mātra rūpe sarvatra pratīyamāne tad svabhāveṣu vastuṣu na itara abhimataḥ itara abhimata pramāṇa anutpādaḥ sat svabhāva tvāt tayoḥ sat iti ca sarvatra pramāṇa sadbhāvāt pramāṇa abhāvāt ca itaretara abhāva jñānam iti nanu na arthānām kiñcid abhinnam rūpam pratyabhijñānāt hi tat avagamyate na ca artha mātram dṛṣṭavataḥ artha antare saḥ eva ayam iti pratyabhijñā asti yathā ekām gām dṛṣṭavataḥ gavā antare sat śabda pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ tu pācaka ādi vat yoga nibandhanā pramāṇa viṣayaḥ hi san iti ucyate na etat sāram na ced abhinna rūpa pratipattiḥ nirviṣaya tvam eva pramāṇasya āpadyeta yatas na vyavacchedam antareṇa bheda pratītiḥ na vyavacchedaḥ kevalaḥ na vidhi sahitaḥ na vidheḥ paścāt pramāṇasya vyāpāraḥ na vidhiḥ eva vyavacchedaḥ iti varṇitam tatra yadi ekam api na gamyate nirviṣaya tā eva syāt apratyabhijñānam ca yadi go vailakṣaṇyāt ucyeta sati api sat mātra rūpa anugame gavā antare api tat na syāt devadatta vailakṣaṇyāt 
[58,iv^2]	na hi yādṛśaḥ devadattasya punar darśane eka tva pratyayaḥ tādṛśaḥ gavā antare atha asti tatra tāvat pūrva apara anusandhānam na tu sataḥ sat antare kim ca bhoḥ anusandhānāt eka tvam na abhinna rūpa saṃvidaḥ na idānīm abhinna deśa kālaḥ arthaḥ ekaḥ syāt deśa kāla bhede hi saḥ ayam iti pūrva apara anusaṃdhānam go maṇḍale ca mahiṣa maṇḍala vilakṣaṇe deśa bhede api abhinna rūpa anugatāt prathamāt eva nirvikalpakāt pratyayāt eka artha pratipattiḥ iṣyate na ca tatra kāla bheda abhāvāt saḥ ayam iti avamarśaḥ yathā uktam nirvikalpaka bodhe api dvi ātmakasya api vastunaḥ grahaṇam lakṣaṇa ākhyeyam jñātrā śuddham tu gṛhyate na ca yathā maṇikam dṛṣṭavataḥ maṇikā antare anusandhiḥ tathā śarāvam dṛṣṭvā tatra mṛd jātiḥ api apahnūyeta atha asti tatra api na tu yathā maṇikā antare sāmānya rūpāṇām bhūyastvāt utkaṭaḥ alpa sāmānya anugamāt sat antare api tathā eva syāt vistareṇa ca etat upariṣṭāt abhidhāsyate iti alam ati prasaṅgena bheda abheda avabhāse dve vijñāne ced parīkṣyatām 
[59,i^1]	yadi matam vidyete tāvat anuvṛtta vyāvṛtta ābhe dve vijñāne na hi tayoḥ abhāve anuvṛtta vyāvṛtta vyavahāra saṃbhavaḥ na ca vijñāna rūpāt anyaḥ artha vyavasthā hetuḥ tasya ahetu tve abhedaḥ api na sidhyet na etat sāram na hi vijñānam iti eva artham vyavasthāpayati tat api hi parīkṣyam yuktyā virudhyate na iti pramāṇa uttham na iti na khalu alāta cakra ādi vijñānebhyaḥ artha tattva vyavasthā syāt etat na pratyakṣam yuktyā apabādhyate satyam pratyakṣa tā eva bheda jñānasya na iti āveditam yathā kṣepīyassarva todij saṃyoga kāritasya alāta cakra jñānasya 
[59,i^2]	tat sat api apramāṇa uttham pratyakṣa sarūpam svapna dṛśya alāta cakra ādi jñāna vat na tattva avagama nimittam nanu uktena prakāreṇa pramāṇāt anyatas api bheda jñānasya udayaḥ na saṃbhavati kaḥ vā anyathā āha na hi paramārthataḥ bheda avagamaḥ asti yadi syāt katham bhedaḥ apahnūyeta apahnave vā katham tad avagamaḥ na avagamyam asti avagamyate ca iti durghaṭam kim tarhi idam avidyā vibhramaḥ yathā avabhāsam vedya sadbhāve ca na vibhramaḥ kim tu samyak jñānam asataḥ ca avagamaḥ anupapannaḥ tasmāt na paramārthataḥ sattvena nirucyate na api asattvena loke siddha tvāt sarva pravādeṣu iti uktam 
[60,i^1]	api ca jñāna dvaye asmin catasraḥ kalpanāḥ saṃbhavanti jñāna bhedāt sāmānya vyakti vibhāgena vastu dvayam yathā āhuḥ saṃsarga vādinaḥ ekam vā sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakam vastu yathā āhuḥ anekānta vādinaḥ viśeṣāḥ eva vā vastūni teṣām ātyantika bheda niścaya asāmarthyāt tad upādānaḥ tad viṣayaḥ eva abhedaḥ kalpanā jñāna gocaraḥ dṛṣṭā hi bhinneṣu abheda kalpanā vanam iti yathā āhuḥ ātyantika bheda vādinaḥ abhedaḥ vā parama arthaḥ tasya anavacchinnasya anantasya tathā niścetum aśakteḥ anādi tvāt ca avidyāyāḥ tad upādānāḥ tad viṣayāḥ bheda parikalpanāḥ dṛṣṭā hi taraṅga bhedāt abhinne candramasi bheda kalpanā tat na aparīkṣya tattva niścayaḥ tatra parīkṣāyām na tāvat dvayam aikātmya prakhyānān avakalpanāt samavāya kṛtam tat ced na bhedasya aparicyuteḥ na tāvat dve vastunī sāmānya viśeṣau prakhyā bhedāt samāna adhikaraṇa tvena hi ime prakhye jāyete san ghaṭaḥ gauḥ svastimatī iti 
[60,i^2]	na vyadhikaraṇa tvena yathā nīla pīta prakhye yathā vā daṇḍaḥ devadattaḥ iti na api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvena yathā daṇḍī iti saṃbandhasya apratibhāsanāt na ca vastu bheda viṣaya tve sāmānādhikaraṇyam avakalpate sati api saṃbandhe saṃbandhi dvayam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tvena dvābhyām ekayā vā buddhyā gṛhyate na tu paraspara ātma tvena paraspara ātma tvena ca iha pratipattiḥ pratyātma vedanīyā vipratipatteḥ ca sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ bhede na anyathā vipratipadyeran sāmānya pratyakṣe ca viśeṣa pratyakṣa abhimānāt anyathā dhūma dṛṣṭau iva agnau parokṣa abhimānaḥ syāt syāt etat na saṃbandha mātrāt bheda pratipattiḥ api tu saṃbandha viśeṣāt samavāyāt sa hi vastu saṃśleṣa ātmakaḥ tat na samavāye api tābhyām rūpa bhedasya anapāyāt anyathā bheda abhāvāt asaṃbandhāt tathā ca na aikātmyena prakhyā yujyate asti ca iyam atas tayā viruddhaḥ prakhyā bhedaḥ na vastu bheda vyavasthāyai prabhavati svayam vā vyāhata tvāt eka adhikaraṇa tvena utpatteḥ 
[61,i]	nanu bhede api paraspara ātma tvena pratipatteḥ nimittam samavāyaḥ tasya khalu eṣa sāmarthya atiśayaḥ yena bhedavatām arthānām bhedam tirodadhāti tathā ca te abhedena prakāśante atra ucyate bheda antardhāna sāmarthyam tasya bhede api ced matam hanta ekasya eva tat kim na yat evam avabhāsate samavāya sāmarthyāt ced bhedavatā urabhedavatā urabheda avabhāsaḥ hanta ekasya eva vastunaḥ sāmarthya viśeṣāt nānā avabhāsaḥ abhyupeyatām vyarthāḥ vastu bheda kalpanā na hi asti viśeṣaḥ yatas bhinnayoḥ abheda prakāśa saṃbhavaḥ na ekasya nānā avabhāsa saṃbhavaḥ iti 
[61,ii]	nanu jvalana ayaḥ guḍa ādiṣu dṛṣṭam evaṃvidham saṃsargasya sāmarthyam tatra darśanāt saṃbhavī saṃsargāt bheda vat sva bheda avabhāsaḥ na ekasmin nāna avabhāsaḥ adarśanāt ucyate dṛṣṭaḥ saṃsarga dharmaḥ ayam yadi ekam api vai tathā nānā avabhāsate citram rūpam ekam tathā matiḥ dṛṣṭam khalu ekam api vividha avabhāsam yathā citram rūpam tat hi khalu na nīla ādi samāhāra mātram teṣām avayava samavāye rūpa antara anabhyupagame ca avayavinaḥ nīrūpa tva prasaṅgāt na ca nīrūpa tvam eva āvayavinaḥ rūpa saṃskāra abhāve hi na sa cākṣuṣaḥ syāt na ca rūpi samavāyāt saṃkhyā karma ādi vat cākṣuṣa tvam evam hi uktam mahati aneka dravya samavāyāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti sarvaḥ ca ittham avayavī nīrūpaḥ syāt atha na arūpaḥ pratīyate iti na ayam prasaṅgaḥ citraḥ api tathā iti na arūpaḥ tat ca asya rūpam nīla pīta ādi nirbhāsaḥ tathā nagara trailokya ādi buddhayaḥ vividha viṣaya ākārāḥ nirbhāsante bheda abhāve api iti viṣaya ākāra jñāna vādinaḥ manyante na ca eka buddhi tattva avyatirekāt viṣaya ākārāḥ parasparataḥ api vyāvartante prāk eva buddheḥ 
[62,i]	syāt etat citram api rūpam saṃsargāt eva eka artha samaveta samavāya lakṣaṇāt tathā avabhāsate tat asat yatas na ca saṃbandhi saṃbandhaḥ saṃsargaḥ vyavadhānataḥ saṃśleṣaḥ hi saṃsargaḥ tatas ca paraspara rūpa avabhāsaḥ sa ca avyavadhāne yujyate na tu sva āśrayābhyām vyavadhāne avayava avayavi rūpayoḥ eka vyavadhāne api asaṃśleṣaḥ kimu dvaya vyavadhāne 
[62,ii]	kim ca vyavahāre para upādhau sarvā dhīḥ vyāvahārikī ayathārthāḥ yadā bhāva bheda kalpaḥ tadā mudhā yasya khalu śuklaḥ gauḥ ityādi buddhayaḥ vyavahāra aṅga bhūtāḥ dravyeṣu guṇa jāti upādhi nibandhanāḥ tasya etāḥ na yathāvastu jāti guṇa dravyāṇām anyonyam artha antara tvāt tathā ca na vastu nibandhanaḥ vyavahāraḥ buddhyā anupadarśitasya avyavahāra aṅgavāt buddhi upadarśitasya ca tathā abhāvāt evam ca pratyaya viracitena eva ayam arthena vyāvṛttaḥ vyavahāraḥ anuvṛttaḥ ca iti vyarthāḥ vastu bheda kalpanā kalpitasya api tasya vyavahāre anupayogāt itarasya ca upayogāt yathārtha tvāya hi vyāvahārikīṇām buddhīnām vastu bhedaḥ kalpyate kalpite ca tasmin para upādhi tvāt tāsām na ayathārtha tva parihāraḥ 
[62,iii_63,i]	syāt etat asati vastu bhede ayathārtham api anuvṛtta vyāvṛtta avagraham vyāvahārikam vijñānam na udetum arhati bīja abhāvāt na khalu sthāṇu śakala ādiṣu puruṣa rajata ādi vibhrāntayaḥ nirbījāḥ sāmānya nibandhana tvāt ucyate ayathārtha dhiyaḥ bījam avaśyam bāhyam eva na dṛṣṭaḥ timirakāma ādiḥ āntaraḥ api hi upaplavaḥ na viṣaya doṣāt eva sādṛśya ādeḥ ayathārtha jñānam ādhyātmikebhyaḥ api tu doṣebhyaḥ timira kāma śoka ādibhyaḥ tatra asati vastu bhedaḥ ādhyātmikaḥ doṣaḥ avidyā lakṣaṇaḥ vyāvahārika jñāna bījam iti na arthaḥ vastu bhedena 
[63,ii]	astu tarhi ekam dvi ātmakam evam hi paraspara ātma pratipattiḥ ca sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ kalpate vastu viparītaḥ ca na artha sāmarthya atiśayaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ vastu nibandhanaḥ vyavahāraḥ na vyāvahārika jñānānām ayathārthā vṛttiḥ syāt etat ekasya dvi ātmaka tā virodhavatī ekam ca dvi ātmakam ca iti vipratiṣiddham api ca sāmānyam bheda antara anuyāyi tatas vyāvṛtta svabhāvaḥ bhedaḥ tayoḥ ekatvam hi virodhāt aśakyāvaham na etat sāram viruddham iti naḥ kva saṃpratyayaḥ yad pramāṇa viparyayeṇa vartate yat tu yathā pramāṇena avagamyate tasya tathā abhāve viruddha tva abhidhāne kam bata ayam āśritya hetum viruddha tva aviruddha tve vyavasthāpayet pramāṇam ca ekasya sāmānya viśeṣa ātmaka tām avagamayati vyāvṛtti anuvṛttibhyām prakhyā rūpa bhedāt sāmāna adhikaraṇyā avagamāt ca tat idam asāṃpratam yatas na īdṛśām vipratiṣiddha artha jñānānām prāmāṇyam eva yujyate saṃśaya jñāna vat anyathā saṃśaya viṣayaḥ api dvi ātmā syāt dvi ābhāsa tvāt tasya sāmāna adhikaraṇyāt ca tad avabhāsayoḥ 
[63,iii]	atha matam na saṃśayite rūpa samuccaya avagamaḥ yathā sāmānya viśeṣavati ayam vā ayam vā iti pratīteḥ mā bhūt samuccayaḥ vikalpaḥ syāt saḥ api na vastunaḥ vikalpa anupapatteḥ ekam api tarhi na dvi ātmakam ekasya dvi ātmaka tā virodhāt tatra yathā saṃśaya jñānam vipratiṣedhāt apramāṇam tathā sāmānya viśeṣa pratipattiḥ api aika adhikaraṇyāt 
[63,iv]	syāt etat na saṃśaya jñānam vipratiṣedhāt apramāṇam nirṇaya jñānena tu bādhanāt yatra tarhi na nirṇayaḥ tatra vikalpa ātma tā syāt api ca yathā bādhāyām ekasya aprāmāṇyam nirākaraṇāt evam virodhe api dvayoḥ ekasya vā jñānasya viruddha rūpa upagrahe tad rūpa adhigatyoḥ anyonya nirākaraṇāt tatra eka nirākaraṇe itarasmāt niścayaḥ paraspara nirākṛtau tulya bala tve sandehaḥ iti na saṃśaya jñānāt ekasya sāmānya viśeṣa pratipattiḥ viśiṣyate tasmāt iha ana ekāntikam vastu iti evam jñānam su niścitam iti sva pakṣa upavarṇanam 
[64,i]	api ca eka tvam avirodhena bheda sāmānyayoḥ yadi na dvi ātma tā bhavet ekatara nirbhakta bhāga vat avaśyam anena padārthānām bheda abhedau vyavasthāpayatā yathā tāvat sāmānyam abhinnam viśeṣāḥ bhidyante iti bheda abhedayoḥ lakṣaṇam vācyam tatra rūpa virodhaḥ anyonya abhāvaḥ bheda lakṣaṇam viparyayaḥ abheda lakṣaṇam rūpa virodhāt hi anyonya abhāva paryāyāt viśeṣāḥ bhidyante bhidyamāneṣu api teṣu sāmānyam abhinnam viparyayāt tatra sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ yadi sva rūpa virodhaḥ anyonya abhāvaḥ na ekatvam bhedānām iva parasparam atha sāmānya viśeṣa buddhi eḥ aika ādhikaraṇyena utpatteḥ svarūpa virodhaḥ abhyupeyate na tarhi ekam dvi ātmakam sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ sva rūpa virodha abhāvāt asati bhede dvi tva anupapatteḥ yathā na sāmānya aṃśaḥ dvi rūpaḥ viśeṣa aṃśaḥ vā rūpa virodha abhāvāt tatra ekasmin nirbhakte dvi tva abhāvāt tathā sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ api sāmānādhikaraṇya buddheḥ yadi na rūpa virodhaḥ na paraspara ātma abhāvaḥ dvi tvam na yujyate atha rūpa virodhaḥ na ekatvam iti 
[64,ii^1]	yadi matam na sva rūpa virodhāt nānātvam tad abhāvāt ca eka tvam yena sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ sva rūpa virodha abhāvāt dvi tvam na syāt anyatarasya iva bhāgasya kim tu buddhe rūpa bheda abhedābhyām sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ ca paraspara ātma tvena pratipatteḥ asati api anyonya abhāva lakṣaṇe sva rūpa virodhe buddhe rūpa bhedāt dvi tvam aṃśe tu rūpa abhedāt eka tvam atas vastunaḥ dvi rūpa buddhi grāhya tvāt dvi ātma tā iti tatra ucyate aikātmya buddheḥ bhāge ced evam vastuni tarhi asau na ced kutastyam eka tvam asti ced dvi ātma tā katham yadi tarhi buddheḥ eka rūpa upagrāhi tvāt abhedom aśasya vastu vicāryam tatra api buddhiḥ kim eka rūpa upagrāhiṇī na vā iti 
[64,ii^2]	tatra yadi na eka rūpa upagrāhiṇī vastuni buddhiḥ sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakam hi vastu tad dvi rūpa buddhi upagrāhyam katham ekatvam vastunaḥ buddhi rūpā bhedasya abheda lakṣaṇasya abhāvāt rūpa bhedasya ca bheda lakṣaṇasya bhāvāt atha eka rūpa upagrāhiṇi eva vastuni buddhiḥ na dvi ātmaka tvam aṃśa vat eva atha matam buddhi rūpa bhedaḥ paraspara ātma abhāvaḥ ca bheda lakṣaṇam tatra gavā ādayaḥ bhedāḥ bhinna rūpa buddhi upagrāhyāḥ parasparān ātmānaḥ ca na tu sāmānya viśeṣau buddhi rūpa bhede api paraspara ātma tvena pratipatteḥ evam api sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ bheda lakṣaṇena virahāt na dvi ātma tā aṃśa vat iti uktam 
[65,i]	yadi manyeta buddhi rūpa abhedaḥ paraspara ātma pratipattiḥ ca dve abheda lakṣaṇe tatra aṃśasya rūpa abhedāt eka tvam ubhayoḥ tu paraspara ātma tva pratīteḥ viśeṣāṇām tu na buddhe rūpa avibhāgaḥ na paraspara ātma pratipattiḥ iti bhinnāḥ iti evam api abheda lakṣaṇe sati paraspara ātma pratipattau ubhaya abhāve ca bheda lakṣaṇe avidyamāne na dvi ātma tā na ca ekasya abhedasya dve lakṣaṇe yujyete lakṣaṇa abhedaḥ hi abhedam vyavasthāpayati tad bhedaḥ ca bhedam lakṣaṇa bhede api ced tattvam anya tvam ca lakṣaṇa abhede api yadi vyartha tā eva lakṣaṇasya syāt iti 
[65,ii^1]	api ca sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ abhede buddhi antarasya vaiyarthyam eka aṃśaḥ iva ca āpatet nānā tvāt arthavattā ced eka tvāt vyartha tā na kim buddhi antara pravṛttiḥ eva sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ eka vastu ātma tām apākaroti sā hi nānā ātma tve bhedeṣu iva arthavatī anadhigata adhigamāt eka tve tu yathā sāmānya viśeṣa vibhāgayoḥ sva buddhi samadhi gatayoḥ na vilakṣaṇam buddhi antaram arthyate tathā sāmānya buddheḥ na buddhi antaram vilakṣaṇam viśeṣa adhigamāya prārthyeta tathā viśeṣa buddheḥ na sāmānya adhigamāya atha na atyantam avyatirekaḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ vyatirekaḥ api tu tatra vyatirekāt arthavat tā iti tat asat evam api kutas etat vyatirekāt arthavat tvam bheda vat na punar avyatirekāt eka aṃśa vat vaiyarthyam 
[65,ii^2]	tulyayoḥ hi bheda abhedayoḥ kutas etat bhedāt ekayā buddhyā na grahaṇam na punar abhedāt grahaṇam iti buddhi antara vaiyarthyam autsargikaḥ ca hetu abhāve phala abhāvaḥ svabhāva siddhaḥ tasya hetu bhāve phala bhāvaḥ apavādaḥ tatra abhede hetu bhāvāt ekayā eva buddhyā ubhaya adhigamaḥ yuktaḥ na ekatve anyatara adhigama hetuḥ na asti iti śakyam vaktum atha api kathañcid nā asti iti ucyeta tathā api asti tāvat eka tvāt tatra hetu bhāvāt phala bhāvaḥ syāt tasya kāraṇa tvāt na tu abhāvaḥ abhāvasya kāraṇam svabhāva siddhaḥ tu abhāvaḥ phalasya tasya hetu nibandhanaḥ phala bhāvaḥ nivartakaḥ sa ca hetuḥ ubhayatra asti tāvat asattvam tu anupayogam akāraṇa tvāt iti 
[66,i^1]	api ca sāmānyam na hi vastu ātmā na bhedaḥ citraḥ eva saḥ tasyānanvayataḥ bheda vādaḥ śabda antara āt ayam yasya ekam ubhaya ātmakam vastu na tasya sāmānya mātram vastunaḥ ātmā na viśeṣa mātram tanmātra tve vastu bheda prasaṅgāt tasmāt saṃbhinna ubhaya rūpaḥ śabalaḥ vastu ātmā na ca śabalasya anyatra anugamaḥ yasya tu anugamaḥ sa vastu rūpam na bhavati tathā ca śabda antaram avalambya bhedāḥ eva satyāḥ iti etat pratipādyate śabda antareṇa vā hetunā dvi ātmakam ekam iti anuganturavastu svabhāva tve kalpanā viṣaya tvāt syāt etat mā bhūt vastu tad aṃśa tvam tu na vāryate 
[66,i^2]	anyathā nirbījā kalpanā api na bhavet kaḥ punar ayam aṃśaḥ nāma na tāvat vastu eva tanmātra rūpa tve vastunaḥ bheda prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam na api vastunaḥ anyat svayam vastu sāmānya viśeṣa tadvatām trayāṇām vastūnām prasaṅgāt atha na vastu eva na anyat svayam vastu pariśeṣāt kalpanā viṣayaḥ tattva anya tva abhyām anirvacanīyaḥ nanu na aṃśom aśinaḥ artha antaram na api saḥ eva ubhayathānaṃśa tvāt na api avastu atas eva na hi khapuṣpam kasyacid aṃśaḥ bhavati tatra aṃśa anugame vastu eva anugatam bhavati tasya tat avyatirekāt na etat sāram ananugamāt aṃśa antarasya kim na vastunaḥ ananugamaḥ 
[66,i^3]	api tu ananugamaḥ eva tasya samudāya ātmaka tvāt eka abhāve api abhāvāt tathā hi itaretara apekṣau vā sāmānya viśeṣau vastu tad samāhāraḥ vā ubhayathārtha antare viśeṣasya abhāvāt na vastu anvayaḥ pratyekam anapekṣayoḥ vastu tve na ubhaya ātmakam ekam vastu syāt iti suṣṭhu ucyate tasyānanvayataḥ bheda vādaḥ śabda antara āt ayam iti yadi vā akhila bhāvānām abhedāt tat atattvataḥ abheda vāda āśrayaṇam syāt anyavidhayā girā aṃśa anuvṛttyā vā vastu anugame advaita vādaḥ tathā hi gauḥ svatas tāvat gauḥ sat dravya ādi rūpa anugamāt aśva vastunaḥ anugamāt aśvaḥ 
[66,i^4]	tat evam gauḥ gauḥ ca aśvaḥ ca aśvaḥ api tāvat aśvaḥ sat dravya ādi rūpa anugamena go vastunaḥ anvayāt gauḥ tat evam aśvaḥ api aśvaḥ gauḥ ca tat evam sarva bhāvānām tad bhāvāni abhāvābhyām abhedaḥ iti advaitam jagat iti uktam anya prakārayā vācā satyam dvaitam api asti yatas tad bhāvāni abhāvābhyām a bhedaḥ na etat sāram gauḥ api ced aśvaḥ gauḥ ca aśvaḥ ca tad kutas anya tvam gauḥ aśvaḥ iti api bheda abhidhānam anibandhanam eva siddhe hi gavāśvabhede etat upapadyate gavāśvasya tu pratyekam gavāśva tve bheda abhāvāt anibandhanam eva tat nanu viśeṣa aṃśānām vyāvṛtteḥ anyatva siddhiḥ 
[66,i^5]	tathā ca dvaitādvaita ātmakam jagat iti atha viśeṣa vyāvṛtteḥ anya tva siddhiḥ kim ubhaya rūpa tvāt vastunaḥ vastu antare anugamaḥ na asti aśvavastu go vastu na bhavati atha asti anugamaḥ aśvaḥ api gauḥ bhavati tatra pūrvasmin kalpe vastunaḥ ananvayāt anuyataḥ ca avastu tvāt bheda vādaḥ iti uktam atha viśeṣa vyāvṛttau api tad vastu anugatam bhavati aśvaḥ gauḥ kutas anyatva siddhiḥ yadi matam anugatam ca ananugatam ca aśve go vastu bhavati ca aśvaḥ gauḥ gauḥ tu gauḥ eva bhavati eva hi tatra go vastu tatas anyatva siddhiḥ iti atha go vastu katham vaktavyam 
[66,i^6]	kim yat gauḥ bhavati eva atha yat na bhavati api tatra pūrvasyām kalpanāyām na vastunaḥ anugamaḥ iti ananvitāni vastūni dvitīyasyām vastunaḥ vastu antare anvayāt advaitam sarvathā yena viśeṣeṇa ayam aśvāt govastu vyavasthāpayati anyat tad viśeṣa yujaḥ tu tasya ananvayāt bheda vādaḥ atha ananvaya doṣāt na viśeṣam āśrayati abheda vādaḥ iti na dvaita advaita kalpanā upapadyate iti dravya paryāya arthakānām nayaḥ etena vāritaḥ teṣām api dravya nayaḥ paryāyanayaḥ eva vā ye ca dravyam nityam mṛd suvarṇa ādi tasya ghaṭa rucaka ādayaḥ paryāyāḥ viśeṣa ākhyāḥ apāyinaḥ upāyinaḥ ca avyatirekāḥ 
[66,i^7]	na ca te dravyam eva tasya sthitimat tvāt na ca tatas atyantam vyāvartante bhedena anupalabdheḥ dravyasya eva rucaka ādi rūpeṇa pratyayāt evam dravya paryāya rūpam vastu atha tu dravyam eva syāt vardhamānaka bhaṅgena rucaka kriyāyām na kiñcid utpannam naṣṭam vā iti prīti śokau tad arthinoḥ na syātām atha tu paryāya mātram hema arthinaḥ madhyastha tā na syāt paryāya mātre hi hemni hemnaḥ vināśāt paryāya vināśe katham madhyastha tā utpāde vā tasmāt dravya paryāya rūpa tvāt vastunaḥ utpatti sthiti bhaṅgānām ekatra saṃbhavāt dravya rūpa sthiteḥ mādhyasthyam paryāyayoḥ utpatti vināśābhyām prīti śokau avakalpete iti manyante 
[66,i^8]	tat nītiḥ api anena eva nirākṛtā prakāreṇa tathā hi teṣām api vastunaḥ vastu antara anvaye api bhāga abhāvāt dravya mātram syāt atha na vastu anveti dravya paryāya rūpa tvāt vastunaḥ paryāya antare ca paryāya antarasya ananugamādananvitāni tarhi vyāvṛtta svabhāvāni vastūni yasya anugamaḥ kalpyate tanmātra rūpasya avastu tvāt paryāya mātram avasthitam hi dravyam ucyate na ca evam avasthitam kiñcid ekam vastu asti vastunaḥ tu apoddhṛtasya aṃśasya avasthāna kalpanā kalpanā eva vastunaḥ citra tvāt tasya ca atathā bhāvāt iti 
[68,i^1]	api ca utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām ekatra samavāyataḥ prīti madhya stha tā aśokāḥ syuḥ naḥ syuḥ iti durghaṭam yasya khalu dravyāt paryāyāḥ bhidyante tasya dravya mātra arthinaḥ dravyasya sthiteḥ vināśa abhāvāt apūrvasya anutpādāt madhyastha tā rucaka arthinaḥ tasya apūrvasya utpatteḥ prītiḥ vardhamānaka arthinaḥ tasya vināśāt śokaḥ iti vyavasthā kalpate yasya tu na paryāyebhyaḥ ananyat dravyam na dravyāt anye paryāyāḥ tasya utpatti sthiti bhaṅgānām ekatra samavāye dravya arthinaḥ madhyastha tā bhavet na bhavet ca prīti śokau syātām na syātām na hi tat dravyam avatiṣṭhate eva vinaśyati apūrvam ca utpadyate tatra vināśāt apūrva utpatteḥ ca prīti śokau syātām na madhyastha tā madhyastha tā ca sthiteḥ syāt iti durghaṭam āpadyeta tathā vardhamānaka arthinaḥ tad nāśāt śokaḥ syāt na ca syāt sthiteḥ 
[68,i^2]	prītiḥ ca tasya apūrvasya utpādāt syāt na ca bhavet pūrvasya eva sthiteḥ vināśāt ca śokaḥ syāt iti atha bhedaḥ api asti iti na ayam doṣaḥ abhedaḥ api asti iti kim na bhavati atha na atyantam abhedaḥ tena na saṃkaraḥ na atyantam abhedaḥ iti vyavasthā api na yujyate na ca asya kiñcid kvacid ekāntataḥ sarvatra anekāntam abhyupayataḥ yena ayam viśeṣaḥ ucyate na atyantam abhedaḥ iti asaṃkaraḥ iti tathā ca na ekāntaḥ sarva bhāvānām yadi sarva vidhānataḥ apravṛtti nivṛtti idam prāptam sarvatra hī jagat yadā hi sarva prakāreṣu anaikāntika tvam bhāvānām tathā sati na ayam lokaḥ kvacid abhimata sādhana tā prakāram avadhārya pravarteta yatas na asau tathā eva na api nivarteta yatas na asā avatathā eva tathā duḥkha hetoḥ na nivarteta na asau tathā eva na api na nivarteta yatas na asā avatathā eva iti kaṣṭām bata daśām āpadyeta 
[69,i_70,i]	atha vā yat uktam prīti madhya stha tā aśokāḥ syuḥ naḥ syuḥ iti durghaṭam iti tatra brūyuḥ sarva vastuṣu sarva prakārāṇām anaikāntika tvāt kā durghaṭa tā tathā hi prīti madhya stha tā aśokāḥ na ekāntataḥ santi na ekāntataḥ na santi iti atra ucyate na ekāntaḥ sarva bhāvānām iti yadi khalu prīti ādīnām sat asat tve na aikāntike na prīti arthī prīti sādhaneṣu pravarteta prīteḥ vidyamāna tvāt na api na pravarteta tasyāḥ abhāvāt tathā duḥkha nivṛtti arthī na duḥkha sādhana saṃparkam pariharet tasya asattvāt na api na pariharet tasya sattvāt iti apravṛtti nivṛttikam bata viśvam āpannam iti evam tāvat na dve vastunī na ekam dvi ātmakam tatra dvayam avaśiṣyate bhedaḥ satyaḥ tad upādāna abheda kalpanā abhedaḥ vā satyaḥ tad upādānāḥ bheda kalpanā iti tatra āpekṣika tvāt bhedaḥ hi bheda graha purassaraḥ na eka jñānam samīkṣya ekam na bhedam tattva hānataḥ 
[70,ii]	na bhedam upādāya abheda kalpanā kutas āpekṣikaḥ hi bhedaḥ na anyam anapekṣya śakyate grahītum na ca agṛhītaḥ bhedaḥ abheda kalpanāyāḥ upādānam bhavati para apekṣa tve ca asya grahaṇam anupapannam yatas na agṛhīte bhede para ātmānau vyavatiṣṭhete na ca para ātma vyavasthām antareṇa bheda grahaḥ asti iti prāc prapañcitam na tu evam abheda grahaṇam abheda grahaṇa apekṣam na api bheda grahaṇa apekṣam abheda hāna prasaṅgāt na hi bhede gṛhīte abhedasya avakāśaḥ asti tatra abhedam gṛhītvā tam upādāya tasya yathāvat niścaya aśaktau vyavaccheda kalpanā upapadyate yathā eka buddhi nirgrāhyeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu avayava vibhāga kalpanā na tatra bheda upādāna abheda kalpanā bhedaḥ hi paramāṇuṣu vyavatiṣṭhate te ca atīndriyāḥ nanu ca eka tvam api anusandhāna pratyaya avaseyam sa ca na bhedam antareṇa bheda asparśe hi kim kena anusandhīyatām iti pratyuktam etat na idānīm abhinna deśa kālaḥ arthaḥ ekaḥ syāt asati ca ekasmin kim āśrayā bheda āśaṅkā syāt yasya anusaṃdhānāt eka tvam ucyate iti 
[70,iii]	api ca sarva pratyātma vedanīyam etat abheda upādānaḥ bhedaḥ iti tathā hi ālocyate vastu mātram jñānena āpāta janmanā acetyamānaḥ bhedaḥ api cakāsti iti ati sāhasam vastu mātra viṣayam prathamam avikalpakam pratyakṣam tad pūrvāstu vikalpa buddhayaḥ viśeṣān avagāhantaḥ iti sarva pratyātma vedanīyam syāt etat viśiṣṭa rūpa upagrāhyā iva pratyakṣam sa tu bhedaḥ śabdena asaṃsparśāt na tathā upalakṣyate yathā vikalpa buddhau tat ayuktam vipratiṣedhāt na ca upalakṣyate pratyakṣa buddhau viśeṣaḥ prakāśate ca iti vipratiṣiddham atas atisāhasam ucyate yaḥ tu saṃvittau eva vipratipadyate sarvān ātma vyāvṛtta spaṣṭa pratibhāsam pratyakṣam iti vadan tasya uttaram āhuḥ vidhātṛ pratyakṣam ityādi uktam eva iti 
[71,i]	kim ca pratiṣṭhitam ca vijñānam artha mātra avalambanam bhedeṣu tu apratiṣṭha tvam asti indriya dhiyām api vastu dvaya anupapatteḥ ekasya ca dvi ātma tā yogāt avaśya kalpanīye anyatarasya mithyātve yuktam viśeṣa avabhāsasya mithyātvam rajata ādi vibhrāntiṣu darśanāt na ca vastu mātra avabhāsasya na hi vastu mātra vyabhicāraḥ kvacid jñāne dṛṣṭaḥ asti antatas tasya eva vastunaḥ pratibhāsanāt dṛṣṭa tad bhāvasya eva tad kalpanā laghvī kḷpta tvāt yogyatāyāḥ itaratra tu kalpya tvāt syāt etat mānasyaḥ eva buddhayaḥ kḷpta yogya bhāvāḥ mithyātvam prati na indriya janmānaḥ indriya buddhi samadhigamyāḥ ca bhedāḥ iti etat ca vārtam indriya doṣa anuvidhāyi tvāt bhrāntīnām iti 
[71,ii]	api ca yasya matam vyāvṛtta sva lakṣaṇāḥ bhāvāḥ tena te anyonya abhāva svabhāvāḥ vyākartavyāḥ tad viśeṣaṇā vā na anyathā vyāvṛtta śabdaḥ arthavān bhavati tasya itaretara abhāva nimitta tvāt tatra anyonya abhāva rūpa tvam sarveṣām na prakalpate tatra upādhau pratīyantām tathā bhinnā na rūpataḥ ekasmin anapekṣe sthite tad abhāva rūpaḥ anyaḥ vyavatiṣṭhate sarve tu na anyonya abhāva rūpāḥ kalpante paraspara āśraya sthiti tvāt atha viśeṣaṇam anyonya abhāvaḥ kāmam atada ātmānaḥ api viśeṣaṇa anurāgāt tathā avagamyantām na tu svabhāva bhedaḥ syāt nanu na anyonyābhāvaḥ nāma kaścid yaḥ bhāvānām tattvam viśeṣaṇam vā syāt artha siddhiḥ eva eṣā na ced anyonya abhāvaḥ kaścid siddhaḥ tarhi abheda iti 
[72,i]	api ca bheda tvāt eva viśvasya bhedaḥ abheda upādānaḥ iti śakyate anumātum dṛṣṭaḥ hi maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādiṣu abhinna mukha upādānaḥ tad bhedaḥ na ca tatra bhāva antara utpattiḥ viruddha pariṇāma tvāt syāt etat abhedaḥ api śakyaḥ bheda upādānaḥ anumātum vanābhedasya taru bheda upādāna tvāt na bheda abhāva prasaṅgāt evam hi na kaścid ekaḥ abhinnaḥ paramāṇuḥ api tad abhedaḥ api hi bheda upādānaḥ syāt vana ādi vat tathā tad aṃśa abhedaḥ api iti anavasthāyām ekasya abhāvāt tat samuccaya rūpaḥ abhedaḥ na syāt atha kvacid avatiṣṭhate saḥ ekaḥ tad abhedaḥ na bheda upādānaḥ iti vyabhicāraḥ tat idam ucyate daparṇa ādau mukhasya iva bhedaḥ abheda avalambanaḥ bheda avalambanaḥ abhedaḥ na tathā tad abhāvataḥ 
[72,ii]	api ca pratyekam anuviddha tvāt abhedena mṛṣā mataḥ bhedaḥ yathā taraṅgāṇām bhedāt bhedaḥ kalāvataḥ abheda anuviddha tvāt pratyekam viśvasya bhedaḥ mṛṣā yathā jala taraṅgeṣu candramasaḥ tatra hi pratyekam candramāḥ iti abheda anvayaḥ tathā viśvasya bhede api pratyekam idam tat arthaḥ vastu iti abheda anvayaḥ taru bhedaḥ tu yadi api na mṛṣā vanam iti abheda anugamaḥ ca na pratyekam na hi pratyekam taruṣu vanam iti buddhiḥ atas na tena vyabhicāraḥ etad artham ca pratyekam iti uktam 
[72,iii^1]	api ca ekasya eva astu mahimā yat nānā iva prakāśate lāghavāt na tu bhinnānām yat caka asati abhinna vat idam tāvat ayam bheda vādī praṣṭavyaḥ katham ayam vyāvṛtta sva lakṣaṇeṣu abheda avabhāsaḥ anuvṛtta vyavahāraḥ ca yadi sādṛśyāt tat atyantam ananviteṣu anupapannam atha vyāvṛtteḥ agrahāt kaḥ hi guñjā pravāla ādīnām rāga vyāvṛttim avagrahītum kṣamate iti tat asat vyāvṛtta svabhāvasya tat agrahe grahaṇam eva hi na syāt atha niścaya pratyakṣayoḥ ātma bhedāt aniścayāt tat asat ubhaya rūpa vyavahāra darśanāt tathā hi kāla akṣyām go sāmāni anibandhanaḥ ca vyavahāraḥ gavā antara vyāvṛttiḥ ca dṛśyate na ca gavā antara vyāvṛtteḥ aniścaye sa yujyate atha eka artha kriyā kāri tvāt atad kriyā vyāvṛtteḥ tulya tvāt 
[72,iii^2]	tat api asāṃpratam artha kriyāṇām api bhedāt atad kriyā vyāvṛtteḥ tulya tva ayogāt na eka sādhya anyasya artha kriyā yena atad kāri vyāvṛttiḥ tulyā syāt vastu svabhāvaḥ ca vyāvṛttiḥ prativastu bhedāt na tulyā atha asvabhāvāḥ teṣām katham tulyā atha anādi vāsanā upādānaḥ na vastu gata viśeṣa apekṣaḥ tat api ayuktam niyamāt kāsucid eva hi vyaktiṣu kaścid eva avabhāsaḥ sa vāsanā mātra upādāna tve na yujyate tasmāt prakṛtyā eva kecid kasyacid abheda avamarśasya yogyāḥ kecid na iti svabhāva viparītāḥ bhāvānām sāmarthya atiśayā kalpayitavyāḥ tathā sati evam gauravāt kalpanāyāḥ ekasya eva astu māhātmyam yat ekaḥ api na anā iva avabhāsate laghu tvāt kalpanāyāḥ na tu bhinnānām te sāmarthya atiśayāḥ yat amī abhinnāḥ iva bhāsante 
[73,i_73,ii]	bheda vyavahāraḥ ca yathā avabhāsam bheda vādinām iva abheda vyavahāraḥ upapadyate tathā hi ātyantika bheda vādinām yathā avabhāsam abheda vyavahāraḥ na yathāvastu saṃsarga vādinām api sāmānyasya arthasya artha antara tvāt yatha avabhāsam eva bhedeṣu abheda vyavahāraḥ ye api anartha antara vādinaḥ teṣām api śabala tvāt vastunaḥ tasya ca ananvayāt yathā avabhāsam eva ubhaya vyavahāraḥ na vastu anupāti iti darśitam iti yathā anuvṛtta vyavahāra siddhim yathā avabhāsam kathayanti bāhyāḥ tathā eva bheda vyavahāra yogam vadanti vedānta viveka bhājaḥ 
[74,i^1]	evam pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt karma vidhi virodhāt ca śruta artha parigrahe ye manyante vedāntānām upacarita artha tvam tad pratibodhanāya vihitaḥ prayatnaḥ saṃprati tu kāryaḥ eva arthe vedasya prāmāṇyam na bhūta rūpe evam hi uktam codanā lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ dharmaḥ codanā pramāṇakaḥ veda arthaḥ iti yāvat codanā ca pravartakam vacanam tasmāt kārye arthe vedaḥ pramāṇam vedāntānām api tu pratipatti kartavya tā pramāṇa bhājām tad mukhena tad anugata bhūta ātma tattva viṣaya bodhaka tvam atas te api kārya niṣṭhatām na ativartante 
[74,i^2]	tathā ca katham tarhi mantra artha vādāḥ sa upaniṣatkāḥ iti āśaṅkya codanā hi bhūtam bhavantam iti ādi uktam etat uktam bhavati kāryam artham avagamayantī codanā eva bhūtādikam api artham avagamayati iti ye manyante tad pratibodhanāya prayatyate tisraḥ ca pratipattayaḥ brahmaṇi prathamā tāvat śabdāt anyā śabdāt pratipadya tad santānavatī dhyāna bhāvanā upāsana ādi śabda vācyā anyā tatas labdha niṣpattiḥ vigalita nikhila vikalpā sākṣātkaraṇa rūpā tatra prathamām adhikṛtya ucyate śabdāt yat ātma vijñānam tat na tāvat vidhīyate bhavati adhīta vedasya tat hi karma avabodha vat 
[74,ii]	brahmaṇaḥ hi pramāṇa antara anadhi gamanīya rūpa tvāt śabda adhigamya svabhāva viṣayam jñānam vidheyam tatra yat śabdāt eva jñānam tat avidheyam vidhim antareṇa bhāvāt karma avabodha vat yathā eva svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti śruta vākyasya vākya artha avabodhaḥ tad vākya prāmāṇyāt eva bhavati na vidhi antaram apekṣate tathā ātma svarūpa abhidhāyi vākya prāmāṇyāt ātmā avabodhaḥ vidhi anapekṣaḥ saṃjāyate sati pramāṇe tad sāmarthyena eva prameya bodha utpatteḥ na khalu sa upakaraṇe samagre pramāṇe sati icchā api puruṣasya apekṣyate jñānam prati aniṣṭānām api avabodhāt prāk eva vidhiḥ 
[75,i]	tām eva vidheḥ anapekṣa tām karma avabodhe darśayati svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti bodhe asmin na vyapekṣyate vidhiḥ anyaḥ anavasthānāt na ayam karma vyavasthiteḥ na karma vidhi vākya artha jñāna pravṛttau vidhiḥ apekṣyate anyaḥ na tad gataḥ eva vā anyasmin anavasthā doṣāt tad artha jñāne api vidhi antarasya apekṣaṇīya tvāt tad gatasya ca karma viṣaya tvena tad bodham vidhātum asāmarthyāt 
[75,ii^1]	nanu yathā eṣām grahaṇe vidhi antaram apekṣyate svādhyāyaḥ adhyetavyaḥ iti na ca anavasthā tadvat tad artha bodhe api syāt asti ca vidhiḥ vedaḥ kṛtsnaḥ adhigantavyaḥ iti viṣamaḥ upanyāsaḥ apravṛttaḥ api hi svādhyāya adhyayana vidhi vākya adhyayane puruṣa antara adhītāt tatas tasya ca anyeṣām ca vākyānām adhyayane pravartate śākhā antarīya aṅga upasaṃhāraḥ iva śravaṇa mātrāt na khalu svādhītam eva vākyam pravartayati yathā ekaḥ tathā puruṣa antarāṇi api anādi tvāt veda vat tat adhyayanasya api anavabuddha arthaḥ tu avabodha vidhiḥ na avabodhe pravartayati tad artha bodhaḥ ced vidhi apekṣaḥ na tatra saḥ eva pravartayati anavabuddha artha tvāt itaretara āśrayam syāt tad artha bodhāt pravṛttiḥ pravṛttasya ca tad artha bodhaḥ iti 
[75,ii^2]	tasmāt vidhi antaram apekṣitavyam iti anavasthā na ca vedaḥ kṛtsnaḥ adhigantavyaḥ iti apūrva artha vidhiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam iti nyāya prāptaḥ arthaḥ pradarśyate atha api eṣa vidhiḥ svādhyāya adhyayana vidhinā artha ākṣiptam artha jñānam na ucyeta tathā api brahma svarūpa abhidhāyi veda vākya prabhave bodhe na pṛthagvidhiḥ apekṣitavyaḥ karma vidhi vākya vat yathā eva svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti sāmānya vidhinā siddhe na anyaḥ apekṣyate anavasthānāt sati api vidhau anyasya apekṣaṇāt na ca etat gataḥ eva karma viṣaya tvāt evam tattva pratipatti pareṣu api vākyeṣu na vidhiḥ apekṣitavyaḥ vākya sāmarthyāt eva tattva bodha utpādāt iti 
[76,i]	itas ca phalam vidheya avagamāt pravṛttiḥ ca uttarā vidheḥ anyonya saṃśrayāt na eṣa śābdaḥ bodhaḥ sa no paraḥ śabdāt avagamya vidheyam yā pravṛttiḥ sā vidheḥ prayojanam na tu śabda prabhavaḥ vidheya avagamaḥ eva anyonya saṃśrayāt avagate śabda arthe pravṛtteḥ pravṛttasya ca avagamāt śabda artha bodhāt eva vā śabda artha bodhaḥ iti ātma āśrayaḥ anyonya saṃśrayaḥ tu tulya anupapatti tvāt uktaḥ yaḥ tu tattva avabodha parāt vākyāt tattva avabodhaḥ na asau śabda artha bodhāt parācīnaḥ kintu saḥ eva iti 
[76,ii]	api ca jāte bodhe na pravartyaḥ natarām khalva bodhake śabde na niścaye tasmāt anyasmāt anya vāñchanam udapādi ced sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti upakramāt tat tvam asi iti antāt vākyāt ātma tattva avabodhaḥ padānām paraspara anvitā artha tvāt kim anyat vidhiḥ kariṣyati na pravṛttaḥ eva pravartyaḥ atha padārtha samanvaya mātrāt na tattva bodha utpādaḥ suta rām apravartyaḥ śābdasya tattva avabodhasya asaṃbhavāt syāt etat utpanne api tattva avabhāse śabdāt niścaye pravartyaḥ evam idam iti tat na yadi tasmāt śabdān niścayaḥ sa jātaḥ eva atha anyatas niścayaḥ anyavāñchanam pramāṇa antara apekṣā na tatra tattva niścaya nibandhanam śabdaḥ syāt evam tāvat na tattva niścayāya vidhiḥ arthyate 
[76,iii_77,i]	atha avivakṣita artha tva nivṛttyai prārthyate vidhiḥ arthaḥ jñātavyaḥ iti ukte jñeyaḥ syāt na avivakṣitaḥ yat api matam sati api vākyāt artha upaplave tātparyam durlabham bhūta artha parasya vaiyarthyāt sāṃśayika tvam vā atātparyasya api darśanāt japa mantreṣu vidhau tu satyartha jñānasya codita tvāt na arthaḥ avivakṣitaḥ bhavitum arhati tasmāt vivakṣita artha tvāya vidhiḥ prārthyaḥ 
[77,ii]	tat vārtam artha para tā śabdānām loka vedayoḥ aviśiṣṭaḥ tu vākya arthaḥ iti utsargavatī yatas autsargikaḥ śabdānām artham prati śeṣa bhāvaḥ nimitta antarāt tu sva rūpa pradhāna tvam avivakṣita artha tvam apavādaḥ loke tathā vede api lokau agamya tvāt śabda sāmarthyasya tat uktam aviśiṣṭaḥ tu vākya arthaḥ iti 
[77,iii]	dṛṣṭa artha tā ca svādhyāya vidheḥ atra na bhidyate bhavet itarathā kṛtsnaḥ sa vidhi arthaḥ avivakṣitaḥ yathā eva karma vidhīnām dṛṣṭaḥ hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam iti na avivakṣita arthānām adhyayanāt phala antara kalpanā tathā dṛṣṭa tvāt ātma tattva avabodhasya vedāntānām na ca bhūta artha pratipattau vaiyarthyam iti vakṣyate pratipatti vidhau ca tulyam avaśyam ca etat evam vijñeyam anyathā saha vidhāyakena kṛtsnasya avivakṣita artha tā syāt yatas vidhāyaka śabda nibandhanam anyeṣām vivakṣita artha tvam vidhāyakasya tu na tad nibandhanam asti evam ca tasya avivakṣita artha tve itare api tathā syuḥ atha vidhāyakaḥ prakṛtyā dṛṣṭa artha tvena ca artha paraḥ itare api tathā iti vyarthaḥ asau vidhiḥ 
[77,iv_77,v]	jñānasya puruṣa artha tva siddhaye vidhiḥ iṣyate sarvatra puruṣa artha tvam vidheḥ iti api apeśalam vidhi adhīnaḥ puruṣa artha sādhana tā avabodhaḥ tad śabdataḥ labdha janmanaḥ api ātma tattva avabodhasya puruṣa artha sādhanatva avagamaḥ vidheḥ iti etat api na śobhanam jñeya abhivyāptitaḥ yasmāt na vijñānāt phala antaram iṣyate mokṣaḥ iti ced sādhyaḥ tattva cyuteḥ na saḥ 
[78,i]	jñānasya hi dṛṣṭam eva phalam jñātrā jñeyā abhivyāptiḥ jñātāram prati tasya prakāśanam na tu adṛṣṭam kāla antara bhāvi yad arthaḥ vidhiḥ syāt syāt etat ātma jñānasya phala antaram api iṣyate mokṣaḥ tat na asādhya tvāt na hetu janyaḥ asau mokṣaḥ tattva cyuteḥ kāryatve vināśāt tasya punar saṃsārāt ātyantikī ca saṃsāra nivṛttiḥ mokṣaḥ iti ucyate nanu kāryaḥ api nāśaḥ na naśyati satyam bhāva rūpam tu mokṣam niratiśaya ānanda lakṣaṇam niratiśaya aiśvarya lakṣaṇam ca abhipretya etat ucyate bhāvasya kāryasya vināśena āvinā abhāvāt āgāmi śarīra indriya buddhi saṃyoga abhāvasya prāgabhāvasya kārya tvam anupapannam eva bandha hetu nivṛttiḥ tu yadi api kāryā kāryatve api ca na asyāḥ anitya tva prasaṅgaḥ tathā api na asau tattva jñānāt pṛthak iti na tena sādhyā avidyā hi bandha hetuḥ tattva jñāna udayaḥ eva ca tad nivṛttiḥ 
[78,ii]	athavā param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa avatiṣṭhate iti svarūpa sthitiḥ muktiḥ uktā sādhya tve ca na svarūpa sthitiḥ syāt atas mokṣa tvāt cyaveta yat tu na sa punar āvartate iti śruteḥ prāmāṇyāt kāryasya api mokṣasya nitya tvam iti dṛṣṭa viparītam api tadā aśrīyeta ananya gati tve śruteḥ yadā tu vidita ātma tattvasya advayam viśuddha prakāśam ātmānam paśyataḥ samutkhātāyām anavayavena avidyāyām hetu abhāvāt punar bandhasya asaṃbhāvya tvāt prāptam eva artham vartamāna apadeśāt anuvadati śrutiḥ artha vāda tvena tadā kutas tad prāmāṇyāt ananta phala tvam tathā hi vartamāna apadeśāt eva na apunarāvṛttiḥ sādhya tvena avagamyate na ca kāma upabandhaḥ asti yatas sādhya tā gamyeta tasmāt artha vādaḥ arthavādāt api ca yā phala kalpanā sā api jñāne jñeya tattva avabhāsa dṛṣṭa phala nirākāṅkṣe anupapannā puruṣa artha tā ca asya vakṣyate iti 
[78,iii]	anye punar āhuḥ vidheḥ vinā kārya śūnyam bhūta artham anuvādakam vacaḥ syāt anuvādaḥ ca pramāṇa antara gocare tad pramāṇa antara apekṣam prāmāṇyam ativartate māna antarasya aviṣaye vidhi arthe tu pratiṣṭhitam anapekṣam pramāṇa tvam aśnute karma vākya vat para pravṛtti abhāve api prāmāṇyāya eva tad vidhiḥ vidhim antareṇa na kārya upadeśa pratītiḥ yathā avasthitam vastu tadvidhasya anuvāda mātra tvam gamyate anuvādaḥ ca pramāṇa antara viṣayaḥ iti tad apekṣaḥ bhūta arthaḥ na arthaḥ ucyate iti sa apekṣa tvāt aprāmāṇyam vidhi arthasya tu pramāṇa antara aviṣaya tvāt tad niṣṭham anapekṣam pramāṇam karma vidhi vākya vat pramāṇa antara aviṣayaḥ ca vidhi arthaḥ na hi kuru iti śabda jñānāt anyatas pratītiḥ evam ca sati tattva pratipatti pare vākye yadi api vākya artha bodhāt parācīnā pravṛttiḥ vidhi phalam na asti prāmāṇyāya eva tu vidhi niṣṭha tvam eṣitavyam iti 
[79,i]	atra ucyate pramāṇa antara yātā artha bhāvaḥ kim anuvāda tā uta bhūtārtha tā tatra siddhārtham api yat vacaḥ na māna antara labdha artha tayā tasya avabodhakam na tad sāpekṣam eṣā ced abhipreta anuvādatā kaḥ punar anuvādaḥ adhigama antara saṃbhinna artha tvam māna antareṇa adhigataḥ iti pratipādanam āhosvit bhūtārtha tā mātram tatra pūrvasmin kalpe bhavatu adhigama antara saṃbhinna artham sa apekṣam yat tu bhūta artham api na māna antara adhigataḥ iti bodhayati na tad anuvādakam na sa apekṣam pūrva adhigama saṃsparśena pratipatteḥ abhāvāt 
[79,ii]	atha aparaḥ kalpaḥ sa apekṣatāyāḥ kaḥ hetuḥ śuddhā siddhārtha tā yadi pramāṇa antara saṃbhedaḥ tad vyapekṣaṇa kāraṇam anṛdhī prabhave na asti bhūta arthe api sa vaidike bhūta artha mātram ced anuvāda tā na sa apekṣa tva hetuḥ asti na bhūtārtha tā eva sa apekṣa tva hetuḥ bhūta arthayoḥ api pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ anapekṣa tvāt tasmāt bhūta arthe abhūta arthe vā adhigama antara saṃsparśaḥ pramāṇa antara apekṣā hetuḥ smṛtau darśanāt sā hi adhigama antara saṃbhinna artha iti tad sādhanam apekṣate evam ca puruṣa buddhi prabhavam bhūta artham abhūta artham vā vacaḥ bhavati sa apekṣam tatas hi tad saṃbhinnaḥ eva arthe pratyayaḥ na tu anapekṣita pūrva adhigamaḥ svātantryeṇa arthe yathā uktam api ca pauruṣeyāt vacanāt evam ayam puruṣaḥ vedaḥ iti bhavati pratyayaḥ na evam arthaḥ iti apuruṣa buddhi prabhava tvāt veda vacasi bhūta arthe api na sa apekṣa tva hetuḥ puruṣa saṃbandha kṛta tvāt pūrva adhigama saṃbhedasya 
[80,i^1]	syāt etat apauruṣeye api bhūta arthe tad viṣaye pramāṇa antarasya saṃbhavāt tad apekṣā tathā hi saṃbhavati pramāṇa antare tad viṣaye tad visaṃvādaḥ api śaṅkyeta tasmāt tad abhāvāya tad saṃvādaḥ apekṣaṇīyaḥ asaṃbhavati tu kārye arthe na kutaścid visaṃvāda āśaṅkā iti na apekṣyam asti atra ucyate na ca saṃbhava mātreṇa tad apekṣau akalpate viśeṣaḥ na hi gamyeta sa apekṣa tve tadā tayoḥ dvayoḥ eka viṣaya saṃbhave kutas etat śabdaḥ tad apekṣaḥ na punar tad pramāṇa antaram śabda apekṣam syāt iti yadi śabdaḥ pramāṇa antara adhigata viṣayaḥ loke dṛṣṭaḥ iti pramāṇa antarasya aviṣaye tarhi natarām prāmāṇyam tasya bhavati pramāṇa antara viṣaye hi pramāṇa antara saṃbhavāt api tāvat syāt anyatra tad abhāvāt durlabham tat 
[80,i^2]	atha pauruṣeya tva kāritā loka vacasām pramāṇa antara adhigata artha tā na śabda sāmarthya kāri tā śabdasya pramāṇa antara asaṃbhinnaḥ eva arthe sāmarthyam na tarhi pramāṇa antara saṃbhavāt śabdaḥ eva sa apekṣaḥ tat api śabda saṃbhavāt śabda apekṣam syāt kim atas tasya sa apekṣa tvena apramāṇam syāt na śabdasya tatra apekṣā yujyate sati hi tasya prāmāṇye tad saṃvāda visaṃvādau apekṣyeyātām atha śabdasya aprāmāṇyāt na tat śabda apekṣayā pramāṇam pramāṇam eva anapekṣa tvāt śabdasya aprāmāṇyam kutas pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt tasya ca prāmāṇyam anapekṣa tvāt anapekṣa tvam ca śabdasya aprāmāṇyāt itaretara āśrayam pramāṇe hi śabde tad viṣaye saṃbhavati tat api sa apekṣam syāt tad saṃbhavaḥ iva śabdaḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt atha śabda saṃbhave api na tad sāpekṣam tad saṃbhave api na śabdasya sa apekṣatā viśeṣa abhāvāt 
[81,i^1]	api ca pratyakṣa anumayoḥ evam vṛtteḥ anyonya gocare paraspara vyapekṣa tvam aviśeṣam prasajyate syāt akṣam api sa apekṣam yat akṣa antara gocare saṃbhava mātreṇa sa apekṣa tve pratyakṣa anumayoḥ ekasmin viṣaye saṃbhavāt anyonya apekṣa tvāt aprāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ tathā sattā guṇa tva dravyeṣu aneka indriya grāhyeṣu indriya antarāṇām indriya antara sāpekṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ atha śabdasya eva pramāṇa antara saṃbhave sa apekṣa tvam viśeṣa hetuḥ vācyaḥ pramāṇa antara adhi gata artha tva darśanāt iti ced uktam atra yadi śabda mātra dharmaḥ ayam asaṃbhavāt eva tad viṣaye pratyakṣa ādeḥ buddha ādi vākya vat aprāmāṇyam prāpnoti saṃbhave tu indriya viṣaye pratyayita puruṣa vacaḥ vat yujyate prāmāṇyam 
[81,i^2]	yathā uktam tat ced pratyayitāt puruṣāt indriya viṣayam vā avitatham eva tat iti atha pauruṣeya dharmaḥ ayam na saṃbhavat pramāṇa antara viṣayasya api apauruṣeyasya śabdasya sa apekṣa tvam api ca pratyakṣa adhigata viṣayam kiñcid anumānam iti na sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya tathā pratyakṣa sāpekṣatā yathā ca āgama pūrvakam ṣaḍja ādi viveka viṣayam pratyakṣam iti na sarvam pratyakṣam tathā evam puruṣa vacasām pramāṇa antara adhigata viṣaya tva darśane api na apauruṣeyasya tathā abhāvaḥ bhūtārthasya api anyathā sutarām pramāṇa antara asaṃbhavāt aprāmāṇyam syāt iti uktam 
[81,ii^1]	api ca asaṃbhavāt auṣadha ādi niyogasya anapekṣatā laukikasya prasajyeta nara pratyaya pūrvakaḥ viniyogaḥ tatra tena vyapekṣā vaidike punar abuddhi pūrvakaḥ saḥ api iti anapekṣa tvam ucyate yadi kārye niyoga arthe pramāṇa antarasya asaṃbhavāt veda vacasām tad niṣṭhānām anapekṣa tvam jvara viyoga kāmaḥ idam auṣadham pibet svarga kāmaḥ sikatā bhakṣayet iti loka vacāṃsi api kārya niṣṭhāni anapekṣāṇi prāmāṇyam aśnu vīran atha yaḥ tatra sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ sa puruṣa vivakṣā pūrvakaḥ tena tatra sa apekṣatā vede tu sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ api na puruṣa vivakṣā pūrvakaḥ iti anapekṣa tvam 
[81,ii^2]	yaḥ vā viṣaya niyojya niyogānām saṃbandhaḥ sa puruṣa buddhi viracitaḥ loka vākye vede tu kevalam niyogaḥ apuruṣa buddhi pūrvakaḥ saḥ api iti anapekṣa tvam ucyate nṛ buddhi pūrvatā eva ittham hanta apekṣā nibandhanam māna antara asaṃbhave api tatra sa apekṣatā yatas asaṃbhavat pramāṇa antara kārya niṣṭhe api ced vākye puruṣa saṃbandhāt sa apekṣa tvam puruṣa buddhi pūrva tā eva tarhi pramāṇa antara vyapekṣā kāraṇam anvaya vyatirekābhyām tad bhāve loke sa apekṣa tvāt tad abhāve vede nirapekṣa tvāt na viṣaye pramāṇa antara saṃbhavaḥ tad abhāve api loka niyoge sa apekṣa tva darśanāt 
[82,i]	atha matam vede niyoga niṣṭha tvam viniyoga pradhāna tā loke vede na vyapekṣā tat loke ca vyapekṣaṇam niyoga paryavasitam vaidikam vacaḥ sa ca pramāṇa antarasya agocaraḥ iti anapekṣa tvam sādhya sādhana bhāva niṣṭham tu laukikam vacaḥ sa pramāṇa antara viṣayaḥ iti sa apekṣatā na śabda mātra sāmarthya pravibhāgaḥ ayam īdṛśaḥ loka avagata sāmarthyaḥ śabdaḥ vede api bodhakaḥ na tāvat ayam śabda mātrasya anapekṣita puruṣa saṃbandha asaṃbandhasya śakti pravibhāgaḥ yat ekatra niyogaḥ śabda arthaḥ anyatra viniyogaḥ yathā go śabdasya sāsna ādimān aśva śabdasya kesara ādimān yatas loka adhigata sāmarthyaḥ vede api pratipādakaḥ loke ced viniyogaḥ śabda arthaḥ tatra eva asya sāmarthyam adhigatam na niyoge tatra vede api viniyogaḥ eva pramāṇa arthaḥ syāt atha māna antarāt jñātvā prayuṅkte puruṣaḥ vacaḥ arthe tat tena tad niṣṭham itarat tu anyathā sthitam 
[83,i]	atha matam na eṣa śabda mātrasya sāmarthya vibhāgaḥ śabdasya hi nijam sāmarthyam kārya niṣṭhatā eva tathā hi kāryaḥ niyoga arthaḥ kāryāya ca anyasya anvayaḥ pratīyate na tu kāryasya anya arthaḥ anvayaḥ tasmāt kāryatvāt niyogasya tad pradhāna tā puruṣaḥ tu pramāṇa antarāt avagamya artham tatra prayuṅkte vacanam na ca niyogaḥ pramāṇa antara gocaraḥ tasmāt na tatra prayoktum arhati viniyogasya tu tathā abhāvāt tatra yujyate prayogaḥ tasmāt viniyoga pradhānam puruṣa vacaḥ vaidikam tu sāmarthyena kāryatvāt niyogasya tat pradhānam iti 
[83,ii_83,iii]	atra ucyate māna antara vyapekṣa tvāt saṃbhavī anya pramāṇakaḥ hanta asya gocaraḥ na asmāt apekṣā asya pramā antare yadi puruṣaḥ adhigate viṣaye vacaḥ prayuṅkte iti viniyoga viṣaya tā tasya kalpyate pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt tarhi saṃbhavat pramāṇa antaraḥ asya viṣayaḥ na tu saṃbhavat pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvāt puruṣa vacaḥ api sa apekṣam sa apekṣa tva nimitta tvāt tadvidhasya viṣayasya tasmāt māna antarāt gatvā parasya pratipattaye vacaḥ prayuṅkte puruṣaḥ na akasmāt tena tat giri pramāṇa antara saṃbhedaḥ vyapekṣātaḥ na saṃbhavāt 
[83,iv]	sva upalabdhi khyāpanāya puruṣasya gīḥ tatas tasyām pramāṇa antara saṃbhedaḥ mayā upalabdhaḥ ayam arthaḥ iti arthaḥ tena tatra upalabdhe saṃbhava asaṃbhavau eva apekṣyeyātām yatra upalabdheḥ niścayaḥ saṃbhavati asya upalabdhiḥ na ca anupalabhya ayam bravīti iti tatra prāmāṇyam yathā āpta puruṣasya pramāṇa viṣaye yatra tu upalabdheḥ asaṃbhavaḥ eva yathā dṛṣṭa arthe buddha ādi vākye yatra ca anupalabhya api vacana pravṛtti saṃbhāvanā tatra aprāmāṇyāt na tu pramāṇa antara saṃbhavāt puruṣa vacane api tad apekṣā 
[83,v_84,i]	apauruṣeya tā tena pauruṣeya tvam eva ca anapekṣa vyapekṣa tva nimitte varṇite budhaiḥ bhūta artham api sa apekṣam na atas apuruṣa buddhi jam atas eva pauruṣeya tva apauruṣeya tve sa apekṣa tva anapekṣa tva kāraṇe nyāya vidbhiḥ daśite pauruṣeya tva nirākaraṇa prayatnena autpattikaḥ tu śabdasya arthena saṃbandhaḥ iti autpattike śabda artha sambandhe asvātantryāt śabdasya na puruṣa buddhi pūrvakatvam iti na pramāṇa antara saṃbhinnā śabdāt artha avagatiḥ iti nirapekṣa tvam nanu pramāṇa antara asaṃbhave api kṛtaḥ eva yatnaḥ sat saṃprayoge iti satyam codanā eva pramāṇam na anyat iti avadhāraṇa siddhaye na tu pramāṇam eva iti 
[84,ii^1]	atha pramāṇa antara saṃbhave api yadi codanā prāmāṇyam na vyāhanyate kaḥ arthaḥ pramāṇa antara nirākaraṇena dharma tattva jñānam pramāṇa antara saṃbhave hi sarva jña abhimata buddha ādi upadiṣṭaḥ api dharmaḥ pratīyeta tatra na dharma tattvam avadhāritam syāt tad avadhāraṇa arthaḥ ca ayam yatnaḥ codanā prāmāṇyam api tad artham mṛgyate na adṛṣṭāya athavā tad virodhāt codanāyāḥ bādhaḥ syāt saṃśayaḥ vā tulya bala tve tena tasya asaṃbhavaḥ pratipādyate na tu tad saṃbhavāt sa apekṣata iti nanu tad abhāvaḥ apekṣaṇīyaḥ syāt kāmam na tu śabdaḥ pramāṇa antara apekṣam artham pratipādayati yatas yad arthasya pratipādakam na tu tat apekṣyate yat apekṣyate na tad artham pratipādayati 
[84,ii^2_84,iii]	na hi virodhi pramāṇa abhāvaḥ pratipatti hetuḥ virodha saṃbhava mātreṇa ca aprāmāṇye pratyakṣa ādīnām api tat syāt api ca virodhi saṃbhavāt aprāmāṇyam kārya niṣṭha tve api aparihāryam kartavyatā dvāreṇa bhūta artha pratipatteḥ iṣṭa tvāt tatra tu pramāṇa antara virodhi saṃbhāvanāt bhūta arthasya pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvāt tena kārya niṣṭhatā varṇyate pramāṇa antara viṣaya tve kila anuvāda tvāt pramāṇa antara apekṣam artham pratipādayati pramāṇa antareṇa ayam adhigataḥ iti na svātantryeṇa kārya niṣṭha tve tu svātantryeṇa tasya pramāṇa antara agocara tvāt uktena prakāreṇa na sa apekṣa tvam iti bhūta artham api sa apekṣam na atas apuruṣa buddhi jam iti suṣṭhu uktam atha saṃsarga bhājaḥ no padārthāḥ kriyayā vinā kim āyātam vidheḥ sā api tu asti ādiḥ sulabhā kva na 
[85,i]	yadi matam ākhyāta padārtham antareṇa na nāma padārthānām saṃsargaḥ kriyāḥ hi padārtha saṃśleṣa hetuḥ tad abhāve sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt atas siddhaḥ arthaḥ brahmādiḥ na śabda gocaraḥ padasya avidita saṃgati tvena anavabodhaka tvāt na vākya arthaḥ tasya saṃsarga ātmaka tvāt kriyā rahitānām ca padārthānām asaṃsargāt evam api kriyā abhyupeyatām tad dvāreṇa ca padārtha saṃsarga siddhiḥ āśāsyatām na vidheḥ kaścid arthaḥ sā api ca kriyā sarvatra sulabhā eva aśrūyamāṇā api astyādiḥ astiḥ bhavantī paraḥ prathama puruṣaḥ aprayujyamānaḥ api gamyate iti tatra brahma svarūpa pratipatti param vākyam asti artha niṣṭham tad nibandhanaḥ tatra padārtha saṃśleṣaḥ sattāyāḥ ca prakṛtyā eva sat pradhāna tvāt tad dvāreṇa viśiṣṭa vastu siddhiḥ iti 
[85,ii]	atra āhuḥ na pramāṇa avagamya tāyāḥ anyā kācana sattā tathā hi yat pramāṇena avagamyate tatra asti iti vyavahāraḥ laukikānām viparyaye na asti iti na khalu anyaḥ sat asat vibhāga hetuḥ lakṣyate artha kriyā bhāva abhāvau ced na tayoḥ api pramāṇa bhāva abhāva adhīna tvāt tathā hi kārye api sat vyavahāraḥ yadi kārya antara nibandhanaḥ anavasthā tasmāt ante api pramāṇāt eva sat vyavahāraḥ tad viparyayāt ca asat vyavahāraḥ evam ced ādau eva pramāṇa abhāva abhāva nibandhanau sat asat vyavahārau stām tathā ca asti artha niṣṭham vākyam pramāṇa antara apekṣam eva artham bodhayati pramāṇa viṣaya tāyāḥ asti artha tvāt 
[85,iii]	atra ucyate na ca mānau agamya tvam asti iti viṣayaḥ mataḥ mānāt eva yatas buddhiḥ abhūt asti bhaviṣyati dhūma ādinā mite hi syāt vahni ādau iyam anyathā bhidyeta uttara kāle vā bhavantī na khalu tridhā na pramāṇau agamya tvam asti arthaḥ na asti iti buddheḥ tad viṣayaḥ yatas pramāṇāt eva tridhā buddhiḥ bhavati dhūmāt asti atra agniḥ nadī pūra viśeṣāt abhūt vṛṣṭiḥ megha udaya viśeṣāt bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti tatra yadi buddhiḥ pramāṇa viṣaya tām gocarayati pramite hi syāt na pramāṇāt eva na hi prāk pramāṇa utpatteḥ san pramāṇa saṃbandhaḥ pramāṇa saṃbandha nibandhanā ca iyam buddhiḥ atha vaiyātyāt uttara kāla tām eva asyāḥ brūyāt traividhyam anupapannam pramāṇa saṃbandhasya abhedāt bhinna kāleṣu api artheṣu 
[86,i_86,iii]	sva saṃbandhi tayā mānam atha vastu adhigacchati tathā api na eva bhidyeta na ittham ca anya vyapekṣatā atha matam ātma saṃbandhi tayā eva pramāṇena arthaḥ avagamyate atas na asti iti buddheḥ uttara kāla tā pramāṇa saṃbandha viṣayāyāḥ api sva ātma saṃbandhi tayā eva arthasya pratīteḥ evam api asti iti eva sarvatra syāt na traividhyam sarvasya pramitau pramāṇa saṃbandhasya vartamāna tvāt na ca ittham pramāṇa antara vyapekṣa tvam asti artha niṣṭhe vacasi tad pramāṇa saṃbandhasya eva asti artha tvāt anyamānau agamya tvam atha liṅgāt tridhā iṣyate syāt liṅgam api sa apekṣam tad siddheḥ tatas eva ced nairapekṣyam yadi na tat vede daṇḍaiḥ nivāryate 
[86,iv]	atha matam pramāṇa antara gamya tā eva liṅgena adhigamyate tena na uttara kālatā tat ca pramāṇam tri kālam iti traividhyam kim punar tat pratyakṣam tathā hi bhūtāyām dṛṣṭau kasyacid bhūtam pratyakṣam bhaviṣyantyām bhaviṣyat vartamāne agnau vartamānam iti etat ca vārtam nitya anumeye tasya abhāvāt api ca liṅgam api evam pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt apramāṇam syāt atha liṅgāt eva pramāṇa antara sadbhāvasya siddheḥ nirapekṣa tvam tathā hi pramāṇa antara sadbhāvaḥ eva idānīm liṅgam pramāṇam na ca tatra anyat apekṣyate pramāṇa sadbhāva dvārā prameya siddhiḥ iti na ayam vidhiḥ vede daṇḍa vāritaḥ vaidikam api vacaḥ asti artha niṣṭham viśiṣṭa artha pramāṇa sadbhāvaḥ eva pramāṇam tatra nirapekṣam tad pramāṇa dvārā ca viśiṣṭa artha siddhiḥ iti samānam 
[87,i]	tad saṃbhavaḥ alaukika arthe buddha vākya arthavat na tu atra iti sākṣātkaraṇa abhyupāyāt asamañjasam syāt matam yuktam liṅgasya prāmāṇyam evam arthe tasya pramāṇa antarasya saṃbhavāt saṃbhavati hi vṛṣṭi ādiṣu pramāṇa antaram tatas tad dvāra artha gatiḥ na tu sarva viśeṣa atīte brahmaṇi āmnāya eka nibandhane abhyupagamyate tatra yathā eva buddha ādi vākyānām eva m ayam puruṣaḥ vedaḥ iti jñāna niṣṭhānām atīndriya arthe jñānasya asaṃbhavāt na arthe prāmāṇyam atīndriya artha upadeśinām tathā atra api syāt saṃbhavi pramāṇa viṣaya āpta vacana vat tu liṅgasya pramāṇa niṣṭha tve api yujyate prāmāṇyam tat asat brahmaṇi api sākṣātkaraṇasya abhyupagamāt avidyā saṃhāre avidyāvatām tu tadāmnāya eka nibandhanam ucyate
