[87,ii]	api ca meya tvam eva sattā ced māne trividha tā kutas tad saṃbandhāt atas na arthe traividhyam avakalpate yadi ca liṅgena pramāṇam eva mīyate mīyamāna tā eva ca sattā tatra pramīyamāṇa tvāt pramāṇam sarvam sadeva sat ca vartamānam iti ucyate tatra vartamāna tvāt pramāṇasya sarvatra arthe asti iti eva syāt na pramāṇa traividhyāt arthe traividhyam mīyamānasya sattvāt sataḥ ca vartamāna tvāt iti 
[87,iii]	api ca idam ayam praṣṭavyaḥ kim vartamāna pramāṇa yogaḥ pramāṇa saṃbandhaḥ sattā tad viparyayaḥ asattā āhosvit pramāṇa yoga mātram anāśrita kāla viśeṣam tatra vartamāna pramā yogaḥ sattā sattā viparyayaḥ mate yadi tatas prāptam asat tvam smṛti gocare na smaryamāṇasya vartamāna pramāṇa saṃbandhaḥ nanu smaryamāṇe vināśa saṃbhavāt na eva asti iti vyavahāraḥ satyam na asti iti api na asti yadi vartamāna pramāṇa yogaḥ sattā tad viparyayaḥ asattā na asti iti eva syāt na ca asti iti tasmāt anye sat asat tve 
[88,i_88,ii]	pramāṇa yoga mātram ced sattā sattāḥ viparyayaḥ prāptā pramita naṣṭena ghaṭena madhu dhāraṇā pramite ca na jijñāsā punar syāt sada sattvayoḥ anāśrita kāla viśeṣe pramāṇa yoga mātre sattve pramita naṣṭam api vastu sat iti tena artha kriyā prasaṅge anaṣṭena iva sattva aviśeṣāt naṣṭānaṣṭayoḥ viśeṣāt na evam iti ced saḥ eva tarhi viśeṣaḥ sat asat vyavahāra vyavasthāyāḥ hetuḥ kārya vyavasthāyāḥ iva na pramāṇa yogaḥ tad anusāriṇī eva eṣā dṛśyate loke na khalu pramita naṣṭam sat iti upacarati lokaḥ kim ca pramite arthe sat asat tve jijñāseran na punar laukikāḥ siddha tvāt pramāṇa yoga mātrasya tad lakṣaṇa tvāt ca sattvasya atha pramāṇa yogya tvam sattā naṣṭāt ca tat cyutam smaryamāṇe pracalitam kvacid iti api asundaram 
[88,iii]	atha matam na vartamāna pramāṇa yogaḥ sattā nānā āśrita kālam tad yoga mātram api tu pramāṇam prati yogyatā sā ca naṣṭāt cyutā iti na tasya sattva prasaṅgaḥ smaryamāṇe tu kutaścid cyutā kutaścid na iti na sarvasya asattvam iti etat api na sundaram abhyupagata hānāt tathā hi ittham artha svabhāvaḥ eva sattā varṇitā bhavati pramāṇa yogyaḥ artha svabhāvaḥ sattā artha svabhāva nibandhanaḥ eva sat asat vyavahāra vibhāgaḥ na pramāṇa tad abhāva upādhiḥ tasya tu eṣa kathana upāyaḥ na pramāṇa saṃsparśaḥ yathā nīla ākāra jñāna yogyaḥ arthaḥ nīlaḥ iti ākhyāte api na nīla śabdaḥ nīla jñāna upādhiḥ tathā ca saḥ asti śabdena abhidhīyate iti artha svabhāva niṣṭham asti artha pradhānam vākyam iti kutas sa apekṣa tvam pramāṇasya asaṃsparśāt 
[89,i^1]	syāt etat bhinnāḥ eva artha svabhāvāḥ pramāṇam prati yogyāḥ sat śabda vācyāḥ santu na ekā sattā mā bhūt na etat sādhyam sarvathā artha svabhāva abhidhāyyasti śabdaḥ na pramāṇa yoga nimittaḥ iti pramāṇa saṃsparśe hi sa apekṣatā syāt aneka tā tu na kañcid doṣam āvahati api ca yadi tasya anekatvam katham abhinna śabda pravṛttiḥ tathā hi bhinneṣu abhinnam viśeṣaṇam upalakṣaṇam vā aśritya ekaḥ śabdaḥ varteta bhinna nimittaḥ vā sādhāraṇa śabdaḥ syāt akṣa ādi vat tatra na tāvat ananta artha svabhāveṣu sādhāraṇa tvam upapadyate saṃbandha grahaṇa sāmarthyāt 
[89,i^2]	parimita jāti viṣayāḥ hi akṣa ādi śabdāḥ parimita upalakṣaṇa lakṣitāḥ vā syuḥ syāt etat dravya tva ādi sāmānya traya upalakṣitānām arthānām sat śabdaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ iti tat na yaḥ hi sattām avajānīte sa dravya tva ādīni api avajānītaḥ eva na kila tejaḥ dṛṣṭavataḥ apsu tad avamarśaḥ bhavati api ca sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyāḥ api santaḥ eva na teṣu aupacārikaḥ sat śabdaḥ pratyayasya availakṣaṇyāt na ca sāmānyāt vinā upacāraḥ sati vā sāmānye tat eva sat śabda arthaḥ tat eva ca sattā tulya tvāt pratyayasya atha matam sarva pravādeṣu sarva padārthāḥ parimitaiḥ kaiścid dharmaiḥ upasaṃgṛhītāḥ 
[89,i^3]	tad upalakṣaṇānām anantānām api arthānām sat iti sādhāraṇaḥ śabdaḥ tat ayuktam saṃgrahaḥ hi na ekam antareṇa tatra yadi sat śabda artha tayā saṃgrahaḥ etāvat prabhedaḥ sat śabda arthaḥ iti na artha antara nivṛttiḥ syāt tatra na sarva artha saṃgrahaḥ syāt yathā navavidhaḥ go śabda arthaḥ iti na anyeṣām abhāvaḥ eva tatra na pravādebhyaḥ kācid artha tattva avagatiḥ syāt nanu na pravādānām arthavat tā sādhyā na brūmaḥ pravādānām arthavat tā sādhyeti kim tu pratipadyante pravādinaḥ kañcid artha svabhāvam ekam yasya ayam pañca ṣaṣ ityādi prabheda saṃgrahaḥ 
[89,i^4]	yatas na ekam antareṇa upasaṃgrāhakam avāntara saṃkhyānām niveśaḥ atha etāvān pramāṇa yogyaḥ artha kriyā sāmarthyaḥ vā iti pramāṇa yogya tve artha kriyā sāmarthye vā saṃgrahaḥ tābhyām eva sat śabda arthaḥ upalakṣyatām vyarthaḥ parimita dharma upanyāsaḥ tatra sāmānya śabda tā eva syāt na sādhāraṇa śabda tā bhinna nimitta tve ca akṣa ādi śabdebhyaḥ iva nimitta bhedāt saṃśayaḥ syāt na viśeṣa pratītiḥ na hi san ghaṭaḥ iti nimitta bhedeṣu pratipattāraḥ saṃśerate yathā eva śuklaḥ paṭaḥ iti nirākāṅkṣaḥ tathā san ghaṭaḥ iti api 
[89,i^5]	yaḥ tu dravyam guṇaḥ karma rūpam vijñānam iti vā saṃśayaḥ na sa laukikānām laukikāḥ tu abhinnam eva nimittam pratipadyante arthāt ca saṃdehaḥ na śabdāt kutas viśeṣa pratītim antareṇa api pratipattuḥ naiḥ ākāṅkṣyāt yatra hi artha sāmarthyena saṃśayaḥ yathā vṛkṣaḥ chidyatām iti paraśu kuṭhāra ādiṣu tatra anyatara viśeṣa an avagame api nairākāṅkṣam yasya kasyacid upādānāt anyathā anavasthānāt yatra tu śabdāt tatra viśeṣa avagama hetoḥ vinā sa ākāṅkṣa tvam eva tat evam na nānā nimittaḥ sādhāraṇa śabdaḥ viśeṣaṇam api ekam pramāṇam syāt 
[89,i^6]	tat ca prāk api tatas sat śabda anuviddha buddhi utpādāt anupapannam iti uktam mānāt eva yatas buddhiḥ iti prapañcena api ca kāryāt api vṛttam eva pramāṇam avasīyate tatra kutas tad viśiṣṭa tā na khalu arthaḥ asat nihita viśeṣa guṇaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ bhavati na ca niścite viśeṣaṇa abhāve viśiṣṭa abhidhāna anuviddhaḥ saṃśayaḥ bhavati daṇḍa abhāva niścayaḥ iva daṇḍī na vā iti bhavati ca śūnya nagara ādiṣu cira nikhāta nidhiṣu pramāṇa abhāva niścaye api santi naḥ iti saṃśayaḥ tasmāt anyaḥ pramāṇa yogāt sadarthaḥ yatra eṣa saṃśayaḥ na api upalakṣaṇam pramāṇam pramita dhvasteṣu sat śabdā prayogāt smaryamāṇe ca sat śabda anuviddhāt saṃdehāt 
[89,i^7]	vṛtta pramāṇa saṃbandhasya pramāṇa upalakṣita tvāt sattvam eva syāt na asattvam na saṃśayaḥ yaḥ api artha kriyayā sat śabda artham viśinaṣṭi upalakṣayati vā tasya api prāc kārya darśanāt na sat śabda yogaḥ syāt atha pramāṇa jananam eva artha kriyām brūyāt pramāṇāt eva asti buddhiḥ na syāt atha vaikalpikī iyam pramāṇa uttara kālatā iti matam liṅgāt na syāt atha nirjñāta kārya saṃbandham eva liṅgena anugamyate evam tarhi prameya abhāvaḥ tathā hi kāryavat tā hi asti arthaḥ sā ca adhigatā eva kāryavat tayā eva kāryavat tau agamyate iti acatur asram 
[89,i^8]	kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca yaugapadya abhāvāt viśiṣṭa tā anupapattiḥ atha upalakṣaṇam atītasya api sattva prasaṅgaḥ smaryamāṇe ca saṃśayaḥ na syāt iti uktam tasmāt yathā eva nīla ādi śabda arthaḥ artha svabhāvaḥ na kārya lakṣyaḥ na pramāṇa lakṣyaḥ anavasthānāt sva rūpa vyavasthaḥ tu yathāpramāṇam avasīyate tathā sat artha svabhāvaḥ api iti yuktam kārya pramāṇa sadasadbhāva nibandhane hi sat asat vyavahāra vibhāge tasya apravṛttiḥ eva kārya pramāṇa sadasat vyavahāra vibhāgasya api tad nibandha tva prasaṅgāt anavasthānāt tasmāt artha svabhāvaḥ ekā sattā iti brahma vidaḥ manyante 
[91,i]	atha matam na artha svabhāvaḥ yogya tā pramāṇa hetu sadbhāvaḥ tu na ca asatām pramāṇa hetavaḥ santi iti tat ayuktam bhūmau nikhātam nirliṅgam avedya anupapannakam naṣṭa draṣṭṛkam atyeti yat sarvam iti yogya tām bhūmau nikhātam avidyamāna indriya saṃbandham adṛśyamāna avinābhūtama saṃvedyamānānyatha anavakalpamānam vastu pralīna draṣṭṛkam yat tasya na pratyakṣa anumāna arthāpatti āgama hetavaḥ santi sādṛśya viṣayam hi upamānam tasya hetuḥ dūra apetaḥ eva sarva pramāṇa yogyatām atikrāmati na ca tat asat nanu sattvam api asya katham evam api saṃśayaḥ tatra pramāṇa hetu bhāva lakṣaṇa yogya tā rūpe sattve pramāṇa hetu abhāvasya niścayāt saṃśayaḥ na syāt atha svabhāva viśeṣaḥ kaścid pramāṇam prati yogyaḥ sattvam prakṛta hānāt asundaram iti uktam atha vā pramāṇa viśiṣṭaḥ sat śabda arthaḥ iti etat anena nirākriyate na niścite viśeṣaṇa abhāve viśiṣṭa abhidhāyi śabda anuviddhaḥ saṃśayaḥ yuktaḥ iti 
[91,ii]	api ca abhāvasya api prameya tvāt na pramāṇa yogya tā sattā lakṣaṇam tathā hi asat prameyam ca tathā yathā eva sthāpayati ayam amitam hi tathā kasmāt tathā na punar anyathā avaśyam khalu anena sat asat vyavahāra vibhāgam icchatā asat kathañcit vyavasthāpyam anyathā vyavahāra saṃkarāt tatra yadi pramāṇasya aviṣayaḥ yadi sarva śakti virahaḥ vā asat buddheḥ viṣayaḥ sarvathā tathā prameyam aparicchinnam hi tathā pramāṇena kim iti tadvidham na punar anyathā syāt na ced tasya tathā abhāve atathā abhāve vā pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ kiṃnimittaḥ eka pakṣa anurāgaḥ 
[92,i]	api ca amitvā kaṇṭaka abhāvam caraṇam nyasyate katham na anya grahāt tasya bhāve purastāt ca prasaṅgataḥ jijñāsā na pravarteta yadi saṃvitti abhāvataḥ dṛṣṭi pūtam padam nyaset iti kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi abhāve apramite katham tat nyāsaḥ tathā hi kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi artha antara bhū tala ādi paricchedāt sa syāt kīṭa ādi aparicchedāt abhāva paricchedāt vā tatra na tāvat artha antara paricchedāt kaṇṭaka ādi bhāve api prasaṅgāt tatra api vastu antara paricchedasya sattvāt prāk api ca bhū bhāga paricchedāt prasajyeta yasya kasyacid vastu antarasya paricchitteḥ vidyamāna tvāt atha kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi a paricchedāt na tad bhāva abhāva jijñāsā syāt jijñāsā pūrvam api prayatnāt tad apariccheda mātram eva prāpyate yasya abhāvaḥ na prameyaḥ tat ca prāk api tatas asti abhāve tu prameye abhāva niścayāya jijñāsā yujyate na ca aparicchedaḥ eva jijñāsyaḥ svatas siddha tvāt paricchedena hi sa nivartyate aprameya tvāt ca saḥ api khalvabhāvaḥ iti aprameyaḥ 
[92,ii]	atha matam satsu upalambha hetuṣu pramāṇa viṣayasya aparicchedāt pravṛttiḥ tat asat pramāṇa viṣaya tvasya na upayogaḥ atra dṛśyate asat bodhe ananya hetu bhānena hi upayujyate aparicchedāt ced pravṛttiḥ na pramāṇa viṣaya tvasya upayogaḥ itaratra api aparicchedasya tulya tvāt tatas ca pravṛtteḥ yasya svabhāvaḥ prameyaḥ tad paricchedāt pravṛttiḥ tasya ananya nimitta tvena upayoga vat pramāṇa viṣaya tvam na ayam aparicchedaḥ sati eva arthe hetu vaikalya nimittaḥ samagra tvāt tad hetūnām tasmāt artha abhāvāt iti 
[93,i]	atha yatra pravṛttiḥ syāt tatra kevala saṃvidaḥ jijñāseta na sūkṣma artham kaivalyam saṃvidaḥ yadi kevalaḥ viṣayaḥ na iṣṭaḥ rūpa unmiśre api tat yatas viśiṣṭasya ca na asti anyat anyā abhāvāt viśeṣaṇam yadi matam yatra bhū bhāga ādau caraṇa nyāsa ādi lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ tasya kevalasya sā jñānāt iti tatra api saṃpradhāryam kim idam jñānasya kaivalyam abhisaṃhitam eka viṣaya pratiniyamaḥ viṣaya antara asaṃsargaḥ āhosvit viṣayasya yadi vijñānasya pramite api bhū bhāga ādau sthūle sūkṣma kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi bhāva abhāva parīkṣā na syāt pravarteta eva kevala bhū talāva graha jñānāt atha viṣayasya tatra api saṃpradhāryam sva rūpeṇa vā viṣayasya kaivalyam viśeṣaṇa yogena vā tatra na tāvat svarūpeṇa miśre api tasya bhāvāt viśeṣaṇa yogena kaivalye prāptā kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi abhāva viśiṣṭa paricchedāt pada nyāsa ādi lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ yatas na anya abhāvāt viśeṣaṇa m anyādṛśam kiñcid dṛśyate yat viśeṣaṇam vastu kevalam syāt iti 
[93,ii]	na asti iti dhī vyavahṛtī viṣayam kam upāśrite māna abhāvam yadi kṣuṇṇam meyā bhāvasya tatra kim api ca anena na asti iti buddhi śabdayoḥ viṣayaḥ vācyaḥ sa na vastu svarūpeṇa miśre api prasaṅgāt na kevalam abhāvāt anyasya viśeṣaṇasya abhāvāt iti uktam nanu na asti iti ayam arthaḥ na idam pramīyate iti na punar abhāvaḥ avagamyate viruddham idam na asti avagamyate ca iti yadi evam pramāṇa abhāvaḥ viṣayaḥ uktaḥ syāt na asti iti dhī śabdayoḥ tatra kaḥ aparādhaḥ syāt prameya abhāvasya yena tam atilaṅghya pramāṇa abhāvaḥ viṣayaḥ ucyate na hi tayoḥ nirupākhya tve kaścid viśeṣaḥ 
[94,i^1]	atha matam agrahe asat graha bhrāntiḥ abhāva vyavahṛt bhramaḥ abhāve ca vyavahṛteḥ adṛṣṭau dhvānta dṛṣṭi vat na eva stām na asti iti buddhi vyavahārau katham imau sarva janānām pratītau apahnūyete ucyate bhramaḥ ayam sat buddhi abhāve tad viparyaya paricchedaḥ iti tathā sat vyavahāra abhāve tad viparyaya vyavahāra bhramaḥ yathā loka darśana abhāve tamaḥ paśyāmi iti vibhramaḥ na hi tamaḥ nāma kiñcid dṛśyam asti na etat sāram ittham bhavet suṣupta ādau trailokya abhāva dṛś bhramaḥ aparicchindataḥ kiñcid vibhramaḥ ca na yujyate āropaviṣaya āropye na ajānan rajata bhramī na abhāva bhinnāḥ vyavahṛtta dabhāvaḥ ca dhīpade 
[94,i^2]	tamaḥ dṛṣṭiḥ tu bhūt chāyām āloka abhāvam eva vā ālambate na tu adṛṣṭa āviṣṭaḥ darśana vibhramaḥ yadi khalva darśane viparyaya darśana bhramaḥ bhavati suṣupta ādi avasthāsu viśva abhāva darśana bhramaḥ syāt āloka adarśana bhrama vat na ca kiñcid aparicchindataḥ vibhramaḥ tathā hi āropasya viṣayam purovarti vastu āropaṇīyam ca rajatam jñānena anāpnuvat na rajata bhramavān bhavati anyathāpratipattiḥ smṛtiḥ sāmānya pratipattiḥ vā na ca buddhi abhāvaḥ jñānasya viṣayaḥ na vyavahāra abhāvaḥ nābhauva buddhiḥ na abhāva vyavahāraḥ viśeṣaṇasya abhāvasya jñāna aviṣaya tvāt tatra ubhayoḥ viṣaya āropaṇīyayoḥ agrahaṇe na mithyājñānam iti 
[94,ii]	abhyupagamya pramāṇa yogya tām sattām doṣa abhāvaḥ ucyate astu vā māna yogya tvam sattvam tat ca pramīyatām tasmin mite vastu sattvam bhavati āgama gocare na ca sa apekṣatā na asmin antara artha vibhinna tām pracakṣate ye api sattām anyām na pratijānate bhavatu vā pramāṇa yogya tā sattā sā eva ca prameyāḥ tu tat prameyam vastu sattvam āgama arthaḥ na ca pramāṇa antara apekṣa tā doṣaḥ pramāṇa antara saṃbhedasya abhāvāt pramāṇa yogyaḥ iti etāvat mātrā adhigateḥ tathā hi ye api pramāṇa yogya tām sattām āhuḥ na tad vyatirekiṇīm te api na atra antara artha saṃsparśam icchanti tad saṃsparśe hi anyat pramāṇam anveṣyam syāt katham na anveṣyam yadā vacaḥ pramāṇa yogya tāyām paryavasitam na viśiṣṭa artha sattvam bodhayati tatra yasya pramāṇasya yogyaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ arthaḥ tad avaśya apekṣaṇīyam kimartham tat apekṣyate viśiṣṭa vastu sattva adhigamāya kam punar viśiṣṭasya vastunaḥ sattvam pramāṇa yogya tvam adhigatam eva tarhi tat asti artha niṣṭhāt vacanāt pramāṇa yogya tāyāḥ asti artha tvāt 
[95,i]	pramāṇa antara saṃbheda abhyupagame api na aprāmāṇya prasaṅga doṣaḥ iti darśayati pramāṇa antara bhinna artham api mānam na naḥ vacaḥ nirapekṣam iha arthe tu pramitam vastu idam mayā artha mātre ca sa apekṣam anya apekṣā artha bodhanāt abādhitam api tu arthe pramāṇa aṃśe apabādhanāt tatra apramāṇa tām eti buddha an āpta vacaḥ yathā āpta vākyam punar na arthe na māna aṃśe apabādhitam nirapekṣam pramāṇa aṃśe vyavahāraḥ anyathā katham mayā iti vaktra bhāvena saṃbheda rahitam tatas pralīna jñāna vijñeya vibhāgam sva ātma vedanam pravedayantu vedāntāḥ māna antaram alaukikam tad siddhi siddha tā arthasya puṃvacaḥ vat bhaviṣyati 
[96,i^1]	na khalu pramāṇa antara saṃbhinna artham api vacaḥ na pramāṇam pramāṇam eva hi āpta vākyam katham punar pramāṇam sa apekṣam iti ced ucyate nirapekṣam eva tat pramitaḥ ayam mayā arthaḥ iti asmin arthe kevale hi arthe evam ayam arthaḥ iti apratīteḥ evam ayam puruṣaḥ vedaḥ iti ca pratīteḥ puruṣa jñāna apekṣam tatra upalabdhau tāvat anapekṣa tvāt prāmāṇyam aśnute tad siddhi dvāraḥ ca paścāt arthaḥ iti katham tarhi puruṣa vacaḥ kiñcid abādhita artham api sa apekṣa tvena apramāṇam kathyate ucyate yadi api arthe bādhaḥ na asti yad apekṣam tu asya arthe prāmāṇyam yat siddhi mukhena tam sādhayati tatra pramāṇa aṃśe bādhyate tasya asiddheḥ tad dvāreṇa na artha siddhiḥ iti arthe apramāṇam yathā atīndriya arthe buddha vacaḥ puruṣasya darśana asaṃbhavāt 
[96,i^2]	yathā uktam puruṣa aśaktitaḥ tatra sa apavāda tva saṃbhavaḥ iti yathā ca vipralambhaka vākyam ayathā dṛṣṭa artha vādi tvasya pramāṇa avagata tvāt āpta vacaḥ punar na arthe na api pramāṇa aṃśe saṃbhavat pramāṇa gocaram bādhyate pramāṇa aṃśe ca anapekṣam tad mukhena ca artha siddhim vidadhanna apramāṇam bhavitum arhati anyathā śabda nibandhanaḥ vyavahāraḥ na syāt evam ca pramāṇa antara saṃbhinna artha tve api vedānta vacasām na prāmāṇya vyāhatiḥ āpta vākya vat tathā hi tāni api jñāna jñeya vibhāga vikalam sva prakāśa rūpam alaukikam kāmam avagamayantu pramāṇa antaram tad dvārā ca artha siddhiḥ āpta vacana vat iyān tu viśeṣaḥ syāt vede vaktuḥ abhāvāt mayā iti saṃsparśaḥ na syāt 
[96,ii_96,iii^1]	abhyupagama vādam parisamāpya prakṛtam upasaṃharati evam na meya tā sattā paraḥ punar pratyavatiṣṭhate nanu anyā api na yujyate na hi pūrva avamarśena vinā sāmānya kalpanā gām ekām īkṣitavataḥ jāyate anyatra yādṛśaḥ avamarśaḥ dṛṣṭa sataḥ tathā na hi sat antare eka śabda pravṛttiḥ tu daṇḍya ādi vat upeya tām dṛṣṭa rūpa avamarśaḥ sāmānya kalpanāyām pramāṇam yathā bāhuleyam dṛṣṭavataḥ śābaleye saḥ eva ayam iti na ca kiñcid sat gṛhītavataḥ anyatra sa bhavati eka śabda pravṛttiḥ tu vinā api sāmānyena artha antara yoga nimittā daṇḍi pācaka ādi śabda vat atra ucyate kaḥ nu pūrva avamarśaḥ ayam pūrvarūpa anvayaḥ dhiyaḥ 
[96,iii^2]	sat antare api saḥ asti eva kayācid khalu mātrayā sarva ātmanā tu anugamaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ khaṇḍa muṇḍayoḥ na tādṛśaḥ ca id naḥ bheda mātrāt vedyaḥ sva pahnavaḥ na bheda mātrāt mṛd jāti hīnam maṇika mallakam rūpa anvayaḥ pratyayasya maṇikeṣu hi yādṛśaḥ na dṛṣṭa mallakasya asti maṇike khalu tādṛśaḥ kaḥ punar ayam pūrva avamarśaḥ pūrvarūpa avabhāsaḥ buddheḥ atha saḥ ayam iti pūva arpara anu sandhānam tatra yadi pūrvaḥ kalpaḥ saḥ asti eva sat antare mātrayā tathā hi nirupākhya vailakṣaṇyena satām tulya rūpa tā prakāśate anyathā nirupākhya vatsantaḥ api atyanta vilakṣaṇāḥ prakāśeran 
[96,iii^3]	atha sarva rūpa anugamaḥ saḥ abhiprete api sāmānya gocare na asti na hi khaṇḍa muṇḍayoḥ sarva ātmanā anvayaḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt sāmānya abhāva āpatteḥ atha na tādṛśaḥ yādṛśaḥ khaṇḍa ādiṣu tat asat na viśeṣa mātreṇa saṃvedyān vayi rūpa pratyākhyānam yujyate go tva ādeḥ api tad saṃbhavāt na hi devadattasya dvitīya darśane yādṛśaḥ rūpa anugamaḥ tādṛśaḥ khaṇḍam dṛṣṭavataḥ muṇḍa darśane sāmānya gocare api ca na sarvatra tulyaḥ nānā maṇika vilakṣaṇaḥ hi maṇika śara ābayaḥ rūpa anvayaḥ na ca tāvatā mṛd jāti hīna tā tayoḥ kiñcid tulya tayā avabhāsamāna tvāt atha dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ atra ucyate pūrva avamarśaḥ saḥ iti prakhyā iti api na śobhate 
[96,iii^4]	maṇikam vīkṣitavataḥ saḥ api na udeti mallake pūrva apara anusandhāna ātmikā saḥ ayam iti abhedam avagamayantī bhinneṣu api sāmānya kalpanā hetuḥ buddhiḥ pūrva avamarśaḥ iti ucyate iti etat api na śobhate yatas na anusandhānāt eva abheda siddhiḥ abhinna rūpa avabhāsāt api anyathā na abhinna deśa kāle ekaḥ arthaḥ syāt na hi tatra deśa kāla bheda abhāve saḥ iti anusandhānam api ca dṛṣṭa maṇikasya mallake na bhavati drāk iva saḥ iti anusandhānam khaṇḍa muṇḍa vat na ca evam mṛd jāti hīna tā vimṛśataḥ tu tad jātīyam idam iti buddhiḥ sat antare api samānā 
[98,i]	tulye tarhi sāmānya yoge kasmāt kvacid saḥ iti avamarśaḥ na anyatra ucyate sāmānya rūpa bhūyaḥ tve tasmāt tattvam prakāśate vilakṣaṇa tvam alpa tve cakāsti tad anudbhavāt yasmāt sati api sāmānya yoge maṇi śara ābayoḥ na saḥ iti prakhyā maṇikā antare ca bhavati bhūyiṣṭha sāmānya yukte tasmāt sāmānya rūpāṇām bhūyiṣṭha tvena udbhavāt saḥ iti tattva prakhyā alpa tve tu na tathā teṣām anudbhavāt 
[98,ii]	na ca daṇḍya ādi vat eka śabda pravṛttiḥ iti āha pramāṇam kārya vijñeyam asaṃyojya asti dhīryataḥ prathamam jāyate tasmāt na daṇḍya ādi samāna tā na agṛhīta viśeṣaṇā viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ na ca viśiṣṭa buddheḥ prāk pramāṇa grahaṇam tad kālam vā tathā hi pramāṇāt eva sā bhavati pramāṇam ca pramiti kārya unneya tvāt paścāt sat pratipatteḥ gṛhyate tasmāt agrahāt pramāṇasya tad saṃyojana vikalā sā na pramāṇa yoga nimittā yadi tarhi na pramāṇa yogaḥ asti arthaḥ katham tad kāla anuvidhāyinī kāla pravṛttiḥ asti arthe kūpaḥ asti kūpaḥ abhūt kūpaḥ bhaviṣyati iti tad upādhi prakalpita bheda tvāt devadatta sattāyāḥ iva pāṭaliputra saṃyoga upādhi kalpita bhedāyāḥ iti 
[99,i]	na ca kriyām antareṇa na saṃsargaḥ padārthānām iti śabda artha naya vidāma vigānam iti āha saṃbandha mātra avasitam api ca anye vipaścitaḥ āhuḥ vacaḥ akriyam ayam rājñaḥ nā phalinaḥ drumāḥ rājñaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ phalitāḥ ete vanaspatayaḥ iti kriyā rahiteṣu api saṃsargaḥ pratīyate na ca iha api asti kriyā iti yujyate yatas na nirjñāta rāja saṃbandhasya puruṣasya phalavatām ca vanaspatīnām sattā iha pratipādyā gamyate na hi ete vākye sattāyām paryavasyataḥ kim tu puruṣasya rāja saṃbandhe drumāṇā ca phala saṃbandhe yaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ sa rājñaḥ ye ete vanaspatayaḥ te phalitāḥ na yaḥ rāja puruṣaḥ saḥ asti ye ca phalitāḥ te santi iti yat api kecid avadhāryatām iti pratipatti kriyā vidhinā kriyāvat tām manyate tat api śabdāt eva pratipatteḥ siddha tvāt prāk nirastam eva iti 
[99,ii]	atha api na kriyā rahitam vākyam asti kriyāyām ca sa apekṣatā tathā api na doṣaḥ iti āha jani kriyā avasānāt ca viśiṣṭam śakya bodhanam kāraṇam jāyate idam īdṛkṣāt kāraṇāt iti īdṛkṣāt kāraṇāt jagat jāyate iti jani kriyā niṣṭhāt api vākyāt tadvidha kāraṇa sattā śakyate pratipattum yathā īdṛśāt taroḥ idam phalam ajani iti tadvidha taru sadbhāvaḥ tathā ca śrutayaḥ kāścid evam eva brahma pratipādayanti sarvāṇi ha vai imāni bhūtāni ākāśāt eva samutpadyante yathā agneḥ kṣudrā viṣphuliṅgāḥ vyuccaranti evam eva asmāt ātmanaḥ sarve devāḥ ityādi tathā yathā ūrṇanābhiḥ sṛjate gṛhṇate ca yathā pṛthivyām oṣadhayaḥ saṃbhavanti yathā sataḥ puruṣāt keśa lomāni tathā akṣarāt saṃbhavati iha viśvam 
[100,i_100,ii]	tat etat satyam yathā su dīptāt pāvakāt viṣphuliṅgāḥ sahasraśas saṃbhavante sarūpāḥ tathā akṣarāt vividhāḥ somya bhāvāḥ prajāyante tatra ca eva apiyanti tathā divyaḥ hi amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ sa bāhya abhantaraḥ hi ajaḥ aprāṇaḥ hi amanāḥ śubhraḥ akṣarāt paratas paraḥ etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca kham vāyuḥ jyotiḥ āpaḥ pṛthivī viśvasya dhāriṇi iti 
[100,iii^1]	idānīm padārtha saṃsargāya eva vidhiḥ āśrayitavyaḥ iti pratyavatiṣṭhate nanu pramā antara adhīna saṃsargāḥ puruṣa uktiṣu padārthāḥ vidhi adhīna ātma saṃśleṣāḥ itaratra tu padānām racanā tatra vivakṣā paripūrtaye pramāṇa antara gamye arthe vivakṣā ca vyavasthitā vidhi artha siddhaye vede tad abhāve tu asaṃgateḥ viśiṣṭa artha gatiḥ bhrāntiḥ agrahe graha vibhramaḥ vivakṣita artha niṣpattaye hi loke padānām samabhivyāhāraḥ na eka pada sādhyaḥ vivakṣita arthaḥ pramāṇa antara upalabdhaḥ ca vivakṣā viṣayaḥ tena tatra pramāṇa antara āyattaḥ saṃsargaḥ tathā ca tad virodhe asaṃsargaḥ eva padārthānām jaradgavaḥ pāduka kambalābhyām iti vede tu pramāṇa antara abhāvāt vidhi nibandhanaḥ asau tad abhāve tu asaṃbhava ādyā iyam viśiṣṭa artha gatiḥ ucyate sā bhrāntiḥ samabhivyāhārāt 
[100,iii^2]	saḥ ayam viveka agrahe saṃsarga graha vibhramaḥ atra idam eva vicāryam katham loke pramāṇa antara adhīnaḥ saṃsargaḥ iti yadi pramāṇa antareṇa tad avagamāt tat asat apūrvasya api tasya pratīteḥ anyathā vacana vaiyarthyāt anadhigatam hi śrotuḥ artham bodhayitum vacaḥ prayujyate atha saṃsarga yogya tā mātrasya pramāṇa antareṇa avagamāt samānam etat vede tathā hi aruṇayā krīṇāti iti saṃsargaḥ na aruṇayā eka hāyanyā iti tathā bhāva arthaḥ niyoga viṣayaḥ na dravya guṇa śabda arthaḥ iti pramāṇa antara avasita yogya tā sāmarthyena eva vyasthāpyate atha na vivakṣa eka padau agamyā tad artha mātra vivakṣāyāḥ niṣprayojana tvāt tasmāt vivakṣā viśeṣa siddhiḥ na asaṃsṛṣṭeṣu padārtheṣu bhavati iti tathā vivakṣayā prayuktāḥ saṃsṛjyante 
[100,iii^3]	sā ca pramāṇa antara siddhaḥ iti evam api vivakṣā nibandhanaḥ syāt tad prayuktānām saṃsargāt na pramāṇa antara nibandhanaḥ yatas na tat tasya pratipādakam na prayojakam vā yat tu pramāṇa antara siddhe vivakṣā iti bhavatu na tu tasya saṃsargaḥ upayogaḥ tathā hi vipralambhaka vākye api saṃsarga pratītiḥ yat tu virodhe na saṃsargaḥ kāmam na tu tatas saṃsargaḥ virodhe api tu na asaṃsargaḥ pratīteḥ pratītaḥ api tu bādhyate pramāṇa antareṇa evam ca anṛtam kiñcid vacaḥ kiñcid anarthakam daśa dāḍima ādi kiñcid satyam anyathā anṛta anarthaka vibhāgaḥ na syāt atha pramāṇa antareṇa upalabhya artham vivakṣitvā parasmai pratipādayati puruṣaḥ tena tad vacasaḥ pramāṇa antara upalabdhiḥ eva arthaḥ 
[100,iii^4]	sā eva prayojikā padārtha saṃsargasya tasyāḥ prayojikāyāḥ abhāvāt na vede padārtha saṃsarga siddhiḥ mā bhūt sā viśiṣṭa arthaḥ eva prayojakaḥ atha lokau agamya tvāt śabda sāmarthyasya laukika prayojaka abhāvāt na saṃsargaḥ vidhimat tve api na syāt atha loke saṃsarga mātra paratve arthāpattiḥ na tad viśeṣe tanmātreṇa pratīti prayogayoḥ upapatteḥ vinā api pramāṇa antara upalabdhyā viśiṣṭa artha gati siddhiḥ atha pramāṇa antarāt loke saṃsarga satyatā avagamaḥ apūrvaḥ api hi śrotuḥ saṃsargaḥ vaktuḥ pramāṇa anumāna mukhena satya tām labhate tad asaṃbhave asatya tvāt buddha ādi vākyeṣu tena pramāṇa antara nibandhanaḥ loke saṃsargaḥ ucyate bhavatu vede tu pramāṇa antara saṃbheda abhāvāt svātantryeṇa artha pratīteḥ śabda nibandhanaḥ eva 
[102,i^1]	tadā astām etat bhavatu yathā loke idam tu paryanuyujyate katham nu vidhi adhīna tvam yadi syāt anyathā vṛthā vidhiḥ nirviṣayaḥ tulyam idam anya pada udite viśiṣṭa artha avagatya anya padārthaḥ api prayujyate arthavat tve pramābhau ādaḥ tu asau ced anarthakaḥ vidhiḥ na evam kasya hetoḥ atha syāt aparam padam pramāṇa antara siddhe arthe prayogi na vidhāyakam tad arthaḥ ananyagamyaḥ hi mīyamānaḥ samākṣipet viṣayam na yathā siddha padārthaḥ tu anuvāda bhāj avyutpanna pravṛttiḥ syāt saṃbandha jñāna nihnave 
[102,i^2]	padam svadharmam vyutkrāmet anya siddhārtha tā anyathā na tāvat vidhiḥ sākṣāt saṃsarga sāmānyam tad viśeṣam vā bodhayati atha ākṣipati anyathā niyoga mātram nirviṣayam anarthakam syāt padārtha antareṣu api tulyam etat te api kevalāḥ padārtha antara saṃsargam anāpnuvantaḥ apūrva artha pratipatteḥ abhāvāt anarthakāḥ na ca loke padaiḥ sva arthāḥ sva rūpa mātra niṣṭhatayā eva pratyyante kim tu viśiṣṭa artha pratyaya prayuktāḥ tathā vyavahāra upapatteḥ tathā ca pratipadārtham saṃsarga ākṣepaḥ syāt etat loke buddhi pūrva prayuktānām mā bhūt ānarthakyam iti saṃsarga artha tā 
[102,i^3]	vede tu na arthavat tve pramāṇam asti atas padārtha antaram anarthakam eva astu na etat sāram na anyathā anarthakyam iti apramāṇaḥ arthaḥ śakyaḥ pratipattum yasya kasyacid pratipatti prasaṅgāt tasmāt vyavahārāt saṃsarga prayukta sva artha avabodha sāmarthyam eva padānām gamyate tatas vede api saṃsarga ākṣepaḥ yadica anya padārthānām ānarthakyam vidhi arthasya tat na kasmāt atha matam pada antarāṇi pramāṇa antara siddhe arthe prayujyante tāni yathā avagata artha anuvāda paryavasitāni tathā hi anūdyamānaḥ arthaḥ yathā avagamam anuvāda at na apūrva artha ākṣepāya alam 
[102,i^4_104,i]	vidhāyakaḥ tu śabdaḥ ananyagamya artha viṣayaḥ tad arthaḥ pramīyamāṇaḥ śaknoti apūrvam artham ākṣeptum anyathā anava kalpamānaḥ tasmāt vede vidhi nibandhanaḥ apūrva saṃsargaḥ iti tat ayuktam pramāṇa antara aviṣayaḥ ced vidhāyaka arthaḥ tatra saṃbandha jñānam aśakyam iti nihnūyeta tathā ca saṃbandha jñāna anapekṣa tvāt avyutpannaḥ api pravarteta saṃbandha jñāna apekṣa tā ca pada dharmaḥ vyutkramyeta tad nirapekṣa tā vākya dharmaḥ āśrīyeta atha saṃbandha apekṣatā na asya nihnūyeta balāt pramāṇa antara siddhārtha tā āpadyeta tathā ca na viśeṣaḥ śabdāt eva mite yaḥ api manyate saṃgati graham na anyonya saṃśraya avadyam na svayam pramite hi saḥ pareṇa śabda avagate tad pravṛttyā ca sūcite padārtha antara vat tatra sukaraḥ saṃgati grahaḥ 
[104,ii]	yaḥ api manyate na pramāṇa antara siddhe viddhi arthe saṃbandha jñānam api tu śabda siddhaḥ eva na ca anyonya saṃśraya doṣaḥ śabdāt siddhe saṃbandha jñānam saṃbandha jñāna pūrvikā ca śabdāt siddhiḥ iti yatas na svayam śabdāt pramite tat ucyate kim tu vṛddha prayuktāt vṛddha antareṇa avagateḥ tad avagamāt ca tasya vṛddhasya yā pravṛttiḥ tayā anumite nūnam anena vṛddhena pratipannaḥ kaścid pravṛtti hetuḥ arthaḥ asmāt śabdāt yena ayam etat śravaṇāt pravṛttaḥ iti yathā gām ānayaḥ iti sāsnādi mada ānayana darśanāt tad pratyayam anumāya tatra saṃbandha grahaṇam iti 
[104,iii]	tasya evam anumeya tve katham śabda eka gocaraḥ tasya api śabda pūrva tvāt anumāna eka gocaraḥ kasmāt na śabda bodhaḥ api hi anumāna purassaraḥ na idaṃprathama tā labhyā bīja aṅkura vat etayoḥ śabdāt boddhuḥ ca anumānam sarvasya eva puras sthitam padārtha antara vat tena tasya śabda unuvādakaḥ anumānāt budhyamānaḥ śabdāt buddham na budhyate pratipad tṛ antere bodhaḥ na anya bodha anuvāda kṛt pravṛtti hetu mātram ca śabda arthaḥ syāt alaukikaḥ na sa kalpayitum śakyaḥ tad siddheḥ laukikāt api 
[105,i^1]	yadi pravṛtti unnīyamāna pratyaya viśeṣaṇa tvena vyavasthitaḥ anumeyaḥ vidhāyaka arthaḥ saṃbandha jñāna viṣayaḥ na tarhi śabda eka pramāṇakaḥ atha anumānam śabda pūrvakam iti tathā ucyate śābdaḥ api pratyayaḥ anumāna pūrvakaḥ iti anumāna eka gocaraḥ syāt na khalu bīja aṅkurayoḥ iva ānayoḥ ekasya prāthamyam vyavasthāpayitum śakyam śabda avagatasya anumānāt anumitasya vidita saṃgateḥ śabdāt avagamāt api ca sarva pratipattṝṇām anumāna pūrvā śabdāt pratipattiḥ iti teṣām śabdaḥ anuvādakaḥ eva tathā hi śabdāt buddhyamānaḥ anumitam vidita saṃgatim budhyate sarva pratipattā na tu anumimānaḥ śabda avagatam anumimīte 
[105,i^2]	nanu śabda avagataḥ eva anumīyate satyam anena tu pratipattrā na ca anyadīyā pratipattiḥ anya pratipattim anuvādīkaroti pravṛtti hetu mātre ca saṃbandha vyutpatteḥ tanmātram śabda arthaḥ syāt na ca ālaukikaḥ kalpayitum api śakyaḥ laukikāt api pravṛtti siddheḥ syāt etat vaidikīṣu pravṛttiṣu tad asaṃbhavāt alaukika kalpanā na etat loka avagata sāmarthyaḥ hi śabdaḥ vede api pratipādakaḥ tatra laukikīṣu pravṛttiṣu laukike vidita saṃbandhe vede api tat pratipattiḥ eva syāt asaṃbhave vā mithyātvam 
[105,ii]	atha bahuvidha tvāt pravṛtti hetūnām vyabhicārāt aśabda artha tve pravṛtti hetu sāmānyam śabda arthaḥ tatra vede laukikānām viśeṣaṇānām asaṃbhavāt alaukikam viśeṣa antaram pratīyate evam api yaḥ śabda arthaḥ vede sāmānyam sa loka siddhaḥ iti na anuvāda tā vyāvartate padārtha antara vat yaḥ api viśeṣaḥ saḥ anya asaṃbhavena pariśeṣa anumāna gocaraḥ iti na pramāṇa antara aviṣaya tvam na ca pariśeṣa anumānam api śreyaḥ sādhana tāyāḥ saṃbhavāt atha matam loka vyavahāraḥ iva veda vyavahāraḥ api anādiḥ tatra vaidikīṣu pravṛttiṣu laukika pravṛtti hetu abhāvāt alaukike tu pravṛtti hetau vaidikānām vidhāyakānām saṃbandha jñānam na ca anumeya tvam tad pratyayasya pravṛttyā anumānāt tad siddhiḥ tu tad pratyaya sāmarthyena eva sa ca pratyayaḥ śabda utthaḥ iti ananya pramāṇa tā na ca laukikasya eva śreyaḥ sādhana tvasya saṃbhavaḥ iti yuktam laukikī hi pramāṇa antarau agamyā śreyaḥ sādhana tā tatra prayoga darśanāt liṅā ādeḥ tad anusāreṇa ca śabda artha avadhāraṇāt pramāṇa antara gamya tā api śabda artha anupraveśinī 
[106,i]	atra ucyate bhavatu nāma veda vyavahārāt eva śabda artha anugamaḥ tathā api na pramāṇa antara gocara tā vyāvartate tathā hi alaukike pravṛtti hetau śabdasya sāmarthya jñāna kāle pramitaḥ vā syāt na vā pramitaḥ ced śabda saṃbandhasya tadā eva jñāyamāna tvāt avaśyam pramāṇa antareṇa iti vācyam atha na pramitaḥ katham tatra saṃbandha jñānam na hi apramitayoḥ saṃbandhinoḥ tad āśrayaḥ saṃbandhaḥ pramātum śakyaḥ 
[106,ii^1]	yaḥ api manyate śaktiḥ hi śabdasya saṃbandhaḥ sā ca na arthe tasya vyavasthita tvāt pratyayaḥ tu tasya kāryaḥ sa ca pravṛttyā anumitaḥ tatra eva sāmarthya lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ pramīyate iti saḥ idam praṣṭavyaḥ kim pratyaya mātre sāmarthyam gṛhyate atha viśiṣṭe pravṛtti hetu pratyaye yadi pratyaya mātre yat kiñcit tatas pratīyeta atha viśiṣṭe laukika vyatirikta pravṛtti hetu pratyaye pravṛtti pariśeṣābhyām tasya anumita tvāt prāptam pramāṇa antara gocara tvam dvayī hi viśeṣaṇasya gatiḥ smārta ākṛṣṭam viśiṣṭa pramitau aṅga tvam eti yathā agnimān dhūmāt iti 
[106,ii^2]	viśiṣṭa grāhi pramāṇa prameyam vā yathā śuklaḥ gauḥ iti ubhayathā ca pramāṇa antara viṣayaḥ śabdasya anadhigata saṃbandha tvāt smārta ākṛṣṭa tve pramāṇa antaram anveṣyam dvitīye api kalpe viśiṣṭa pratyaya anumāna anumita tvāt atha anumānasya pratyayaḥ eva prāmāṇyam pratīti mātram tu tatra viśeṣaṇasya tāvatā ca tad viśiṣṭa prati iti aṅgam viśeṣaṇa pramitiḥ tu anumitāt pratyayāt yathā puruṣa vacanāt viśiṣṭa artha pramāṇe anumite artha siddhiḥ tatas eva pramāṇāt tatra hi arthaḥ pratīti mātreṇa eva vaktṛ jñānasya viśeṣaṇam tat etat apeśalam smṛti pramāṇa saṃśaya viparyāsa vikalpa antargamāt pratīteḥ 
[106,ii^3]	tatra alaukika viśeṣaṇa pratītiḥ na smṛtiḥ prāc anadhigateḥ na saṃśayaḥ koṭi dvaya saṃsparśa abhāvāt na vikalpaḥ pravṛtti hetu pratyayasya api tathā prasaṅgāt tathā na viparyāsaḥ katham hi tatra yathārtha tve tathābhūta grāhiṇī tad pratītiḥ artha śūnyā syāt pariśeṣāt pramāṇam para jñānena ca paraḥ pratipadyate iti subhāṣitam atha matam na para jñānena paraḥ pratipadyate kim tu sva jñānena eva para jñāna sāmarthyāt atha tasya sva jñānam katamat pramāṇam iti vācyam na tāvat śābdam śabda vijñānāt arthe vijñānam iti lakṣaṇāt na ca tad śabda jñānāt 
[106,ii^4]	kutas tarhi śabda uttha jñānāt anumitāt atha tasya prāmāṇye pravṛtti hetu sadbhāva siddhiḥ prāmāṇyam ca tasya doṣa rahita śabda udbhavāt tena śabdasya tatra prāmāṇyam ucyate tad adhīnaḥ tatra artha niścayaḥ iti tat api asāṃpratam śabdāt artha jñānam śābdam iti lakṣaṇāt puruṣa vacanam api na arthe na pramāṇam kim tu jñāna viśeṣaṇe dvayī ca viśeṣaṇasya gatiḥ uktā tatra smṛti asaṃbhavāt pramīyamāṇaḥ eva sa viśiṣṭa artha pramiti aṅgam anyathā arthe pramāṇa antaram anveṣyam syāt na ca vaktṛ jñānena eva artha siddhiḥ para jñānena na paraḥ pratipadyate iti uktam 
[108,i^1]	yat tu uktam vaktṛ jñāna adhīna artha siddhiḥ iti tat tad mithyā tve tad asaṃbhave vā pramāṇa pratīti bādhane artha pratīteḥ api bādhanāt tat abādhe ca ābādhāt na tu vacasaḥ arthaḥ na viṣayaḥ anyathā pramāṇa antara paratantram puruṣa vacaḥ arthe sa apekṣam iti etat eva na syāt na hi yaḥ yasya aviṣayaḥ sa tatra sa apekṣaḥ anapekṣaḥ vā tathā ca prāmāṇya sthāpanam tu syāt vaktṛ dhīhetu saṃbhavāt iti uktam sthāpanam abādhaḥ na tu prāmāṇyam eva tat ca vaktṛdhī hetu saṃbhavāt vākyasya na tu vaktṛdhiyaḥ eva śabdasya ca arthena saṃbandhaḥ na tu jñānena evam hi uktam autpattikaḥ tu śabdasya arthena saṃbandhaḥ iti artha grahaṇam atra artha asaṃspaśī śabdaḥ jñānena eva śabdasya saṃbandhaḥ iti paśyatām nirākaraṇāya 
[108,i^2]	tasmāt anyonya yogya tā śabda arthayoḥ eva saṃbandhaḥ na ca apramite arthe sa śakyaḥ grahītum pramite pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvam uktam na ca pratīti mātre arthavatyāḥ pratīteḥ smṛti pramāṇayoḥ anyataratra antargamāt ānarthakye kena saṃbandha yadi ca śābda pratīti vyatirekiṇyā api pratītyā sa viṣayīkriyate apramāṇa ātmikayā api bhavati ayam aśābdasya api jñānasya gocaraḥ iti pramāṇa antara āśaṅkā kena vāryate na ca pramāṇa antara avagamyatā śabda artham anupraviśati yatas na anvaya mātreṇa vyatireka mātreṇa vā śabda arthaḥ sati hi anyasmin prayojake arthe yasya abhāve na prayogaḥ saḥ api tasya śabdasya prayojakaḥ iti gamyate yathā satsu hetu antareṣu yasya abhāve na kāryam saḥ api hetuḥ gamyate 
[108,i^3]	iha ca śreyaḥ hetu vivakṣāyām liṅga ādeḥ darśanāt tad abhāve sati api pramāṇa antara gamya tve adarśanāt śreyaḥ hetu tvam tāvat śabda arthaḥ pramāṇa antara gamya tve yadi api darśanam tad abhāve ca yadi api adarśanam na tu śreyaḥ hetu tve sati pramāṇa antara gamya tāyāḥ abhāvāt tatra saṃdigdhaḥ vyatirekaḥ ubhaya abhāve aprayogāt kiṃnibandhanaḥ aprayogaḥ iti tatra śreyaḥ sādhana tāyāḥ prayojaka tvasya avadhārita tvāt tad abhāve tad nibandhanaḥ iti gamyate tanmātreṇa anvaya vyatireka upapattau na anyasya śabda artha tve pramāṇam anyathā śiṃśapā śabda arthe sattva ādayaḥ api anupraviśeyuḥ teṣu satsu prayogāt tad abhāve ca aprayogāt 
[108,i^4]	atha śiṃśapātu asya śabda artha tvāt tad abhāva nibandhanaḥ eva sattā ādya bhāve aprayogaḥ tad sadbhāvāt ca prayogaḥ upapadyate iti na teṣu sāmarthya kalpanā samānam etat atra api atha śreyaḥ hetutvasya pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvāt tasya ca vede asaṃbhavāt aprāmāṇyam tat asat na hi yaḥ ekatra yasya pramāṇasya gocaraḥ saḥ anyatra api mithyā samīpe hi bahis indriya viṣayaḥ dūre tu āgama anumāna gamyaḥ tathā yāga ādiṣu viprakṛṣṭa kāla phaleṣu vedau agamyam śreyaḥ sādhana tvam bhaviṣyati na ca pramāṇa antara anupalabdhyā pramāṇa antara gamyaḥ bādhyate viṣaya vyavasthayā api pramāṇa pravṛtteḥ atha pramāṇa antara viṣaya tve tad virodhāt aprāmāṇyam anantara phala anupalabdheḥ tad aviṣaye tu śabda arthe na tad virodhaḥ iti syāt yadi virodhaḥ syāt na ca asau ānantaryam hi acoditam iti uktam 
[109,i^1]	atha mā bhūt ānantarya codanā mā ca bhūt pramāṇa antara avagamyatā śabda arthaḥ sarvathā pramāṇa antara siddhaḥ ced padārthaḥ āśrīyate sa yathā siddhi āśrayaṇīyaḥ anyathā na tad siddhaḥ syāt anantara śreyaḥ hetu tā ca tad siddhā tat na na tāvat anantara phala sādhana tā niyogataḥ karmaṇām kṛṣi auṣadha pāna ādiṣu anyathā api darśanāt avāntara kāryasya yāga ādau api pramāṇa sāmarthyena siddheḥ api ca viśiṣṭa siddhau viśeṣaṇam api śreyaḥ hetutva mātram siddham tāvat ca śabda arthaḥ na ca tāvati pramāṇa virodhaḥ tat evam laukike api pravṛtti hetau doṣa abhāvāt vyarthāḥ alaukika kalpanā sukha ādi vat ca asya anumeya tvāt 
[109,i^2]	tathā hi mukha prasāda ādi unneya saṃvedanāḥ sukha ādayaḥ tena eva sahonnīyante na evam sattve pṛthak pramāṇam arthyate yadā api idam darśanam vaktṛ jñānam eva puruṣa vacana arthaḥ tatra jñānam na artham antareṇa saṃbhavati iti artha āpattyā anumānena vā artha siddhiḥ tadā api pravṛtti pramitaḥ tadhetu pratyayaḥ na tam antareṇa iti āpta vacana artha vat anumeya tā na vyāvartate atha anumāna hrtoḥ pratyayasya śabda sādhana tvāt śabda pramāṇaka tvam tat asat na āpta vacana artha jñānasya akṣa sādhana tvāt tad arthaḥ śrotuḥ pratyakṣa pramāṇakaḥ bhavati tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate tasya evam anumeya tve katham śabda eka gocaraḥ tathā na sa kalpayitum śakyaḥ tad siddheḥ laukika dapi iti 
[110,i_110,ii]	atha pramāṇa rūpeṇa sa sva śabda prakāśitaḥ ākṣeptā nirapekṣaḥ ca kathyate anya pramām prati atha ucyate na brūmaḥ vidhiḥ anyathā vṛthā syāt iti tad adhīnaḥ saṃsargaḥ kim tu pramāṇān tmanā eva sa sva śabdena pratipādyate tathā ca pramāṇa tvāt prameyasya ākṣeptā pūrvasya pramāṇa antara anapekṣaḥ ca na hi asau śabdavat saṃbandha apekṣa tvāt pūrva siddhim apekṣate iti 
[110,iii]	tathā api asiddhe prāc uktau doṣau siddhe anuvāditā prāmāṇyam asya yatra astu śruteḥ tatra vṛthā tu ayam evam api avyutpanna pravṛtti pada dharma vyatikramau pramāṇa ātmā api sa yadi na pramāṇa antara siddhaḥ atha siddhaḥ yathā avagata anuvāda at na apūrva artha ākṣepaḥ api ca yatra asya prāmāṇyam iṣyate śabdasya eva tatra astu kim anena nanu uktam śabda saṃgati jñāna apekṣa tvāt anuvādakaḥ na apūrva artha avagamāya prabhavati na etat sāram śabdaḥ ced anuvādakaḥ tat prakāśyam pramāṇam api anūdyamānam yathā adhigatam katham apūrva artham bodhayet na prameya saṃsparśa rahitā pramāṇauvagatiḥ atas yathā adhigata prameyam eva tat pratīyate 
[111,i^1]	kva ca pramāṇam eṣaḥ arthe na yāga ādau sva śabdake laukike apūrva saṃsargaḥ śrotuḥ asti avidhau api phala sādhana śaktau ca īchabdaḥ tatra na dūṣyati padārtha antara tulya tvāt vidhi ākāṅkṣā nibandhanaḥ na saṃsargaḥ padārthānām sva śabdaiḥ tu prakāśitāḥ saṃbandha yogya rūpeṇa tasmāt saṃsarga bhāginaḥ viśiṣṭa artha prayuktāḥ hi samabhivyāhṛtiḥ jane atas na viddhi abhāvena saṃsargaḥ na prakalpate na ca niyogasya prameyam nirūpyate na tāvat yāga ādayaḥ prameyāḥ teṣām yajati ādi śabda viṣaya tvāt na api teṣām pramāṇa antarasya agocaraḥ saṃsargaḥ tathā hi avidhiṣu api laukikeṣu vākyeṣu śrotuḥ anadhigataḥ apūrvaḥ saṃsargaḥ pratīyate brāhmaṇa putraḥ te jātaḥ ityādiṣu 
[111,i^2]	atha phala sādhana sāmarthyam prameyam ucyate na kila kāminaḥ niyogaḥ akāma upāye dhātu arthe avakalpate anupāya tve hi tasya na sa kāminyā kṛtaḥ syāt iti tat api asaṃpratam na hi śabdasya tatra kaścid aparādhaḥ yena tam atikramya anyat pramāṇam mṛgyate pramāṇa antara apekṣa tā pratyuktā anantara phala adarśanena tu virodhaḥ niyoga gamye api tasmin aviśiṣṭaḥ ānantaryasya apramāṇa artha tvena tad abhāvaḥ śabde api tulyaḥ atha vā śabdaḥ tatra na duṣyati phala sādhana sāmarthye niyogaḥ tu duṣyati eva na hi tatas puruṣartha sādhana avabodhaḥ saṃbhavati tat ca idam vidhi viveka bhāvanā vivekābhyām avagantavyam tasmāt saṃbandha jñāna apekṣa tvena padārtha antaraiḥ samāna tvāt vidhāyaka arthasya na śakyam viśeṣeṇa vaktum tad nibandhanaḥ padārtha saṃsargaḥ iti 
[111,i^3]	sarve eva tu padārthāḥ saṃbandha yogyaiḥ kāraka ādi bhāvaiḥ sva padebhyaḥ pratītāḥ sannikarṣeṇa saṃsṛjyante yatas lokāt śabda vyāpāra avagamaḥ loke ca padaiḥ sva arthānām pratipādanam sannikarṣeṇa viśiṣṭa artha para tayā na sva artha mātra pratipatti para tayā tathā ca sarva padārtha ākāṅkṣā nibandhanaḥ eva saṃsargaḥ sarve hi te padaiḥ aparyavasita rūpāḥ sva rūpa mātre prakāśyante evam padārtha antaraiḥ tulya tvāt vidheḥ na viśeṣeṇa tad nibandhanaḥ saṃsargaḥ sarva padārtha nibandhane ca saṃsarge na vidhi abhāvena saṃsargaḥ na upapadyate tat evam na saṃsarga artham api vidhiḥ upāsanīyaḥ katham na upāsanīyaḥ yadā niyoga para tayā eva padānām sva artheṣu saṃsarga jñānam 
[111,i^4]	pravartaka vacana antara pravṛtti darśanena hi tad hetu pratyayam anumāya tatra tasya sāmarthyam gamyate na etat apravartake api vākye svarūpa niṣṭhe saṃbandha grahaṇāt sannidhāpita agni vyatirikta pākya upakaraṇam agni arthinam prati yadā ucyate caitra gṛhe kṛśānuḥ iti tadā tatas tena ānayanam dṛṣṭvā gamyate iha anena agni sattā pratītā sā ca asmāt vākyāt na ca śakyam vaktum tatas ānaya gaccha vā tatra iti vākyāt pratyayaḥ agni sattā mātra pratyayena vākyāt pravṛtti siddheḥ na vākyasya niyojane api sāmarthyam śakyate kalpayitum artha antara anvaye ca prayoga pratyaya upapattau na viśeṣa anvaye pramāṇam anyathā veda arthaḥ niṣpramāṇakaḥ eva syāt iti uktam 
[112,i]	atha kartavyatā jñānāt vinā anarthakyam ucyate na pravṛtti nivṛttibhyām anyat vākya prayojanam pratipatti vidhau tulyam yadi sā eva prayojanam samānam et tad artham ca samarpayati ced ayam prajñā kriyā upāsana adhikāra siddhi vyapekṣitam hanta tarhi svarupe tat na vacaḥ paryavasati tulyam etat samāptam ca vākyam vākya antara anugam niyoga anupraveśaḥ asti tavat yadi vṛthā anyathā tattva avabodha vidhi aṃśaḥ tāvat evam samuddhṛtaḥ 
[113,i^1]	atha manyate vastu svarūpa mātra jñānam kartavya tā jñāna rahitam pravṛtti nivṛtti śūnyam anarthakam pravṛtti nivṛtti prayuktā hi vākya pravṛttiḥ atho arthavat tvāya vidhiḥ anyathā narthakyam tatra ucyate pratipatti vidhau api tulyam ānarthakyam tathā hi evaṃvidhaḥ pratipattavyaḥ iti api na tad svarūpa jñāna atiriktā kācana pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ vā atha svarūpa jñānam eva prayojanam tad svarūpa mātra niṣṭhe api tulyam atha pratipatti vidhiḥ prajñām kurvīta sa kratum kurvīta ātmā iti eva upāsitaḥ iti adhikāra vidhi vyapekṣita prajñā upāsanā viṣaya samarpaṇena arthavān na avagata viṣaya svarūpā prajñā śakya iti 
[113,i^2]	svarūpa niṣṭham api vacaḥ tathā artha vat tasya samarpaṇe sutarām sāmarthyam nanu evam asya svarūpa niṣṭhā hīyate niyoga anupraveśinaḥ sva gata niyoga niṣṭham api tarhi tat na niyoga antara anupraveśāt atha matam sva artha paryavasitam eva vākyam vākya antareṇa eka vākya tām upaiti saḥ ayam prākaraṇikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ ucyate anyathā vākya lakṣaṇaḥ eva syāt etat api samānam niyoga anupraveśe api na sva rūpa niṣṭhatā hīyate nanu asti niyoga anupraveśaḥ anyathā ānarthakyāt kāmam tattva pratipatti vidhiḥ tu tāvat ānarthakyāt nirākṛtaḥ vidheḥ vinā api tasmāt śabdāt tatva avabodha siddheḥ 
[113,ii]	nanu utpatti vidhiḥ karma rūpa bodhe vyavasthitaḥ yathā tattva jñāna vidhiḥ tathā bodhe avatiṣṭhatām adhikārāt pravṛttiḥ ca matā karma adhikāra vat ajñāna jñāpanam atas atha apravṛtta pravartanam vidhim ācakṣate dhīrāḥ iti etat api tādṛśam karma svarūpa avagamaḥ tatra na iṣṭam vidheḥ phalam kim tu kārya vyapekṣasya phala vākyena saṃgatiḥ iha adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ yasya tat na vidhīyate tattvam tattva avabodhasya na adhikāra praveśitā na hi vrīhi ādi viṣayam pratyakṣam adhikāra bhāj 
[114,i^1]	yat api codyate yathā utpatti vidheḥ karma rūpa pratipatti mātram arthaḥ āgneyaḥ aṣṭa kapālaḥ iti na tatas pravṛttiḥ adhikāra vidhi nibandhana tvāt tasyāḥ tathā tattva avabodha vidheḥ tattva avabodha mātram arthaḥ pravṛttiḥ adhikāra vidheḥ prajñām kurvīta iti ādeḥ yatas ca pravṛtti pratipatti prayojana bhedaḥ vidheḥ atas asya lakṣaṇa dvayam āhuḥ ajñāta jñāpanam apravṛtta pravartanam iti etat api asāram yatas na utpatti gatasya vidhāyakasya svarūpa avagama mātram iṣyate phalam api tu adhikāra vākya saṃbandhaḥ tathā hi vidheḥ puruṣa artha mātra sādhana tve avabuddhe tad viśeṣa ākāṅkṣāyām adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ labhyate na ca tattva pratipatti vidheḥ api tat eva phalam yatas yasya adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ upāsana ādi viṣayasya ātma tattvasya tat akriyā ātmat tvāt na vidhi viṣayaḥ yat tu tad viṣayaḥ tattva jñānam tasya na adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ vrīhi ādi pratyakṣa vat na hi vrīhi ādi svarūpa grāhi pramāṇam prayoga eka deśa tām bhajate pramitānām adhikāra saṃbandhāt niṣpannānām iva anaḥ vāsaḥ prabhṛtīnām vāna takṣaṇa ādiḥ hi tad kriyā na adhikāram anupraviśati iti 
[115,i_115,ii]	idānīm tṛtīya pratipatti gocaraḥ vidhiḥ parāsyate tattva avabodha viṣaya tvena saṃbandhāt dvitīya pratipatti viṣayaḥ hi na tattva avabodha viṣayaḥ kim tu tad abhyāsa viṣayaḥ sā upāyam anyat tarhi idam śābdāt jñānam vidhīyate pralīna grahaṇa grāhya vibhāga udgrāham advayam na hi bhinna artha saṃsarga rūpa vākya artha dhī padam ātma tattvam niṣprapañcam iti etat api pelavam advaya ātma prakāśaḥ asau anavaccheda vibhramaḥ sva ātma sthitiḥ su praśāntā phalam tat na vidheḥ padam tad sādhana avabodhe hi vidhātṛ vyāpṛtiḥ matā apekṣita upāya tā eva vidhiḥ iṣṭaḥ manīṣibhiḥ tatas hi adhyavasāya ādiḥ na akasmāt na abhidhānataḥ 
[115,iii^1]	na brūmaḥ śabda utthaḥ tattva bodhaḥ vidhīyate iti kim tu pratyasta mita buddhi bodhya bheda avagrahaḥ atas ca advayaḥ dvitīya tadvidha bodha abhāvāt vā pramātṛ prameya dvaya virahāt vā tatas anyaḥ tasya ca alaukikasya pramāṇa antarāt utpatti upāyasya anavagamāt saha upāyaiḥ śama dama manana dhyāna brahmacarya ādibhiḥ vidhānam yatas na śābda jñāna viṣayaḥ ātma tattvam vākya lakṣaṇaḥ hi śabdaḥ pramāṇam tasya ca viṣayaḥ nānā padārtha saṃsarga ātmā tad anugamena pratīteḥ tat jñānasya ca vividha artha mātra saṃbheda avabhāsasya ātma tattvam niṣprapañcam dvaita leśena api anavamṛṣṭam katham gocaraḥ syāt iti etat api asāram yatas yaḥ asau advayaḥ dvaita leśa saṃsparśa vikalaḥ ātma tattva bodhaḥ saḥ avaccheda vibhrānti virahāt tasya svarūpa avasthānam 
[115,iii^2]	avaccheda kaluṣa tayā hi tad anātma rūpeṇa prakāśate na tu tatas anyaḥ tattva bodhaḥ satyam jñānam anantam iti śruteḥ ātma tattvam ca praśānta śoka ādi viśvāśivam apahata pāpma ādi śruteḥ prakāśamānān atiśaya ānandam vijñānam ānandam brahma eṣaḥ asya paramaḥ ānandaḥ etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti iti śrutibhyaḥ tathā ca tad svarūpa sthitiḥ viśva aśiva upaśamāt niratiśaya āhlāda avāpteḥ ca suṣṭhu praśānta aparaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ phalam uktam ca ātma lābhāt na param vidyate iti na ca puruṣa arthe api ajñāta upāye na pravartate iti yuktam yatas pravṛtteḥ pūrvarūpam icchā 
[115,iii^3]	tathā ca tad vāreṇa pravṛtti upadeśa kvacid atha atas dharma jijñāsā tathā yaḥ hi yat icchati sa tat karoti iti uktam api ca ajñāta upāye ced na pravartate avaśyam upāya jñāpanayā tatra pravartyaḥ phalam uddiśya tāvatā ca tatra api pravṛtti siddheḥ na vidhāyakasya tatra vyāpāraḥ āśrayitavyaḥ tat uktam tasya lipsā artha lakṣaṇāḥ iti tasmāt phala sādhanaḥ eva vidhi vyāpāraḥ nanu phalavatī api artha lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ kva tarhi vidhi vyāpāraḥ itthaṃbhāve na etat sāram yatas yathā eva sādhana sāmānye arthāt pravṛttiḥ tathā itthaṃbhāva sāmānye api yatas na ananugrahakam sādhanam samartham atha tad viśeṣe pravartyaḥ sādhana viśeṣe api tathā astu 
[115,iii^4]	api ca apekṣita upāya tā eva vidhiḥ tasyāḥ apravṛtta pravartanā lakṣaṇa tvāt pravṛtti hetoḥ ca dharmasya pravartanā śabda abhidheya tvāt iṣṭa tāyāḥ tad sādhana tāyāḥ ca anyasya pravṛtti hetoḥ abhāvāt iṣṭa tāyāḥ ca pramāṇa antara avaseya tvāt svayam pravṛtteḥ jānāti eva asau mayā etat kartavyam iti na iṣṭatāyāma pravṛtta pravartanātvam iṣṭa sādhana tāyām tu pramāṇa antara avagama abhāvāt śabda eka gamyāyām na śabdam antareṇa apravṛtta puruṣa pravṛtti hetu tvam atas sā śabda pramāṇikā satī vidhiḥ iti gīyate anutiṣṭhataḥ ca sādhanam anuṣṭheyam pravṛtti hetuḥ na svabhāva siddham tena anutiṣṭhataḥ sādhana tā vidhiḥ atas anuṣṭhānam sādhana viṣayam eva vidhāyakāt śabdāt gamyate 
[117,i^1]	nanu adhyavasāyaḥ ākūtam ādyā pravṛttiḥ kāla traya viyuktam pravṛtti mātram ajñāta kriyā kartṛ saṃbandhaḥ iti vidhi vidaḥ vidhim vyācakṣate na etat sāram yatas adhyavasāya ādīnām eva hetuḥ atra mṛgyate sa ca na anyaḥ apekṣita upāya tāyāḥ na ca te nirasta hetavaḥ syāt etat abhidhānam eṣām hetuḥ tat ca vārtam abhidhānāt hi pratītiḥ eṣām syāt na utpattiḥ na hi pratīti mātreṇa ghaṭa ādayaḥ pravṛtti hetavaḥ ityādi varṇitam vidhi viveke athavā na abhidhānataḥ na ca śabdāt adhi avasāya ādiḥ jñāpaka tvāt avyutpanna pravṛtti prasaṅgāt ityādi tatra eva uktam athavā yaḥ manyate mayā idam kartavyam iti yatas adhyavasāyaḥ niyuktaḥ asmi iti yatas buddhiḥ sa niyogaḥ vidhi śabda paryāyaḥ iti tam pratyucyate 
[117,i^2]	tatas eva apekṣita upāya tvāt kartavyam iti adhyavasāyaḥ tathā hi kartuḥ iṣṭa abhyupāye kartavyam iti loke buddhiḥ tad abhāve tu akartavyam iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām te ca tad viṣaye gamyete tathā niyuktaḥ asmi iti pravartitaḥ asmi iti sva ātma pravṛtti hetu pratītiḥ na ca saḥ anyaḥ iṣṭa abhyupāya tāyāḥ na khalu dṛṣṭa sāmarthye akasmāt vinā hetunā hetuḥ iti yuktimat na hi tam parityajya laukikam alaukika kalpane pramāṇam asti kutas ca na abhidhānataḥ na khalvalaukikasya abhidhānam saṃbhavati saṃbandha agrahāt iti uktam atha vā tatas hi adhyavasāya prārambha anuṣṭhāna parisamāpanāḥ apekṣita upāya tvāt tad sadbhāvaḥ eva niyukta pravṛtteḥ yasya kasyacid niyogāt apravṛtteḥ 
[118,i]	syāt etat kartavyam iti pratyayāt pravartate anyathā kartavyam na kṛtam syāt tat ca na na akasmāt kartavya pratyaya utpādaḥ sa hi sva artha avāpti nimittaḥ syāt etat śabdāt eva kartavyatā buddhiḥ tatra ucyate na abhidhānataḥ na śabdāt kartavya tā buddhiḥ niyogaḥ hi śabda arthaḥ sa hi niyoktṛ dharmaḥ svatantraḥ vā syāt kartavyatā tu viṣaya dharmaḥ atha viṣaya dharmam niyogam brūyāt prāptam apekṣita upāya tvam atha niyogāt kartavya tā syāt evam api na tasyām śabdaḥ pramāṇam sākṣāt tasya niyoga abhidhāyi tvāt na api arthāt akartavye api anāpta niyoga darśanāt atha niyogasya kārya tā gamyate tad niṣpatti adhīnā iti viṣaye kartavyatā avagamaḥ tat asat viṣaye kārya tā pratīteḥ loke tathā hi gauḥ duhyatām tvayā iti niyoge anyena dugdhāyām na punar doham ārabhate viṣayasya kārya tā pratīteḥ tasya niṣpādita tvāt na ca anyena eva niyogaḥ niṣpāditaḥ tasya aniyukta tvāt tatra niyoga siddhaye punar doha ārambhaḥ syāt vistareṇa ca ayam arthaḥ vidhi viveke vicāritaḥ iti alam ati prasaṅgena 
[118,ii^1]	syāt etat asya jñānasya mokṣa sādhana tvāt vidhānam vidyā sādhyaḥ hi mokṣaḥ śrūyate vidyayā tadā ārohanti vidyayā amṛtam aśnute yaḥ tam ātmānam anuvidya vijānāti sa sarvān ca kāmān tathā sa yadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ bhavati saṃkalpāt eva asya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhanti ityādi na ca sādhya tve api antavat tvam śabda gamya tvāt anāvṛtteḥ na ca punar āvartate iti na hi eṣa tarka gamyaḥ yena tarkeṇa asya tattvam vyavasthāpyeta śabda gamyasya tu śabdāt eva tattva vyavasthā ananta vidyā asādhya tvāt vā ananta tvam kṣaṇika tve api ca vijñānasya saṃtati rūpeṇa ananta tvam tatra āhuḥ na ca mokṣaḥ phalam tasya sādhyaḥ mokṣaḥ na ca aparaḥ avidyā astamayaḥ mokṣaḥ sā saṃsāraḥ udāhṛtā vidyā eva ca advayā śāntā tad astamayaḥ ucyate kaḥ punar eṣa mokṣaḥ yadi anāgata deha indriya buddhi anutpādaḥ aśarīram vāvasantam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti darśanāt sa prāgabhāvaḥ na sādhyaḥ 
[118,ii^2]	atha brahma prāptiḥ sā caitra grāmayoḥ iva vā syāt jīva brahmaṇoḥ mārga śrutibhyaḥ śatam ca ekā ca hṛdayasya nāḍyaḥ tāsām mūrdhānam abhi nissṛtā ekā tayā ūrdhvamāyan amṛta tvam eti sa yāvat kṣipyet manaḥ tāvat ādityam gacchati etat vai khalu loka dvāram tathā te arciṣam abhisaṃbhavati arciṣaḥ ahar ityādi yathā vā madhuni nānā kusuma rasānām samudre ca nadīnām prāptiḥ avibhāga lakṣaṇā tathā syāt yathā loke madhukṛtaḥ madhu kurvanti iti yathā somya imāḥ nadyaḥ iti darśanāt kāryasya vā kāraṇa bhāva āpattiḥ tathā vidvān puṇya pāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti iti śruteḥ tad rūpa pariṇāma lakṣaṇā vā yoga vyāghra vat sa yaḥ ha vai tat paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati iti darśanāt brahma saṃpadyate iti ca sphaṭikasya iva rāga apakarṣaṇena sva rūpa prāpti lakṣaṇā param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti śravaṇāt 
[120,i^1]	tatra na tāvat prathamaḥ kalpaḥ sarva gata tvāt tad antarasya sarvasya nityam vibhum sarva gatam iti ananya tvāt ca tad vijñānena sarva vijñāna upadeśāt tat tvam asi iti sākṣāt pratipādanāt pratyagātma vṛttinā ca sarvatra ātma śabdena nirdeśāt atha yaḥ anyām iti bheda darśana apavādāt atas eva ca na dvitīyaḥ niravayava tvāt ca niṣkalam niṣkriyam iti paraspara avayava saṃbheda lakṣaṇasya avibhāgasya anupapatteḥ na api tṛtīyaḥ kāryasya sarvadā kāraṇa tvāt atha kārya rūpa nāśaḥ uccheda ātma tā prasaṅgaḥ mokṣasya tatra vidyayā amṛtam aśnute iti virodhaḥ vidyayā eva uccheda prasaṅgāt ātma ucchedasya ca aniṣṭa tvāt aphala tvam 
[120,i^2]	pratiṣiddhaḥ ca akṣaram iti atra mukhyaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheyam iti vikāra anṛta tva pratipādanāt śrutyā na caturthaḥ ananya tvāt eva caitanyasya ca brahma rūpasya aviśeṣāt atha vijñāna ātmanām śoka moha ādi abhāvaḥ viśiṣyate iti ced tatra api śoka ādayaḥ ced ātmānaḥ vijñāna ātmanām anucchedyāḥ atha guṇāḥ artha antaram āgama apāyinaḥ kṣaṇikāḥ kṣaṇika tvāt eva ca ucchidyante iti na tad sādhanam apekṣyam na ca āgāminām anutpattaye apekṣyate iti uktam atha aiśvarya viśeṣaḥ brahmaṇi tad prāptiḥ tad rūpa pariṇāmaḥ mokṣaḥ sa svarāj bhavati iti śruteḥ tat asat aneka īśvara anupapatteḥ 
[120,i^3]	brahmaṇaḥ nyūnam samam vā vijñāna ātmanām aiśvaryam syāt nyūna tvena brahma rūpāpattiḥ na svārājyam tathā hi brahma śabda vācyaḥ parameśvaraḥ teṣām adhipatiḥ syāt tathā ca anya rāja tā tatra ca antava tvam śrūyate atha ye anyathā atas viduḥ anya rājānaḥ te kṣayya lokāḥ bhavanti iti upapadyate ca parameśvara icchayā nyūna aiśvaryāṇām aiśvarya pracyuti darśanāt loke samatvasya tu anapapattiḥ eva yugapad ekaḥ ced sarva adhipatiḥ sarvasya praśāsitā paraḥ kim kurvan īśaḥ syāt virodhāt ca na khalu eṣām ekam ati tve hetuḥ asti tatra ekasmin vastuni viruddha abhiprāyayoḥ eka abhiprāya anuvidhāyi tve tasya itarasya anīśvara tvam 
[120,i^4]	ubhaya anuprāya anuvidhānam na virodhāt ubhayoḥ ananuvidhāne anīśvara tvam ubhayoḥ kārya asiddhaḥ ceda ekamatye hetuḥ pariṣadvat anyathā tasya āsiddheḥ iti ced pratyekam anīśvara tvam atha paryāyeṇa aiśvaryam avirodhāya ucyate antavat tā jagat sargasya ca asaṃbhavāt na brahma tulyam aiśvaryam yatas paraḥ eva jagat sarge śrūyate tad upāsanena sarga uttara kālaḥ apavargaḥ iti tasmāt sphaṭikasya iva rāga ādi apakarṣaṇena svarūpa āvirbhāvaḥ brahma prāptiḥ brahma rūpa tvāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ tathā ca param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti uktam anya rūpa niṣpattau sva śabda anupapatteḥ niṣpadyamānasya abhedāt saṃbandhāt vopapattiḥ iti ced 
[120,i^5]	na viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyāt sarvasya tasya niṣpadyamānasya sva tvāt tatra yathā mala apagame śuklam eva sat vastram śuklam jātam iti ucyate tathā moha āvaraṇa vigame svarūpa āvirbhāve svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti ucyate tathā brahma eva san brahma apyeti iti tat evam sva rūpa sthiti lakṣaṇa tvāt mohasya na kārya tā prāk api svarūpasya bhāvāt āgantukasya asva rūpa tvāt na ca anya tvam yatas avidyā apagamaḥ eva uktena prakāreṇa muktiḥ avidyā saṃsāraḥ vidyā eva ca avidyā nivṛttiḥ yadi agrahaṇam avidyā yatas bhāvaḥ eva abhāva vyāvṛttiḥ atha viparyāsaḥ tathā api virodhita tattva jñāna udayaḥ eva tad nivṛttiḥ 
[120,i^6]	na hi śuktikā jñāna utpādāt anyā rajata jñāna nivṛttiḥ tad sādhyā prayatna antara sādhyāḥ vā tayoḥ yaugapadyāt prayatna antara anapekṣaṇāt ca tathā ca vidyā brahma prāptyoḥ tulya kālatā śrūyate brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati iti tathā ānandam brahmaṇaḥ vidvān na bibheti tadā ātmānam eva avedaham brahma asmi iti tasmāt tat sarvam abhavat tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam anupaśyataḥ veda bhavati vidvān na bibheti kaḥ mohaḥ paśyate iti paurvāparya aśravaṇāt yat tu kvacid paurvāparyam tat vyādāya svapiti iti yathā nanu eka tve tulya kāla tā api anupapannā na ekasya api vastunaḥ bhāva abhāva rūpeṇa vyapadeśāt tathā yadā ghaṭaḥ naśyati tadā kapālāni jāyante iti 
[120,i^7]	katham tarhi mārga avibhāga sarga apyayā aiśvarya śrutayaḥ tatra āhuḥ na mārga śrutayaḥ nirupādhi viśuddha brahma vidyā viṣayāḥ yatra hi sarva upādhi viśuddham asthūla ādikam brahma upāsyam tatra brahma eva san brahmā apyeti na tasmāt prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti atra eva samavanīyante iti prāṇān utkramaṇena vijñāna ātmanaḥ eva āgatiḥ ucyate na hi tad agamane tad upādheḥ tasya brahmaṇaḥ bhedena vijñāna ātma tvam yatra tu manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ bhārūpaḥ iti sa upādhi upāsyam tad viṣayāḥ tāḥ yatra etat śrūyate araḥ ca ha vai ṇyaḥ ca arṇavau brahma loke tṛtīyasya amitas divi tadaiḥ aṃmadīyam saraḥ tat aśvatthaḥ soma savanaḥ tad aparājitā pūrbrahmaṇaḥ prabhu vimitam hiraṇmayam veśmaḥ iti 
[120,i^8]	tathā ca abrahma vidām api tad gati śravaṇam ye ca amī araṇye śraddhām satyam tapaḥ iti upāsate iti para brahma prāptiḥ tu na abrahma vidām yujyate vidyayā tadā ārohanti yatra kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ na tatra dakṣiṇāḥ yānti na avidvāṃsaḥ tapasvinaḥ iti tathā tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum eti iti vacanāt apunarāvṛtti śrutiḥ tarhi katham atra kecid manyate krama mukti āśrayaṇāt tat prāpya tatra utpanna nirupādhi tattva jñānāḥ param padam aśnuvate yathā uktam vedānta vijñāna su niścita arthāḥ saṃnyāsa yogāt yatayaḥ śuddha sattvāḥ te brahma lokeṣu para anta kāle para amṛtāḥ parimucyanti sarve 
[123,i^1]	brahma lokeṣu iti kārya brahma loka nirdeśaḥ bahuvacanāt tatra avayava dvāreṇa bahutva upapatteḥ para anta kālaḥ mahāpralayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sva adhikāra paryavasānam tasmin para amṛtāḥ para brahma rūpeṇa amṛtāḥ santaḥ saṃnyāsa yogāt bhedena parameśvare sva kṛtānām karmaṇām phalānām ca saṃnyāsāt yogāt ca sarvam idam kartṛ ādi brahma iti upāsanāt tathā ca smṛtiḥ brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare parasya ante kṛtātmānaḥ praviśanti param padam anye tu manyate yathā candra loke yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā sthitaḥ eva tasmin bhukta bhogāḥ āvartante na evam sthitaḥ eva brahma loke tatas āvṛttiḥ kim tu tad pralaya paryavasānā tatra sthitiḥ tad pralaye hi na tatas āvṛttaḥ bhavati tatas ca anāvṛttiḥ śrūyate 
[123,i^2]	tathā ca imam mānavam āvartam na āvartante iti imam iha iti viśeṣaṇam amṛta tvam eti iti amṛta tvam āpekṣikam yathā amṛtāḥ devāḥ iti tathā ca paurāṇika smaraṇam ābhūtasaṃplavam sthānam amṛta tvam hi bhāṣyate iti yat tu manyate sarva gata tve api brahmaṇaḥ vikṛta avikṛta bhedaḥ tatas ca deśa bhedaḥ tathā ca avikṛtasya brahmaṇaḥ deśa bhedaḥ śrūyate atha yat atas paraḥ divaḥ jyotiḥ dīpyate iti atas avikṛtasya niyata deśasya brahmaṇaḥ prāptaye yujyate mārga viśeṣaḥ tad saṃpradhāryam na tāvat anutpannā dvaya viśuddha vidyasya ayam mārgaḥ brahma vidaḥ śravaṇāt na api vidyāvataḥ vidyā udaye nikhila bheda ucchedāt iti madhunadī nidarśana avibhāga śrutiḥ api viveka jñāna abhāva parā na tu tadvidhaḥ eva avibhāgaḥ 
[124,i^1]	sarga śrutayaḥ api na sarga parāḥ kim tarhi eka ātma tattva pratipatti pradhānāḥ tatas tad anuguṇa tayā eva tāsām artha vyavasthānam na tu tad virodhena tathā hi kasmin nu bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti eka tvena upakramāt aitat ātmyam idam sarvam tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti upasaṃhārāt eka tvena eva aikātmya tattva pratipatti param ekam idam vākyam gamyate tatra yadi aparaḥ tejaḥ prabhṛti tattva sargaḥ satyatayā vidhīyeta vākya bhedaḥ syāt atas yathā upāṃśu yāja vākye ajāmi tva upakrama upasaṃhāre viṣṇuḥ upāṃśu yaṣṭavyaḥ ityādīni vacāṃsi vākya bheda doṣāt pṛthagvidhi tvam alabhamānāni tādarthyāt tad ānukūlyena stuti artha tayā vyavatiṣṭhante tathā sarga śrutayaḥ api ekatva upāya tayā 
[124,i^2]	na ca viparītam śakyam vaktum ekatva śrutiḥ eva bheda pratipatti artha iti sarvatra eka tvena upakramāt upasaṃhārāt ca yena upakramyate yena ca upasaṃhriyate sa vākya arthaḥ bheda pratipatteḥ ca aphala tvāt eka tva pratipatteḥ tu dṛṣṭam śrutam ca phalam śoka ādi nivṛttaḥ viśuddha aikātmya darśanena tad avagamāt tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam anupaśyataḥ iti śravaṇāt phalavat aṅga tā ca aphalasya upāya tvam ca na ca idam jagat asat mūlam kim tarhi advitīya ekasat mūlam kāraṇa avyatirekāt ca kāryasya sat ekam eva idam ghaṭa ādi vat mṛd rūpeṇa hi ghaṭa ādayaḥ na eka tvam atikrāmanti nanu evam mukhyaḥ eva kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ uktaḥ syāt 
[124,i^3]	na etat ekatva avatāra upāya mātra tvāt na khalu atra kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva pratipādyaḥ yena asau yathāśabdam mukhyaḥ eva gṛhyeta ekatva upāyattvāt iti uktam eka tvam ca anena upāyena avatāryate puruṣaḥ sa ca mukhyaḥ pradhāna virodhī ekam eva advitīyam iti punar punar śruteḥ sarva bheda nirāsa paratvāt na śakyam vaktum kāraṇa ātmanā ekatvam kārya ātmanā nānātvam tat satyam saḥ ātmā iti ca kāraṇasya eva satya tva avadhāraṇāt anyatra ca indraḥ māyābhiḥ iti bhedasya māyā gamya tva śruteḥ sākṣāt ca bheda abhāvasya śravaṇāt na iha nānā asti kiñcanaḥ iti bheda abhedayoḥ ca virodhāt prāc anupapatteḥ varṇita tvāt tad avirodhena varṇyate tad upādāna mātra tayā bheda vikalpasya bimba pratibimba vat varṇa pada vākya ādi vat ca 
[124,i^4]	yathā hi na bimbāt pratibimbānām utpattiḥ nānā rūpāṇām bimba upādāna mātra tayā pratibimba bheda vikalpasya na hi bimbāt para sparataḥ vā vyāvṛttāni kānicid vastūni pratibimbāni bimba upādānam tu tat nānā nirbhāsa mātram tathā na varṇebhyaḥ pada vākya prakaraṇa ādīni kānicid vastūni santi tad upādāna mātra tvāt tad kalpanāyāḥ varṇebhyaḥ padāni niṣpadyante padebhyaḥ vākyam iti ucyate api ca svapne api sṛṣṭiḥ śrūyate na tatra rathāḥ na ratha yogāḥ na panthānaḥ bhavanti atha rathān ratha yogān pathaḥ sṛjate iti tadvat eṣā syāt anya paratvāt svayam eva vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheyam iti vikāra asatya tayā na pāramārthikī iti uktam 
[126,i_126,ii^1]	aiśvarya śrutiṣu api sva guṇa vidyā vipākaḥ ayam śrūyate saḥ ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati sarvān ca kāmān āpnoti sa svarāj bhavati iti na tu mokṣaḥ sa hi nirupādhi brahma vidyā nimittaḥ eva yat api kvacid apunarāvṛtti śravaṇam tasya api dvayī gatiḥ vyākhyātā iti ekam darśanam anye tu manyante āvirbhūta brahma rūpaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sarva ātma tvāt sarva īśitṛ tvāt ca sarva upabhogānām ca bhoktṛ tvāt tad ānanda mātrā rūpa tvāt deva ādi ānandānām sa sarvān ca lokān āpnoti sarvān ca kāmān sa svarāj bhavati iti tasya tad saṃkīrtanam brahma rūpa āvirbhāva lakṣaṇa mokṣa praśaṃsā artham nanu sarva ātma tvena sarva kāma avāptau sarva śoka moha ādi āptiḥ api syāt na teṣām abrahma rūpa tvāt avidyā adhyastatvāt jñāna aiśvarya ānanda bhogāḥ tu brahmaṇaḥ rūpam vijñānam ānandam brahma na anyaḥ atas asti draṣṭā etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti sarvasya īśānaḥ etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi iti ādi śrutibhyaḥ 
[126,ii^2]	tathā ca yat kiñcid īśvara tvam yat ca vijñānam yaḥ ca ānandaḥ brahma ādiṣu sthāvara anteṣu bhūteṣu brahmaṇi tāni tāni āvirbhūta brahma svarūpaḥ samaśnutaḥ iti yuktam loka ādayaḥ tu avidyā adhyaḥ tāḥ na brahma rūpam te katham āvirbhūta brahma svarūpam āskandeyuḥ nanu prapañca śūnyasya advaitasya brahma rūpasya jñeya abhāvāt īśita vyābhāvāt ca vijñānam aiśvaryam ca anupapannam tatra sarvajñaḥ sarveśvaraḥ iti api śrutī samādheye eva na etat sāram yatas na īśitavyakṛtam īśvara tvam jñeya kṛtam vā jñātṛ tvam kim tu siddhena jñāna rūpeṇa siddhayā ca īśana śaktyā jñeyam avāpnoti īśitavyam ca viniyuṅkte praśāsti ca prakāśa dāha vat 
[126,ii^3]	siddhena hi prakāśa rūpeṇa prakāśyam prakāśayati vivasvān na tu prakāśya adhīnam tasya prakāśa rūpam dāhya adhīnā vā agneḥ dāha śaktiḥ tathā ca tad caitanyena eva kṛtsnasya prapañcasya avabhāsanāt tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti na anyaḥ atas asti draṣṭā ityādi śruteḥ sarvajña tvam sarveśvara tvam api tad aiśvaryeṇa yathāyatham īśvaraiḥ īśitavyānām īśanāt evam ca eṣa bhūta adhipatiḥ eṣa lokapālaḥ iti brahma indra yama ādīnām ca aiśvaryam uktam sarva kāma avāptiḥ ca tadīya tvāt deva ādi ānandasya kāmeṣu ānanda prāptyā kāmāḥ āptāḥ bhavanti na sva rūpeṇa 
[126,ii^4]	evam sa tatra paryeti jakṣan krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ strībhiḥ vā iti varṇanīyam tad viṣaya ānanda bhogāt na tu strī ādi yogaḥ yathā ātma ratiḥ ātma krīḍaḥ ātma mithunaḥ iti na hi mukhyam ātma krīḍa tvam ātma mithuna tvam vā saṃbhavati yatas ca anavacchinnāni tadīyāni eva sarva bhūteṣu jñāna ādīni kalpita avacchedāni atas yatra yatra na atyantam avacchedaḥ samutkarṣāt teṣām tāni tāni pratyāsatteḥ bhūtāni ātma tvena bhagavān uktvā munīnām api aham vyāsaḥ ityādi upasaṃjahāra yat yat vibhūtimat sattvam iti tathā adṛṣṭam draṣṭṛ aśrutam śrotṛ ityādi sarva bhūta darśana ādīnām tad caitanya nibandhana tvāt 
[128,i]	anye tu āhuḥ yāvān kaścid parasminnāma rūpa āśrayaḥ vyapadeśaḥ sarvaḥ asau ādhyānāya yathā yaḥ asau āditye puruṣaḥ hiraṇya śmaśruḥ ityādi na hi sva mahima pratiṣṭhasya parasya deśa viśeṣa avarodhaḥ sarva viśeṣa atigasya ca rūpa viśeṣa yogaḥ paraḥ ca eṣaḥ sarva pāpma udaya śruteḥ uditaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥ iti ādhyānam tu tathā vidhīyate tathā sarvajña tvāt api draṣṭavyam iti tat evam brahma ātmanaḥ tad rūpa āvirbhāvaḥ tad prāptiḥ sa mokṣaḥ sā ca vidyā eva tasmāt na sādhyaḥ mokṣaḥ na ca vidyayā anyaḥ iti puṣkalam 
[128,ii^1]	atha matam mā bhūt mokṣaḥ sādhyaḥ bandha hetu kṣayaḥ tu sādhyate tad sādhanam ātma darśanam syāt śrūyate ca tasya phalam bandha hetūnām karmaṇām kṣayaḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare tathā tat yathā iṣīkātūlam agnau protam pradūyeta evam ha asya sarve pāpmānaḥ pradūyante pāpma śabdena puṇyam api saṃgṛhītam sāvadya phala tvāt anyatra ca na etam setum ahorātre tarataḥ na jarā na mṛtyuḥ na śokaḥ na sukṛtam na duṣkṛtam iti upakramya sarve pāpmānaḥ atas nivartante iti upasaṃhārāt na ca tat kṣayam antareṇa kṣema prāptiḥ atas avaśya kartavyaḥ na ca adatta phalasya karmaṇaḥ na kṣayaḥ prāyaścittānām doṣa saṃyogena codyamānānām tad kṣaya phala tvāt tasmāt prāyaścittaiḥ iva vidyayā bandha hetu kṣayaḥ sādhyate sā eva ca muktiḥ bandhana viśleṣa artha tvāt muceḥ 
[128,ii^2]	evam ca na antava tva doṣaḥ pradhvaṃsasya kāryasya api avināśāt tatra ucyate prāyaścitta diśā bandha hetu ucchedaḥ api no tatas sarva avidyā pravilaye na cchedyam avaśiṣyate bandha hetuḥ avidyā ātmā vidyāyām sā astam āgatā bandha hetu dhvaṃsaḥ api na ātma darśana sādhyaḥ tat hi vidadhat eva nikhila avidyā vyavahāra pravilayam udīyate karma phala bhoga vibhāgaḥ ca avidyā upādānaḥ tatra anavayavena unmūlitāyām avidyāyām na cchettavyam asti avidyā adhyastāni hi karmāṇi tad samucchede vidyayā samucchinnāni eva bhavanti tad vipākasya avakāśaḥ eva na asti advaitam ātma tattvam paśyataḥ bheda darśana āśraya tvāt tasya yatas ca avidyā ucchedena eva karma ucchedaḥ atas tulya vat saṃśaya viparyāsābhyām prasaṃkhyātāni karmāṇi bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare 
[129,i^1]	nanu evam karma kṣayāmi upagame tattva darśana samanantaram eva muktiḥ syāt na dehapāta pratīkṣā tasya tāvat eva ciram yāvat na vimokṣe atha saṃpatsye iti deha pāta pratīkṣā śrutiḥ bādhyeta yasya tu vidyā tad kṣaya sādhanam śāstrāt gamyate tasya tad anusāreṇa keṣāñcid kṣayaḥ vidyayā keṣāñcid upabhogena tatra kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi iti aviśeṣāt sarva kṣaya prasaṅge tasya tāvat eva ciram iti deha pāta a adhi śravaṇāt mukteḥ ārabdha kāryāṇām pravṛtta bhogānām na tatas kṣayaḥ bhogena eva kṣayaḥ iti gamyate na hi sarva kṣaye dehapāta pratīkṣā upapadyate 
[129,i^2_130,i]	tat uktam anārabdha kārye eva tu pūrve tad avadheḥ bhogena tu itare kṣapayitvā saṃpadyate iti vidyayā tu avidyā uccheda karma vipāka vyavahāra ucchittau aviśeṣāt sarva ucchedaḥ iti sapadyeva mucyeta na eva doṣaḥ na hi iyam śrutiḥ cira kālatā viśiṣṭam dehapāta vadhim mukteḥ āha kim tu kṣipra tām yathā kaścid kṣepīyaḥ tam pratipādayan bravīti kvacid kārye etāvat me ciram yat snātaḥ bhuñjānasya ca evam iyam api anyathā tāvat eva iti na vācyam syāt ciram iti eva brūyāt tāvat eva iti tu vacanāt kṣaiprya para tā gamyate atas kṣiprā eva muktiḥ na pratīkṣaṇīyam asti dehapāta pratīkṣā tu tatra na antarīyaka tvāt bhavati eva atha vā cira tvam anūdya dehapāta avadhi tvam atra ucyate anyathā cira tve avadhi viśeṣe ca ucyamāne vākyam bhidyeta tatra ayam arthaḥ yadi kasyacid ciram tāvat eva yāvat na vimokṣye iti 
[130,ii]	nanu pūrvasmin pakṣe tattva jñāna anantara tvāt dehapātasya sthita prajña lakṣaṇa abhidhānam na yujyate sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣā ityādi dvitīyaḥ api sarva kṣaye cira tva anupapatteḥ tatra avadhi viśeṣa vidhāna ayogāt anupapannaḥ ucyate sthita prajñaḥ tāvat na vigalita nikhila avidyaḥ siddhaḥ kim tu sādhakaḥ eva avasthā viśeṣam prāptaḥ syāt na ca brūmaḥ brahma vedanā anantaraḥ eva deha viyogaḥ kim tu ārabdha kārya karma kṣayam bhogena pratīkṣate iti tatra kasyacid tad kālaḥ apavargaḥ kasyacid kiyān citkṣepaḥ yathā rajjvām sarpa samāropa samuttha bhaya janmānaḥ vepathu prabhṛtayaḥ tattva darśanāt apāvṛte bhaye kasyacid tadā eva nivartante kasyacid kiyan tañcitkālam anuvartante tad saṃskārāt tathā sarva karma kṣaye api bhujyamāna vipāka saṃskāra anuvṛtti nibandhanā śarīra sthitiḥ kulāla vyāpāra vigamaḥ iva cakra bhrāntiḥ 
[131,i^1]	nanu evam brahma vidaḥ api ced bhokra ādi vibhāga darśanam anuvartate deha pātāt uttara kālam api anuvarteta tatra viduṣaḥ api na avaśyaṃbhāvi kaivalyam syāt tathā ca tāvat eva ciram iti śrutyā virodhaḥ atha ucchedāt avidyāyāḥ na anuvṛttiḥ kṣaṇam api na syāt iti saḥ eva virodhaḥ sā eṣā ubhayataḥpāśāḥ rajjuḥ ucyate yathā bhaya vigame labdha āśvāsasya api saṃskāra mātrāt kampā ādi anuvṛttiḥ na ca bhaya vigame api anuvṛttiḥ iti etāvatā cira kālā bhavati na ca mūla kāraṇa tulya phalaḥ saṃskāraḥ na ca sthāyī anyathā kampa ādīnām nivṛttiḥ eva na syāt na ca bhaya vigama hetoḥ tattva darśanāt tad nivṛttaye hetu antaram apekṣate 
[131,i^2]	tatas eva hi sa krameṇa nivartate svayam eva vā kulāla cakra bhrānti saṃskāra vat tathā nivṛttāyām avidyāyām karmasu ca aviśeṣeṇa ārabdha kāryeṣu anārabdha kāryeṣu ca nivṛtteṣu ārabdha vipāka saṃskārāt śarīriṇam bhoktāram iva ca ayam ātmānam pratyetya ābhāsa mātreṇa vidvān api na tu avidvān iva ārūḍha abhiniveśaḥ sa ca ayam īdṛśaḥ sthita prajñaḥ varṇitaḥ vīta kāmaḥ ātma rūpa saṃtuṣṭaḥ duḥkheṣu cchāyā mātra rūpeṣu tattva darśanāt abhiniveśāt kṛtrimebhyaḥ iva vyāghra ādibhyaḥ anudvigna manāḥ sukheṣu ca kṛtrima ramaṇīyeṣu iva vigata spṛhaḥ yathā khalu a viduṣaḥ mṛd dāru racite strī ādau viṣaye chāyā mātra darśanam abhiniveśa vikalam tathā viduṣaḥ kṣīṇa karma avidyasya tad saṃskāra mātrāt darśanam chāyā mātreṇa eva viṣayeṣu 
[131,i^3]	tathā ca tat yathā ahi nirlvayanī valmīke mṛtā pratyastā śayīta evam eva idam śarīram iti viduṣaḥ śarīre anāsthām darśayati yatas na mūla kāraṇa tulya phalaḥ saṃskāraḥ kampa ādi vat eva na ca cira kāla anuvṛttiḥ alpa kāla sthāyi tvāt saṃskārasya tadvat eva ca na tad nivṛttaye hetu antaram apekṣyate tattva darśanāt eva krameṇa tasya api nivṛtteḥ svayam eva vā sā ca iyam avasthā jīvanmuktiḥ iti gīyate ārabdha kārya karma saṃskāra kṣayaḥ ca dehapātāt eva gamyate tad anuvṛttau dehapātaḥ eva na syāt iti na dehapāta uttara kāle tad vipākasya chāyā mātreṇa api darśanam śakyate yena hi karmaṇā yat śarīram ārabdham tatra eva tad vipāka śeṣa ābhāsaḥ anārabdha kāryāṇām tu alabdha vṛttīnām eva nivṛtta tvāt na asti tad saṃskāraḥ 
[131,i^4]	labdha vṛtti kāraṇa saṃskārāt hi kārya leśa anuvṛttiḥ na khalu bhaye apratilabdha vṛttau anupajanita kampa ādau tad saṃskārāt kampa ādi anuvṛttiḥ tasmāt anārabdha kāryāṇām anālabdha vṛtti tvāt ārabdha kārya saṃskāra kṣayasya ca deha pātāt avagamāt viduṣaḥ patite asmin śarīre kaivalyam avaśyaṃbhāvi atra ca labdha vṛtti kāraṇa saṃskārāt vā kārya śeṣaḥ kārya saṃskārāt eva vā tathā ubhaya saṃskārāt eva vā kampa ādi anuvṛttiḥ bhaya saṃskārāt vā bhayam tatas kampa ādayaḥ kampa ādi saṃskārāt vā kampa ādi anuvṛttiḥ sarvathā bhavati kāraṇa vigame api kārya śeṣa anuvṛttiḥ saṃskārāt atas labdha vṛtti karma saṃskārāt tad vipākāt vā viduṣaḥ api śarīra sthitiḥ tat uktam tantra antare api tiṣṭhati saṃskāra vaśāt cakra bhrama vat dhṛta śarīraḥ iti 
[132,i]	ye tu manyante pravṛtta bhogānām karmaṇām pravṛtta vegasya iṣoḥ iva cakrasya iva vā na śakyaḥ pratibandhaḥ atas bhogena kṣaya pratīkṣā iti tat asat śakyaḥ hi iṣuḥ pratibandhum kuḍya ādibhiḥ nāśayitum ca ccheda ādibhiḥ svapna ādi sūcita upasthita vipāka vartamāna deha bhogya karma kṣaya arthāni ca śāntikāni karmāṇi tasmāt saṃskārāt eva sthitiḥ 
[133,i^1]	nanu saṃskāra kāryaśeṣau avidyā eva tatra katham sarva avidyā pravilayaḥ katham vā na cchedyam avaśiṣyate ucyate viśuddha aikātmya darśana pratipakṣa grastau vilīnau eva tāvat uditau akiñcitkara tvāt abandha tvāt tad nivṛttaye hetu antarasya anapekṣaṇāt viśuddham khalvātmānam sākṣāt anubhavataḥ vipāka ābhāsaḥ tamaspṛśan akiñcitkaraḥ bandha ātmā pralīnaḥ eva yathā citra ādau citra ādi tattvam anubhavataḥ strī ādi ābhāsaḥ rāga ādīnām animitta tvāt tathā avadātam ātmānam jānataḥ viparītam vā khaḍga ādiṣu śyāma ādi ābhāse utpannaḥ api tattva darśanāt avakāśam alabhamānaḥ pravilīnaḥ eva tathā ca na tad nibandhanena malina tvena śocati ātmānam na tejasvitayā abhinandati 
[133,i^2]	avabhāsamānayoḥ api tayoḥ ātmani tattva darśana pratihata avabhāsa tvāt evam ca yat ucyate karmaṇaḥ vā śarīra sthitiḥ syāt saṃskārāt vā kaḥ viśeṣaḥ kaḥ ca karmaṇaḥ kṣayaḥ kārya anuvṛttau tad nivṛttyā hi tad kṣayaḥ gamyate tasmāt bhogena tu itare kṣapayitvā saṃpadyate iti eva yuktam tat api apāstam karma vipākaḥ hi ātma saṃsparśī śoka abhinandana vān aviduṣaḥ viduṣaḥ tu tad asaṃsparśāt ābhāsa mātram maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādi nibandhana viśeṣa vat na vipākaḥ anabhinandyamāna tvāt at viṣyamāṇa tvāt ca tathā ca tat tat prāpya śubha aśubham na abhinandati na dveṣṭi iti darśitam tathā yasyām jāgrati bhūtāni sā niśā paśyataḥ muneḥ paśyate eva śarīra ādi prapañcaḥ niśā tad asaṃsparśāt adṛśyamāna sama tvāt 
[134,i^1]	nanu tattva jñāna pratihataḥ ced utpannaḥ api prapañca avabhāsaḥ na ātma saṃsparśī na kiñcitkaraḥ na bandhaḥ śabdāt eva tasya utpatteḥ kim artham upāsana ādi ucyate parokṣa rūpam śābda jñānam pratyakṣa rūpaḥ prapañca avabhāsaḥ tena tayoḥ avirodhena prapañca avabhāsaḥ na ātma asaṃsparśī na akiñcitkaraḥ na na bandhaḥ yathā pramāṇa antarāt avasīyamāna mādhurye api dravye pratyakṣa sarūpa indriya dvāraḥ tikta avabhāsaḥ adravya saṃsparśī na ābhāsa mātra tayā avatiṣṭhate tathā ca tat dravyam parama artha tiktam iva anavasita mādhuryam iva duḥkhāya bhavati upāsana ādinā sākṣātkṛtātma tattvasya tu virodhāt san api prapañca avabhāsaḥ na ātma saṃsparśī devadattaḥ iva siṃha avabhāsaḥ 
[134,i^2]	siṃhaḥ devadattaḥ iti samārope avabhāsamānaḥ api tat asaṃsparśī akiñcitkaraḥ na bhaya hetuḥ nityaḥ ca ātma tattva prakāśaḥ tatra na punar vipayarya avakāśaḥ asti śābdam tu pramāṇa adhīnam kṣaṇikam jñānam tatra punar api viparyaya avakāśaḥ dṛṣṭam hi pramāṇa an anusandhāne punar sarpa bhrāntyā rajjoḥ bhayam atha atra api satatam śābdam jñānam anusaṃdadhīta kim anyat upāsanam asmāt tasmāt bandha hetu chedaḥ api vidyā eva na tayā sādhyaḥ evam uttara agha āśleṣe api vācyam yathā puṣkara palāśaḥ āpaḥ na śliṣyante evam evaṃvidi pāpam karma na śliṣyate iti kartṛ karma pravibhāgasya vidyayā pravilayāt evam na vidyāyāḥ aneka phala kalpanā bhaviṣyati vartamāna apadeśānām ca phala vidhi tvena na vipariṇatiḥ iti 
[134,ii]	yat uktam na śābda jñāna viṣayaḥ brahma iti tatra ucyate na brahma śabda dhī gamyam yadi aśakyaḥ dhiyaḥ vidhiḥ dhī viśeṣa prarūpāya na asiddhaḥ viṣayaḥ kṣamaḥ vidhiḥ na arūpita padaḥ dhī mātram na vidhīyate na khalu jñāna mātram vidhīyate jñāna viśeṣa vastu na ca aprasiddhe anirūpite tatra niyogaḥ na hi aprasiddhe viṣaye niyoktum śakyate jñānasya ca viśeṣaḥ artha dvāraḥ na ca aprasiddhaḥ arthaḥ tad viśeṣa nirūpaṇāya prabhuḥ na ca ātma rūpasya śabdāt anyatas siddhiḥ śabdāt api ced na siddhiḥ tad dvāra jñāna viśeṣa asiddhau viṣaya anupapatteḥ niyoga anupapattiḥ 
[135,i]	api ca jñāna viśeṣa vidhi vādinaḥ ātma tattve prāmāṇyam eva hīyate iti darśayati vidhiḥ sva siddhi niṣṭhaḥ vā kriyā siddhi paraḥ athavā advaita brahma tattvasya pratipattiḥ ahetukā viniyogāt adhigatiḥ yāsyā jñāna kriyā artha tā atatparā na pramāṇam sārthavāda uttha buddhi vat vidhiḥ kriyā gocara tvāt na dravye vyāpṛti kṣamaḥ sattā anvayāt tu tad siddhiḥ pratyuta iti sa duṣyati viśiṣṭāni akriyā bodhaḥ pramāṇam na viśeṣaṇe pratipattiḥ viśiṣṭā api viṣayasya niyogataḥ sattām na sādhayati eva samāropeṇa saṃbhavāt yadi tāvat niyogasya eva kārya tā pratīyeta tadā sa sva niṣpattau paryavasitaḥ saha śabdena atha viniyogāt viṣaye kartavyatā avagamaḥ tathā api viṣaya siddhau ubhayathā na vastu tattvam saṃspṛśati tatra advaita ātma tattva pratipattiḥ apramāṇikā syāt 
[135,ii^1]	syāt etat yaḥ ātma apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ iti padānām sāmānādhikaraṇyena sambandhāt anyathā vā vastu tattva pratipattiḥ iti tat ca na anya paratvāt sā hi naḥ evam idam iti paryavasitā kim tu evam idam pratipattavyam iti kartavyatā niṣṭhā na vastu tattve pramāṇam vṛttānteṣu iva artha vāda uttha jñānam anya paratvāt na ca ātma tattvam eva vidheḥ viṣayaḥ tasya anuṣṭheya viṣaya tvāt kriyāyāḥ ca tathā abhāvāt siddha vatsva śabda upādāne ananuṣṭheye dravye vyāpāra ayogāt pratyuta avidheya kāla traya anyatama saṃspṛṣṭa satta anugamena dravya svarūpa siddhiḥ īdṛśam vastu abhūt asti bhaviṣyati vā iti tasmāt svarūpa siddhau duṣyati na hi vidheyasya kāla traye api sattā avagamaḥ 
[135,ii^2]	na hi yajeta iti ukte yāgasya bhūtakālā vartamāna kālā bhaviṣyat kālā vā sattā pratīyate nanu bhaviṣyat kāla avagamyate bhaviṣyat kāla viṣaya tvāt vidheḥ na etat na hi vihitam niyogataḥ anuṣṭhāsyate vihita akaraṇa doṣa abhāva prasaṃgāt nanu viśiṣṭa kriyā abhidhānam viśeṣaṇe api pramāṇam iṣyate yathā somena yajeta tathā aṅgadī kuṇḍalī vyūḍha uraskaḥ devadattasya putraḥ adhīte iti adhyayana kriyāvat sarvaḥ viśeṣaṇa kalāpaḥ pratīyate satyam viśiṣṭa kriyā pramāṇam viśeṣaṇe api pramāṇam anyatra pratipatteḥ pratipattiḥ hi viṣaya viṣeśa viśiṣṭā pramīyamāṇāḥ na viṣaya viśeṣasya sadbhāvam gamayati anyathā bhūte tathā ābhāsa samāropeṇa api saṃbhavāt asau vāva lokaḥ gautama agniḥ iti yathā dyu prabhṛtiṣu anagni dṛṣṭeḥ 
[136,i^1]	atra āha nanu naḥ viparīta arthāḥ dhīḥ pratīti virodhataḥ anāśvāsāt ca rajata pratyayaḥ rajate smṛtiḥ na khalu anyat anyathā pratīyate iti yuktam pratīti virodhāt katham anyasmin pratibhāsamāne anyaḥ viṣayaḥ anāśvāsāt ca viṣaya rūpa vyabhicāriṇi jñāne na tatas viṣaya niścayaḥ syāt api ca viṣaya rūpam ananukurvat aviṣayam anālambanam jñānam agrāhyam eva syāt jñāna hetu mātrasya anālambana tvāt cakṣuḥ ādi vat tathā ca āvedaka tvāt na anya apekṣāt api tatas artha siddhiḥ kim tarhi idam śukti saṃnikṛṣṭe cakṣuṣi rajatam iti smṛtiḥ sāmānya grahaṇāt bhrāntiḥ tarhi katham 
[136,i^2]	pratyakṣa smaryamāṇayoḥ viveka agrahaṇāt saḥ ayam bheda agrahaṇe abheda grahaṇa abhimānaḥ viveka rahitānām yathā dūrāt antarāla agrahaṇe vṛkṣa ādiṣu saṃśleṣa grahaṇa abhimānaḥ tasmāt smarāmi iti viveka śūnyā rajata smṛtiḥ eṣā atra ucyate na etat na hi pravarteta śuktikā śakale tadā rajate sā pravṛttiḥ ced na tasya asaṃnidhānataḥ asaṃnidhāna ābodhāt ced pravṛtti niyamaḥ kutas pravartate yat tatra eva tad tad saṃnidhi kāritam anyatra bheda grahaṇāt viveka agrahaṇāt tathā pravṛtti bhedaḥ sādṛśyāt viveka agrahaṇam yadi adṛṣṭeṣu pravarteta loṣṭa ādiṣu avivekataḥ 
[136,i^3]	 na tatra yadi tad buddhiḥ śuktikā śakale api na atha asti viparīta arthā khyātiḥ nihnūyate katham adṛṣṭa tvāt apravṛttiḥ śuktikā śakale samā dṛṣṭam tat yena rūpeṇa tad pravṛtteḥ akāraṇam dṛṣṭa smṛtauvivekāt ced idam atra parīkṣyatām tattva bodhāt atha atattva abodhāt rajata vedanāt dṛṣṭe pravṛttiḥ pūrvasmin viparīta artha tā mateḥ na dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭayoḥ bhedaḥ parasminna upayoginī sva yoga darśane te hi samāropa upayoginī na adṛṣṭe asaṃprayukte vā cākṣuṣaḥ syāt viparyayaḥ 
[136,i^4]	yadi cakṣuṣā saṃprayuktam śukti śakalam na rajatam iti pratīyāt rajatam vā tathā na śuktikā śakalaḥ āditsayā pravarteta rajata arthī tasya rajatam iti anavagateḥ loṣṭa ādi vat na ca smaryamāṇe rajate sā pravṛttiḥ tad deśa asaṃnidheḥ na hi pratītim upagate api vastuni yatra tasya asaṃnidhiḥ tatra tena arthī pravartate syāt etat rajatasya pratīteḥ asaṃnidheḥ ca apratīteḥ tatra pravṛttiḥ tat na śuktikā śakalaḥ eva pravṛtteḥ tatra eva tu pravṛttiḥ tad saṃnidhi nibandhanā rajata mātra pratīteḥ smṛti viveka śūnya tvāt ca pravṛttiḥ anyatra api syāt asaṃnidhāna agrahaṇasya tatra api aviśeṣāt 
[138,i^1]	atha matam anya deśeṣu vastuṣu sa viśeṣa pratyakṣa avagateṣu rajatāt viveka grahaṇāt apravṛttiḥ śuktikā śakale tu rajata sādhāraṇa śukla bhāsvara rūpa mātra pratīteḥ viśeṣāt pratyayāt ca smṛti viparivartinaḥ rajatāt viveka grahaṇāt pravṛttiḥ evam api adṛṣṭeṣu loka ādiṣu tatas anya tā anavadhāraṇāt pravṛttiḥ syāt atha na teṣu rajata avagamaḥ itaratra api na bhāve vā viparītā khyātiḥ abhyupagatā syāt atha adṛṣṭa tvāt eva adṛṣṭeṣu na pravartate śuktau api na pravarteta nanu yat tu tathā rajata rūpam na tena avagamaḥ sa yathā cakṣuṣā saṃprayuktasya na asti tathā saṃprayuktāyāḥ api śukteḥ
