[138,i^2]	yadi manyeta dṛśyamāna smaryamāṇa yoga vivekāt cakṣuḥ saṃprayuktaḥ eva pravartate na itarasmin tatra api idam vicāryam viveka grahaṇasya viveka kṛtaḥ abhāvāt saṃnidhi pratīteḥ abheda bodhaḥ tatas vā pravṛttiḥ bheda avabodha abhāva mātrāt vā pūrvasmin viparyayaḥ uttarasmin dṛśyamānādṛśyamānayoḥ saṃprayuktā saṃprayuktayoḥ vā na viśeṣaḥ bheda agrahaṇasya tulya tvāt na hi indriya saṃyogasya darśanasya vā kaścid agrahaḥ upayogaḥ abhūta samārope tu asti na kathañcid agṛhīte asaṃprayukte vā aindriyakaḥ samāropaḥ upapadyate 
[138,ii^1]	smṛtam pratyakṣatas bhinnam sva jñānāt eva ced kutas avivekaḥ anyathā tu syāt sadā sāmānya darśane viparyayaḥ anyam smarataḥ na ca saṃśaya darśanāt smṛta dvaya aviveka uttham saṃśayam yadi manyate tat na ubhayoḥ api yatas smṛtau dṛṣṭaḥ viparyayaḥ viśeṣa jñānataḥ adhyakṣe smṛtam yadi vivicyate na sva jñānāt asati asmin dvi smṛtau katham eka dhīḥ eka tvam eva smarataḥ prāgrūpam śaśini sphuṭam timira ādi pradoṣeṇa katham te dvi tva vibhramaḥ pipāsataḥ ca salilam śuktikā hita cetasaḥ viparyayaḥ na hi bhavet bhavan vā salile bhavet api ca idam tatra bhavān vyācaṣṭām smaryamāṇam dṛśyamānāt sva jñānāt eva vivicyate na vā smṛti jñānasya svarūpam eva tādṛśam yat pramātavyāt bhedena avabhāsayati sva rūpa mātra niṣṭham vā tatra pūrvasmin smaraṇa gocarayoḥ avivekaḥ kutas sva jñānāt eva vivikta tvāt 
[138,ii^2]	itarasmin api sadā smṛtau viparyayaḥ syāt sāmānya darśane ca anya smṛtau avivekāt na ca tat tathā saṃśayasya api darśanāt atha matam eka smṛtau viparyayaḥ tatas avivekāt aneka smṛtau tu saṃśayaḥ na ekasmāt avivekāt tat asat aneka smaraṇe api hi dṛśyate viparyayaḥ yadi ca pratyakṣe arthe viśeṣa jñānāt smaryamāṇam vivicyate na sva jñānāt asati tatra viśeṣa jñāne ca dvayoḥ smṛtau saṃśayaḥ eva syāt na eka avabhāsaḥ viparyayaḥ atha tu sva jñānāt smṛtam vivicyate smṛti viparyaya bhedaḥ ca abhyupagamyate tadā aneka smaraṇe api indriya doṣa viśeṣāt i uktaḥ viparyayaḥ darśitam ca idam sāmānya darśane api kadācid ekām koṭim smarataḥ na saṃśayaḥ na viparyayaḥ doṣāṇām apuṣṭeḥ atas sva jñānāt eva tadā smṛtam vivicyate na dṛśya viśeṣa paricchedāt evam ced kutas dṛśyamāna smaryamāṇauvivekaḥ 
[140,i_140,ii]	api ca anyat eva smarataḥ pūrvarūpam eka tvam śaśini dvi tva vibhramaḥ na smaryamāṇā viveka jaḥ na ca jñāna indriya vṛtti bheda avivekāt tayoḥ apratyakṣa tvāt smaryamāṇa tvāt ca śuktikā hita cetasaḥ ca salilam pipāsataḥ na syāt viparyayaḥ salila ābhāsaḥ vā smaryamāṇasya sva jñāna vivekāt na ca sarvā niyogena bhrāntiḥ sādṛśya bandhanā śvete pīta bhramaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ madhure tikta vibhramaḥ kiñcid sādṛśyataḥ hi syāt na kaścid tatra na bhramaḥ tasmāt indriya doṣāṇām sāmarthyasya vibhāgataḥ bhrameṣu niyamaḥ doṣāt agrahe na bhrame yamaḥ yadi ca sadṛśa darśanāt sadṛśa smṛteḥ bhramaḥ katham śvete pīta bhramaḥ madhure vā tikta bhrāntiḥ āntara pitta saṃvedane avyāpārayataḥ api bahis indriyam syāt añjana vat ca akṣi gatasya tad gata kṛṣṇim ādi vat ca adṛśya tvāt kiñcid sādṛśye sarva prakāra bhrama prasaṃgaḥ tasmāt indriya doṣa sāmarthya bhedāt niyatā viparyaya utpattiḥ agraha mātre tu doṣa vyāpāre kāmila ādi doṣāt bhrānti niyamaḥ na syāt na hi sādṛśya nimittaḥ asadṛśe api bhrānti darśanāt 
[140,iii]	viśeṣa smaraṇāt na api smṛtau api tad agrahaḥ deśa kāla viśeṣāt ca na smṛtam pravivicyate aneka deśa adhigatam viviktam na punar tatas smṛtiḥ iti api vijñānam smṛteḥ anyat udāhṛtam na ca māna phalāt bhinnāt tat siddhi ati phalāt ṛte sati smṛti viveke ca pratyabhijñāna vibhramaḥ atha ana saṃnihitaḥ vyarthaḥ vedyaḥ saṃnidhimat tayā avivikta smṛteḥ evam viparīta artha tā bhavet manasaḥ anupaghātāt ca na asaṃnidhya parigrahaḥ doṣaḥ hi agrahaṇe hetuḥ indriyāṇām udāhṛtaḥ pravṛtti niyamaḥ na syāt iti ca atra niveditam sarva jñānāni mithyā ca prasajyante atra kalpane sarva ātmanā arthaḥ jñānena kenacid na hi gṛhyate tathā ajñāta vivekasya dvi candra ādi viparyayāt anuvṛttimataḥ paśyan kasya sva ātma apanihnute 
[141,i^1]	atha matam sva jñānāt eva smṛtam vivicyate kadācid tu tatra pratyakṣaḥ iva viśeṣa āgrahaḥ tataḥ avivekaḥ sataḥ tu viśeṣa grahaṇaḥ indriya saṃyukte sāmānya darśane api na āvivekaḥ tatas ubhaya koṭi smaraṇe na saṃśayaḥ ekasmṛtau na saṃśayaḥ na viparyayaḥ evam api dvayoḥ smaraṇe na viparyayaḥ syāt na ca smṛtau viśeṣa grahaṇam viśeṣa smaraṇāt atha deśa kāla viśeṣāt smaryamāṇam vivicyate tatra deśa kāla bheda āgrahaḥ iti tat na ananta deśa kāla bheda avagatam tad deśa avagatam ca dṛśyāt smaryamāṇam viviktam gamyate na ca deśa kāla bheda grahaṇāt ananta smaraṇa anupapatteḥ tad deśa avagate ca deśa bheda abhāvāt atha smaryamāṇa tayā agrahaṇāt avivekaḥ smaryamāṇa tā jñānāt ca vivekaḥ tasmāt smarāmi iti jñāna śūnyāni rajata ādi jñānāni bhrānti hetavaḥ paripūrṇā eva tarhi smṛtiḥ na tayā sva viṣayasya kiñcid na gṛhītam svayam eva sā sva viṣayam dṛśyāt vivinakti iti na asti dṛśyamāna smaryamāṇayoḥ avivekaḥ yatas smarāmi iti jñānam anyat eva darśana smaraṇa viveka kāri smṛteḥ tatra idam vicāryam smṛtiḥ sva viṣayam vivinakti vā na vā 
[141,i^2]	yadi vivinakti tadā viparyaya abhāvaḥ atha na smṛtiḥ sva viṣayam vivinakti tadā sāmānya darśane ca anya smṛtau viparyayaḥ syāt iti uktam na smarāmi iti vivekāt ced saḥ eva smṛteḥ svayam avivecaka tvena syāt kārya gamyasya hi jñānasya bhedaḥ kārya viśeṣa unneyaḥ na ced smṛteḥ pramāṇa kāryāt kāryam viviktam syāt kena sā viviktā gamyeta sati api smṛti viveke dṛṣṭaḥ pratyabhijñā bhramaḥ saḥ eva iti na ca pratyakṣasya āvivekaḥ eka vivekena ubhayoḥ vikārāt smṛtāt avivekāt ca smṛti vibhramaḥ syāt na pratyakṣa bhramaḥ 
[141,i^3]	tasmāt na smarāmi iti pramoṣāt avivekaḥ atha asaṃnihitasya saṃnihita ātmanā pratītiḥ avivekaḥ smṛteḥ viparīta artha tva prasaṃgaḥ atha asaṃnidhya grahaṇāt bhavatu sa svapna jñāne natu indriya jāyām bhrāntau manasaḥ anupaghātāt upaghāta hetu tvāt ca agrahaṇasya na ca ittham pravṛtti niyamaḥ syāt iti uktam sati ca vastu grahe kasyacid aṃśasya agrahāt bhrāntau sarva jñāna bhrama tvam na hi kasyacid jñānasya sarva ātmanā vastu viṣayaḥ iti sati api ca viveka jñāne pramāṇa antarāt dvi candra diś moha ādi anugatiḥ dṛṣṭā iti na agrahaṇa mātram viparyayaḥ 
[142,i^1]	prasakta pratiṣedha ātmā khyātiḥ prāptau prakalpate na agrahaḥ prāpakaḥ abhāvaḥ prāpikāḥ viparīta dhīḥ ye ca khyātī tu rajataḥ cakṣuḥ saṃyukta vastunoḥ na ayam tad upanīta artha pratiṣedhaḥ avagamyate na ca agrahaṇam eva eṣā pratītiḥ apabādhate sarvā hi agraha bādhena janma na syāt tathā īdṛśī viveka vijñānam idam na prasakta niṣedha dhīḥ iti bruvāṇaḥ vaiyātyāt svām pratītim apahnute na krame yaugapadye vā viveka matiḥ īdṛśī prāpte syāt aikya saṃvittau na bhedasya anirūpaṇe rajatasya smaran cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya ca vastunaḥ sāmānya dṛṣṭyā rajatāt abuddhvā ca viviktatām paścāt viviñcan pratyeti na evam sāmānya darśane koṭi dvaya smṛti abhāve saṃśayaḥ na niyogataḥ viveka grahaṇa abhāvāt kāla saṃnidhi saṃvidaḥ tadvat ābhāsanāt prāpta āviṣṭaḥ syāt anyathā grahaḥ 
[142,i^2]	tatra agrahaḥ nimittam syāt athavā saṃnidhi grahaḥ bheda graha apavādena rahitaḥ bhāva rūpataḥ viparyaya anabhyupāye bhramaḥ agraha nibandhanaḥ śabda eka gamyaḥ uktaḥ syāt agrahaḥ agraha bandhanaḥ na idam rajatam iti prasakta pratiṣedha rūpā pratītiḥ na agrahaṇe avakalpate prasaṅga abhāvāt na khalva grahaṇam kasyacid prasañjakam abhāvaḥ hi saḥ viparītā tu khyātiḥ saṃnihitasya rajata tām abhūtām rajatasya vā saṃnihita tām ādarśayantī prasañjayati nanu ca rajata nayana ghaṭita vastunoḥ khyātī staḥ te eva prasañjike satyam na tu tad upanītayoḥ iyam niṣedha avagatiḥ na hi na idam rajatam iti rajata mātram cakṣuḥ saṃyukta vastu mātram vā nirasyamānam avasyāmaḥ kim tu cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya tu rajata tām rajatasya vā cakṣu saṃyuktām na ca etayoḥ agrahaṇam prāpakam agrahaṇa tvāt eva tasmāt avaśyam pratiṣedhya prāptaye viparīta khyātiḥ upāsanīyā 
[142,i^3]	na ca na idam iti agrahaṇam eva vāryate sarva jñāneṣu tādrūpya prasaṃgāt sarva jñānānām agraha bādhena utpattau ca viveka jñāna mātram idam na prasakta pratiṣedha rūpam iti prati iti anusāriṇaḥ anurūpam na hi rajata śukti kāśa kalayoḥ yugapad viviktayoḥ grahaṇe īdṛśī pratītiḥ na krameṇa aviviktayoḥ grahaṇaḥ īdṛśī syāt iti ced yuktā viviktayoḥ grahaṇe aviveka pratiṣedha rūpa tvāt viviktayoḥ grahaṇe prāpti abhāva yuktā api ca bhavati kadācid yaḥ smarati ca rajatasya cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya vastunaḥ sāmānya mātra darśī na rajatāt vivekam gṛhṇāti punar cakṣuḥ prasādāt pratyeti na ca tadā tathā pratītiḥ aviveka grahaṇa abhāvāt nanu sāmānya darśane na ced viparyayaḥ saṃśayaḥ syāt tat apanodi ca nirṇaya jñānam īdṛśam eva na etat sāram na hi asati koṭi dvaya smaraṇe sāmānya darśane api saṃśayaḥ na ca viparyayaḥ bhavati hi puras avasthite bhāsvara rūpa mātra pratītiḥ rajate ca smṛtiḥ 
[142,i^4_144,i]	na ca tayoḥ anya tvam pratipadyate na ekatvam ca tatra na viveka jñānam evaṃrūpam ekatva apratipatteḥ atha matam viveka agrahaṇāt kāla saṃnidhi pratīteḥ ca rajatam vā cakṣuḥ saṃprayukta vat avabhāsate cakṣuḥ saṃyuktam vā rajata vat atas prāptiḥ iti pratiṣedha upapattiḥ abhyupetā tarhi viparīta khyātiḥ na hi anyā sā atada ātmanaḥ tathā avabhāsanāt kāmam tattva ajñāna nimittā syāt na hi sā tattva jñāne sati udeti virodhāt iti tatra api saṃnidhi khyātiḥ eva nibandhanam tasyāḥ tu viveka grahaḥ apavādaḥ agrahaṇe nirapavādā sā eva kāraṇam na abhāvaḥ viparīta khyāti anabhyugame ca agrahaṇa nibandhanaḥ bhramaḥ iti agrahaṇam agrahaṇa nibandhanam iti su vyāhṛtam svapne ca dvitīya abhāvāt kutas avivekaḥ smṛta tvena aviviktasya tathā viveke dharmiṇi pratipanne dharma antara pratipanne dharma antara pratipatteḥ bādhaka tvam pūrvasyāḥ ca bhrānti tvam syātām iti yaḥ pratīti virodhaḥ tu sa sva doṣaḥ udāhṛtaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyena bodhāt rūpyam idam mitam idam śuklam rajatam iti sāmānādhikaraṇyena pratīteḥ ātmā upālambhaḥ parasmin āsajyate pratīti virodhaḥ jñāna bheda kalpanāyāḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt 
[144,ii^1]	anāśvāsaḥ jñāyamāne jñānena eva apabādhyate vyabhicārāt asāmarthyam na tad kāryasya lābhataḥ vyabhicārāt prameya tve kāryam eva na labhyate yaḥ hi jñāyamāne arthe anyathā api syāt iti anāśvāsaḥ tasya tena eva jñānena tathā tva paricchedinā utpattiḥ nirudhyate tathā hi anāśvāsa nivṛttaye tadvidham jñānam eva apekṣyate tat ca asti eva na ca vyabhicāra doṣāt asamartha pramāṇam jñānam iti yujyate pramāṇa kāryasya paricchedasya jñāna rūpāt eva siddha tvāt paricchedataḥ hi prāmāṇyam atantra tā tu vyabhicāra avi abhicārayoḥ asati tasmin dhūma ādeḥ avyabhicārasya api apramāṇa tvāt vyabhicāravataḥ api ca sita asita ādiṣu cakṣuṣaḥ sati tasmin prāmāṇyāt na ca vyabhicāraḥ bādha hetuḥ doṣa vat prāmāṇya upaghātī kvacid dṛṣṭaḥ cakṣuḥ ādau vyabhicāravati pramāṇa tvāt nanu dṛṣṭaḥ vyabhicāraḥ prāmāṇya upaghātī prameya tva ūrdhva tva ādau na etat sāram na tatra vyabhicārāt aprāmāṇyam api tu pariccheda kārya abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ ca hetu abhāvāt 
[144,ii^2]	avyabhicārāt hi liṅgāt liṅgi paricchedaḥ yatra tu avyabhicāraḥ na kāraṇam tatra vyabhicāre api sati paricchede prāmāṇyam avivādam akṣeṣu tadvat eva ca jñānam pariccheda nimittam na liṅga vat na ca saṃśaya utpattyā vyabhicāraḥ prāmāṇyam upahanti samyak paricchinne dvaividhi asya asaṃśaya hetutvāt na niścite sthāṇau ūrdhva tvena saṃśerate utpattyā eva jñānam artham avadhārayati anavadhārakam tu na eva iha adhikṛtam evam ca avadhāraṇā deva anavadhāraṇam iti vipratiṣiddham yaḥ eva tu avyabhicāram arthayate jñānasya āśvāsa artham tasya eva anāśvāsaḥ avyabhicāra jñāne api anāśvāsāt na hi tat asiddha vyabhicāram ātmani jñāna antareṣu ca āśvāsa kāraṇam jñāna antarāt siddhau anavasthā api ca jñāna rūpāt ced na artha āśvāsaḥ tasya asiddhau kena saha avyabhicāraḥ jñānasya gṛhyeta kim ca jñāna rūpāt eva avyabhicāraḥ api kathyate viparīta khyātau tad virodhāt tathā sati tat eva viṣayasya sādhakam vyarthaḥ avyabhicāraḥ na ca vyabhicāraḥ prāmāṇyam upahanti iti uktam 
[145,i]	api ca agrahaṇe abhīṣṭam yat viveka nibandhanam na parāṇudyate daṇḍaiḥ tad viparyaya darśane na udreka hetavaḥ doṣāḥ kārya sāmarthya ghātinaḥ graha āgraha vibhāgaḥ syāt atas tad sadasattvataḥ viparyaye hi nitarām upaghātaḥ prakalpate iṣṭa kārya uparodhena viparīta udayena ca tasmāt tad sat asat tvābhyām vivekaḥ atra api kalpate doṣe asati a graha āśaṅkā katham ca vinivartate na hi kāraṇa sadbhāve kārya sattā niyogataḥ pratyakṣam kāryam evam ca hetunā anumitam bhavet viparyaye phala abhāvaḥ hetu abhāvāt tu yujyate viveka upāyaḥ ca doṣa abhāva bhāvau grahaṇa agrahaṇayoḥ na daṇḍa vāritau viparyaye viparyaya hetavaḥ abhyupaghātakāḥ sutarām iṣṭa kārya uparodhāt viparīta udayāt ca na ca aduṣṭeṣu api indriya ādiṣu agraha āśaṅkā nivṛttiḥ yatas hetu bhāve api na niyogataḥ kāryam viparyayaḥ ca syāt pratyakṣā saṃvittiḥ hetunā anumīyeta phalāt tu hetoḥ hetu bhāva anumānam doṣa abhāvāt tu viparyaya kārya asattvam yukta anumānam hetu abhāve kārya anutpādāt 
[146,i]	anālamba natā pattiḥ yathā ākāra antara arpaṇam svarūpa anarpaṇāt evam bhavet agrahaṇe api te kasyacid tu arpaṇam tulyam atha tatra na tat tathā parasya api hi tatra evam atha tatra tathā sthiteḥ sarvatra syāt tathā bhāvaḥ syāt evam grahaṇe api te yathā tatra animitta tvāt samya jñāne animitta tā śaṅkyate grahaṇe api evam agrahe sā nirūpitā jñānāt eva nimitta tvam anyeṣām na viśiṣyate ālambana tvahānam ca yathā ākāra antara avabhāse cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya tathāgrahaṇe api sva rūpa ānarpaṇasya tulya tvāt atha kasyacid sāmānya rūpasya su ākāra tvāt atha kānicid cakṣuḥ saṃyuktāni vastūni svena rūpeṇa gṛhyante iti kasyacid agrahaṇe api nānā ālambana tvam tulyam ākāra antara avabhāse api keṣāñcid sva ākārāṇām avabhāsanāt atha agrahaṇe na eva cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya ālambana tvam iṣyate paraḥ api na eva viparyayaḥ icchati evam hi uktam tasmāt yat anyathā santam anyathā pratipadyate tad nirālambanam jñānam abhāva ālambanam ca tat 
[147,i]	atha viparyaye cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya ālambana tvāt anyatra api anālambana tā śaṅkā agrahaṇe api tulyā yathā khalu viparyaya jñāne cakṣuḥ saṃprayukta vastu svabhāva nirapekṣa tā dṛṣṭā samyak jñāne api śaṅkyate jñāna tva sāmānyāt tathā cakṣuḥ saṃprayuktam api vastu na avikala rūpam gṛhyate tena anālambanam bhavati sadṛśa smṛti hetu tām ca pratipadyate iti agrahaṇe dṛṣṭa anālambana tā grahaṇeṣu api kasmāt na śaṅkyate doṣa abhāvāt iti ced viparyaye api tulyam na ca anyathā ālambane nirālambana tvam cakṣuḥ tu anyathā api na ālambyate ālambana arthaḥ ca rajata vyavahāra yogya tā śukteḥ tathā hi rajata arthī tām ādatte ghaṭasya api hi na eva anyat sva jñāna ālambana tvam anyatra vyavahāra yogya tāyāḥ yatas na viṣaya ākāram jñānam tatra śuktiḥ sva rūpeṇa na ālambitāḥ rajata jñānena tad nibandhana vyavahāra bhāvāt rajata rūpeṇa tu tad nibandhanasya upādāna vyavahārasya tatra bhāvāt iti 
[147,ii^1]	kriyā niṣṭhe api vidhau vastu svarūpa siddhaye kaścid āha avaghāta prokṣaṇa ādeḥ yathā dravya artha tā sthitā jñānam svabhāvāt dravya artham karma tvāt ca ātmanaḥ tathā bhavatu evam tathā api iṣṭa rūpa siddhiḥ kutas matā śabdaḥ tad artha kārya tve tau ajñānasya niṣṭhitaḥ jñānāt jñeyasya kaḥ anyaḥ arthaḥ sva rūpa pratibhāsanāt adṛṣṭa kalpanā yuktāḥ na ca dṛṣṭasya saṃbhave tasmāt yathā prokṣaṇa ādi vidheḥ vrīhiṣu gamyate adṛṣṭā saṃskṛtiḥ jñānavidhe rūpam tathā ātmanaḥ yathā avaghāta prokṣaṇa ādayaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva dravya arthāḥ dvitīyayā ca dravyasya karma tvena nirdeśāt tathā jñānam api svarūpeṇa para artham karma tvena ca ātmanaḥ nirdeśāt tad artham atas jñāna viṣayaḥ api vidhiḥ ātma rūpam saṃspṛśati na jñāna mātre paryavasyati jñānasya ātma rūpa artha tvena kartavyatā avagamāt jñāna niyogena eva ātma rūpasya ākṣepāt syāt etat bhavatu jñānasya ātma arthatā abhipretā apahata pāpma ādi rūpa ātma pratītau tu pramāṇam vācyam 
[147,ii^2]	śabdaḥ tāvat evaṃvidha ātma jñāna kartavyatāyām paryavasitaḥ evaṃvidha ātma uddeśena jñānam kuryāt na tu evaṃvidhaḥ ātmā iti tatra ucyate na hi tatra akiñcitkarasya tādarthyena kartavyatā yujyate jñānasya ca karmaṇi na anyat phalam tad rūpa saṃvitteḥ na hi tasyām dṛṣṭāyām anyasya adṛṣṭasya kalpanā tatra yathā vrīhīn prokṣati iti prokṣaṇa vidheḥ eva vrīhiṣu adṛṣṭa saṃskāra avagamaḥ prokṣaṇa viṣayāt api na anyathā vrīhi arthe prokṣaṇe kartavyatā yujyate na hi tatra kiñcid akurvat prokṣaṇam tad artham kṛtam syāt iti evam vidheḥ eva adṛṣṭa saṃskāra sadbhāva siddhiḥ yathā svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti na anyathā svarga kāmasya yāga kartavya tā pratītiḥ yujyate yadi na svarga upāyaḥ yāgaḥ anupāye ced niyujyate na svarga kāmaḥ niyuktaḥ bhavati anuṣṭhitaḥ api na svarga kāmena anuṣṭhitaḥ bhavati iti kriyā viṣayāt api vidheḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva avagamaḥ śābdaḥ tathā jñāna viṣayāt api vidheḥ ātma rūpa bodhaḥ na hi tadvidham ātmānam uddiśya jñāna niyogaḥ yujyate atadvidhaḥ ced ātmā tena jñānena pratīyate iti 
[148,i^1]	ukta uttaram idam yasmāt arūpeṇa api bhāsakam jñānam pradarśitam na syāt anyathā tad vidheḥ phalam layaḥ nivartyaḥ na tathā vikṣepaḥ hi yathāsukhaḥ laya vikṣepa bhedaḥ ca na syāt agraha mātrake nanu arūpa avabhāse syāt adṛṣṭa phala kalpanā rūpa avabhāse dṛṣṭam tu phalam tat siddhi lakṣaṇam na dṛṣṭa mātrāt dṛṣṭa artham puruṣa artha anugam tu tat na bhidyate ca tad bhāvaḥ rūpā rūpa avabhāsayoḥ yathā prapañca śūnya tve tattve jñāna avabhāsite duḥkha karma kleśa hānam atattve api tathā bhavet etat ca atra bhavet yuktam pratyakṣa ādi avirodhataḥ anaupacārikā arthāḥ ca syuḥ karma viṣayaḥ yatas ātma artha jñāna vidheḥ etāvat gamyate jñānena saḥ avabhāsyate ālambyate vyavahāra yogya tām āpadyate tat ca avabhāsanam sva rūpeṇa ca dṛṣṭam para rūpeṇa ca rajata ātmanā śuktikāyāḥ pratipāditam etat na agraha mātram etat anyathā ākhyātiḥ tu 
[148,i^2]	tatra ubhayathā saṃbhave kutas etat tattva pratipattiḥ avaśya abhyupeyā na atasmin tad khyātiḥ anyathā na ātma jñāna vidhiḥ phalavān syāt sa khalu ana ātma rūpa pravilaya arthaḥ anātma rūpa vilayena hi vastunaḥ avagatiḥ dṛṣṭā iti yadi ca na ātmanaḥ nāma rūpa prapañca rūpeṇa prakāśanam kim pravilāpyeta atha matam dvi prakārā iyam avidyā prakāśasya acchādikā vikṣepikā ca svapna jāgaritayoḥ vikṣepikā suṣuptaḥ ācchādikā laya lakṣaṇā tatra ācchādaka avidyā nivṛttiḥ jñāna vidheḥ phalam tat ca asat yatas na ācchādikāyāḥ avidyāyāḥ nivṛttiḥ puruṣeṇa arthyate tathā yathā vikṣepasya sa hi vividha duḥkha ātmakaḥ layaḥ tu vividha duḥkha nivṛtteḥ asakṛt ānanda tvena śrutau gītaḥ pratyuta arthanīyaḥ syāt api ca viparyāsam anicchataḥ avidyā bhedaḥ eva na syāt avasthā traye api agrahaṇa mātra tvāt tasmāt agrahaṇa viparyaya grahaṇe dve avidye kārya kāraṇa bhāvena avasthite svapna jāgaritayoḥ ubhe kāraṇa bhūta agrahaṇa lakṣaṇā suṣuptaḥ iti avidyā pravibhāgaḥ upapadyate 
[148,i^3]	tat uktam kārya kāraṇa baddhau tāviṣyete viśva taijasau prājñaḥ kāraṇa baddhaḥ tu dvau tu turye na sidhyataḥ nanu anyathā ayam bhedaḥ agrahaṇa samyak grahaṇābhyām agrahaṇa lakṣaṇa ācchādikā suṣupte asamyak grahaṇam itarayoḥ tathā hi abhinnasya vastunaḥ apradeśasya grahaṇe tathā abhāvasya ca agrahaṇāt pṛthaktvena pratyavabhāsaḥ na etat sāram yadi tāvat asamyak grahaṇa mātram tat apaṭu tvam vā jñānasya kenacid drūpeṇa vā grahaṇam na sarva ātmanā tatra dūra sthe sūkṣme ca bhavati apaṭu jñānam sāmānya jñānam na ca tat avidyā na ca kiñcid jñānam sarva ātmanā arthasya grāhakam iti sarva jñāna mithyātva apātaḥ abhedasya agrahaṇe api bhedasya āvartane api bhedasya asaṃvitteḥ na nivartanīyam asti vidyayā na khalva bheda agrahaṇam nivartanīyam na hi tat kiñcid aparādhyati bhedaḥ tu vividha duḥkha āyatanam 
[148,i^4]	atha asamyak grahaṇam pṛthak pratyavabhāsaḥ apṛthak ātmanaḥ abhyupetā tarhi viparyaya khyātiḥ apṛthak pṛthak prakāśate iti atha ucyeta na brūmaḥ pṛthak prakāśate kim tu pṛthak iva prakāśate iti kaḥ iva arthaḥ yadi yathā pṛthak bhūtam aprakāśamāna ekatvam prakāśate tathā ekam api ātma tattvam agṛhyamāṇā eka tvam prakāśate iti kenacid aṃśena grahaṇam sarva ātmanā ca agrahaṇam uktam bhavati tatra ca uktam atha prakāśataḥ iva na tu prakāśate prakāśane kaḥ upamā arthaḥ tad nibandhana vyavahāra pravṛttiḥ tad nibandhanaḥ ced vyavahāraḥ prāptam prakāśanam na asati kāraṇe kāryam bhavati iti atha abheda āgrahaḥ eva pṛthaktva c raha abhimānaḥ tat asat agrahaṇasya abhāvasya sva rūpeṇa para rūpeṇa vā grahaṇa anabhyupagamāt aprakāśamāne ca pṛthaktve kutas tad avagrahaḥ abhinne ca bheda abhimānam parityajya abheda agrahaṇe bheda graha abhimānam ūrīkurvatā kim parihṛtam syāt tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate laya vikṣepa bhedaḥ ca na syāt agraha mātrake iti 
[151,i]	nanu anātma rūpeṇa pratipatteḥ na dṛśyate kiñcitphalam tatra adṛṣṭa kalpanā syāt ātma rūpa pratipatteḥ tu dṛṣṭam phalam tad svarūpa siddhiḥ ucyate na yasya kasyacid darśanāt dṛṣṭa artha tā kim tu puruṣa artha saṃsparśinaḥ tena hi tad vidhiḥ nirākāṅkṣā bhavati na ca puruṣa arha bhedaḥ tattva atattva pratipattyoḥ yathā hi viśuddham advaitam ātmānam pratipadyamānaḥ tathābhūtaḥ na śokena saṃspṛśyate śocanīya abhāvāt na karma āśayam upacinoti kartavya abhāvāt na kvacid drajyati kiñcid dveṣṭi vā viṣaya abhāvāt evam jīvan eva vidvān vimuktaḥ bhavati tathā atathābhūtam api tathā bhāvanā puraḥsaram sākṣāt iva pratipadyamānaḥ abhūtaḥ api arthaḥ paribhāvanā atiśayāt bhūta vyavahāra hetuḥ bhavati idam eva ca atra yujyate pratyakṣa ādīnām avirodhāt karma vidhīnām ca bhūta artha tvāt parama arthe hi prapañca śūnya tve pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni bādhyeran karma vidhayaḥ ca ābhūta kalpanā upādāna vyavahāra siddhārtha gocarāḥ syuḥ tasmāt aparama arthena eva advaita ātma jñāna vidhiḥ yujyate 
[151,ii^1]	jānātiḥ tattva bodhe ced na mithyā ādi viśeṣaṇāt na ātmā jñātaḥ tathā syāt ced na tad rūpā vidhānataḥ pramāṇa antara siddha tve natarām anyathā yadi śabda arpitena rūpeṇa tasya jñānam vidhīyate atattvena api tena asya vijñānam avakalpate yadi matam sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ iti jānātiḥ tattva paricchedaḥ eva vartate tena na abhūta samāropeṇa jñāna vidhiḥ syāt iti tat na mithyātva ādibhiḥ jñānam viśeṣyate mithyājñānam samyak jñānam saṃśaya jñānam iti tad eka niyame na upapadyeta paunaruktyāt virodhāt ca 
[151,ii^2]	syāt etat asvarūpeṇa pratipattau na tad ātma jñānam anya jñānam eva bhavati tattva jñānam ca vidhīyate tasmāt tattva siddhiḥ iti tat ca na na khalu etāvat eva tat ātmā jñātavyaḥ iti yadi syāt tad rūpa jñāna vidhiḥ tat ca na ubhayathā anupapatteḥ pramāṇa antara siddham ced ātma rūpam na tat jñānam vidheyam atha asiddham aśakyam eva tat syāt etat apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā iti śabda samarpita rūpasya tasya jñānam vidhīyate tena ca tattvena api tad saṃbhavati samāropitena api tena na niyogataḥ tathābhūta jñāna vidheḥ tathā abhāvaḥ asya pratīyate 
[152,i]	jñānam yadi ca dṛṣṭa artham prāptam dṛṣṭatas eva tat ātma rūpa vijijñāsaḥ rajijñāsoḥ vṛthā eva tat tad upāyaḥ na ced jñātaḥ tasya eva astu vidhiḥ tatas avaghāta ādi vidhayaḥ na adṛṣṭa sparśa varjitāḥ alaukikam idam jñānam atas yadi vidhīyate na rūpa siddhaye tāvat yatas kartavyatā vidheḥ kartavyatā ca dṛṣṭa arthe dṛṣṭāt eva prasiddhyati alaukike artha rūpe atas śabdena pratipādite jñāne jñeya abhyupāya tvāt svayam eva unmukhaḥ pumān tad upāye tu avijñāte vidhinā sa pravartyatām niyoga anupraveśaḥ atas vihanti eva pramāṇa tām bhūtarthaḥ iti na upāsyaḥ bhūta artha gatim icchatā 
[152,ii^1]	yadi ca jñānasya dṛṣṭam phalam tatas eva pravṛtti siddhe vyarthaḥ vidhiḥ yaḥ hi ātma rūpam anubhavitu kāmaḥ sa tasya jñāne svayam eva yatate yaḥ tu na tathā tasya tat vyartham iti vidhi śatena api sa na pravartyate atha upāya ajñānāt dṛṣṭa phale api na pravartate svayam atas vidhīyate iti tat ca vārtam yatas saḥ eva upāyaḥ vidhīyatām yatra ayam ajñānāt na pravṛttaḥ jñāne tu dṛṣṭa phala tvāt pravartate eva syāt etat avaghāta ādiṣu dṛṣṭa phaleṣu api dṛṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ satyam na tu adṛṣṭa saṃsparśa rahitaḥ tatra api hi niyama adṛṣṭam phalam taṇḍuleṣu tad praṇāḍyā vā pradhāna pūrva siddhiḥ adṛṣṭā eva atha matam advaita ātma jñānam adṛṣṭa pūrvam alaukikam atas anantara phalam api vidhīyate iti 
[152,ii^2]	tatra ucyate kimartham vidhīyate pramāṇa antara agocarasya svarūpa pratipatti artham āhosvit anuṣṭhāna artham tatra na svarūpa siddhi artham anuṣṭhāna phalaḥ hi vidhiḥ na anuṣṭhānāya dṛṣṭa artha tvāt eva tad siddheḥ tasmāt alaukike apahata pāpma ādi rūpaḥ ātma tattve śabdāt pratipanne tasya sākṣāt jñānam prati tad anubhava upāya tvāt svayam eva puruṣasya abhimukhyam bhavati iti vyartham tad vidhānam yathā āścarya bhūte kasmiṃścid arthe āgamāt pratipanne tasya sākṣātkaraṇe svayam eva unmukha tvam bhavati tad upāyeṣu tu ajñāteṣu upāya tva jñāpanāya vidhānam yujyate tat evam jñāne niyoga anupapatteḥ niyoge ca vastu rūpa avagame prāmāṇya ayogāt vyavasthita ātma tattva pratipattim icchatā śabdāt na tasya niyoga anupraveśaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ iti 
[153,i]	idānīm dvitīya pratipatti vidhi nirāsāya āha atas eva na vijñāna saṃtāna vidhi niṣṭhatā tatra api pūrvavat na syāt svarūpa avagati pramā svarūpa niṣṭhāt śabdāt tu pramitasya vacaḥ antarāt upāsana vidhānam syāt prāpteḥ tat api vā vṛthā abhyāsena pratyayasya prakarṣasya abhivīkṣaṇāt tasmāt bhavati akārye arthe vedāntānām pramāṇa tā 
[153,ii^1]	yat api matam sa kratum kurvīta prajñām kurvīta nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti yatra api svarūpa niṣṭhatā eva lakṣyate tat tvam asi iti tatra api sat asmi iti cetaḥ dhārayet iti vivakṣita tvāt śravaṇāt anyat anucintanam dhyānam pratyaya pravāhaḥ vidhīyate karma vat eva amṛta tva phalam tat api atas eva na yujyate pūrva uktāt tattva avagati pramāṇa abhāva prasaṅgāt anya niṣṭha tvāt vākyasya atha tu vākya antarāt tattva niṣṭhāt adhigate tad viṣaya pratyaya pravāha vidhānam iṣyate bhavatu na kaścid doṣaḥ tathā ca vijñāya prajñām kurvīta iti ātma tattva vijñānasya siddha tām darśayati tat api vā vyartham eva prāpta artha tvāt sākṣātkaraṇa phalam hi tad tad anucintanam dṛṣṭa artham na tatas anyat phalam ākāṅkṣyate 
[153,ii^2]	amṛta tvam hi na svarūpa āvirbhāvāt anyat iti prāk varṇitam dṛṣṭā ca jñāna abhyāsasya samyak jñāna prasāda hetu tāḥ loke bhāvanā viśeṣāt hi abhūtam api anubhavam āpadyate kim punar bhūtam sa kratum kurvīta iti tu na sakala viśeṣa atigātma tattva anucintanam vidhīyate tad bhāva phalam api tu nāma rūpa upādhi manaḥ maya prāṇa śarīra ādi rūpa anudhyānam aiśvarya phalam krameṇa vā sākṣātkaraṇa phalam tam eva dhīraḥ vijñāya iti na prajñā karaṇa vidhiḥ tam eva iti anya nivṛtteḥ śrutattvāt nivṛttau tātparyam gamyate raktaḥ paṭaḥ bhavati iti tayā rakta para tvam vākyasya atra ākāśa ādi tattva bheda pūrvam avibhāgaḥ pratipāditaḥ tatra tathā eva prajñā karaṇa prasaṅge tam eva iti vidhīyate 
[153,ii^3]	tathā ca pūrva ardhe virajaḥ paraḥ ākāśāt ajaḥ ātmā mahān dhruvaḥ iti ākāśa ādibhyaḥ paratvena ātma tattvam darśitam tasya tathā eva prajñā karaṇa prasaṅge tad nivṛttaye tam eva iti ucyate anyathā naḥ eva śabdasya phalam na ca nivartyam vijñāyeta tathā ca tat eva uttareṇa prapañcyate na anudhyāyāt bahūn śabdān iti eka vākyatā anyathā vākyam bhidyeta śabda mātre ca anudhyāna aprasaṅgāt śabda pūrvat tvāt tasya śabda artha viṣayam eva idam iti evam ātmā iti eva upāsītaḥ iti evakāra śruteḥ tad artha vidhiḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti api ātmanaḥ tu kāmāya iti upakramāt idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā iti upasaṃhārāt ātma svarūpa param ekam vākyam tad antargatāḥ draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti na pṛthagvidhayaḥ kṛtya pratyaya yoge api 
[153,ii^4]	kṛtya pratyayasya artha antare api smaraṇāt arha ādau stuti arthāḥ yathā upāṃśu yāja vākya antargatāḥ viṣṇuḥ upāṃśu yaṣṭavyaḥ iti evamādayaḥ aitat ātmyam idam sarvam tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti bhūtaḥ eva paryavasitam vākyam tatra sat asmi iti dhārayet iti kalpanā iyam tasmāt trividhasya api jñānasya vidheya tva ayogāt vinā ca vidheḥ vākya artha pratipatteḥ apauruṣeya tvena nirapekṣa tvāt bhūte api arthe vedāntānām prāmāṇya siddhiḥ tathā ca tat tu samanvayāt iti codanā lakṣaṇāt dharmāt tu śabdena viśeṣyam brahma samanvaya gamyam uktam samanvayaḥ hi padārthānām saṃsargaḥ viniyogaḥ tatas brahma gamyate na ca udanātaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[155,i_155,ii]	nanu aviśeṣeṇa kārye arthe vedasya prāmāṇyam varṇitam codanā lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ dharmaḥ iti codanā lakṣaṇaḥ veda arthaḥ iti arthaḥ na etat sāram evam hi siddha prāmāṇya veda artha vicāraḥ ayam syāt tad uttara lakṣaṇa vat tatra anantaram prāmāṇya pratipādanam na yujyeta vṛttam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam iti ca mantra artha vādeṣu ca kārya artha tvena vipratipattiḥ na syāt sā ca upariṣṭāt eva nirasiṣyate bahu ca atra vaktavyam iti alam prasaṅgena yathā anya māna vyatibheda muktā matiḥ pramāṇa tvam upaiti kārye apauruṣeya āgama labdha janmā tathā eva siddhe nirapekṣa bhāvāt 
[156,i_156,ii^1]	evam tāvat pratipatti kartavya tā prāmāṇya vyājena yaiḥ aprāmāṇyam uktam tad pratibodhanāya kṛtaḥ prayatnaḥ idānīm tu aprāmāṇyam eva āhuḥ ye tad bodhanāya prayatyate tatra pūrva pakṣaḥ nanu anvita padārtha tvāt vākya arthasya padārtha tām aprāpya na syāt vākya arthaḥ padārtha tve anya mānakaḥ na tāvat brahma antaryāmya ādi padam pramāṇam saṃbandha jñāna apekṣayā pūrva siddhe pratyaya hetu tvena na api vākyam na hi tad sākṣāt vācakam padārtha dvārā tu tat pratipattiḥ apadārthe jñānasya abhāvāt te hi saṃsargāt guṇa pradhāna bhāvena itara padārtha viśiṣṭam ekam padārtham gamayanti tatra padārthaḥ eva viśiṣṭaḥ vākya arthaḥ bhavati na ca anadhigateṣu pramāṇa antareṇa padārtha tvam sambandha jñāna apekṣaṇāt iti uktam tatra āpadārtha tve na vākya viṣaya tvam anavabodhakam teṣām vākyam padārtha tve pramāṇa antara adhigateḥ anuvādakam tatra atyanta aparidṛṣṭa brahma ādi artha pramāṇa abhimateṣu vākyeṣu tad vācīni padāni syuḥ na vā 
[156,ii^2]	yadi na santi na te itaraiḥ saṃsṛjyeran na bhidyeran iti na teṣām prameyāḥ loṣṭa ādi vat atha tu santi tathā api taiḥ adhigata saṃbandhaiḥ na pratipādyeran apratipannāḥ ca na viśiṣṭa vākya artha pratipatti hetavaḥ tatra yathā avanāt pikaḥ ānīyatam iti pika padārtha jñāne avabodhaka tvam tathā teṣām api tasmāt na ca udanātaḥ apūrva padārtha avagamaḥ sā hi vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām kriyāsu puruṣam adhikaroti traividhya vṛddha parigrahaḥ tu japa upayogāt upaniṣadaḥ vedāntāḥ iti tatra viniyogāt tatra ucyate sāmānyena padārtha tve siddhe asādhāraṇaiḥ guṇaiḥ śakyā pūrva viśeṣasya loka vat pratipādanā 
[157,i]	yathā loke dvīpa viśeṣe evaṃnāmānaḥ marataka maya pādāḥ padmarāga maya cañcavaḥ sauvarṇa rājata pakṣāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ iti pakṣi sāmānyam pramāṇa antaradhigatam ananyasādhāraṇena dharma kalāpena saṃsṛjyamānam pramāṇa antara anadhigatam viśeṣa rūpam āsādayati vākyena ca pramīyate pramāṇa antara anadhigatena viśeṣa rūpeṇa sarvasya eva hi vākyasya anadhigataḥ viśeṣaḥ eva prameyaḥ tathā kāraṇa sāmānyam vā sat sāmānyam vā yatas vai imāni bhūtāni jāyante iti asthūlam anaṇva hrasvam ityādi padārthaiḥ saṃsargāt bhedāt ca pramāṇa antara anadhigatam viśeṣa rūpam āsādayati vākyasya ca prameyam bhavati tat evam loka siddha padārtha anvayena eva apūrva artha pratipatteḥ na anavabodhaka tvam anuvādaka tvam vā 
[157,ii_157,iii]	sarva pratyaya vedye vā brahma rūpe vyavasthite prapañcasya pravilayaḥ śabdena pratipādyate pravilīna prapañcena tad rūpeṇa na gocaraḥ māna antarasya iti matam āmnāya eka nibandhanam athavā na loke atyantam aprasiddham brahma sarva pratyaya vedya tvāt brahmaṇaḥ vyatirekeṇa pratyetavyasya abhāvāt viśeṣa pratyayānām ca sāmānya rūpa anugamāt bheda upasaṃhāra avaśiṣṭam ca satyam brahma iti pratipādanāt vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyam iti dṛṣṭāntāt kim tarhi śabdena pratipādyate prapañca abhāvaḥ tatra prapañca padārthaḥ api siddhaḥ niṣedhaḥ api siddhaḥ tayoḥ saṃsargāt tad abhāva pratipattiḥ āmnāya eka nibandhana tvam tu tasya ucyate pratyakṣa ādīnām avidyā saṃbhinna tvāt pratyastamita nikhila bhedena rūpeṇa aviṣayīkaraṇāt bheda pratyasta mayasya āmnāyau agamya tvāt iti 
[157,iv_158,i^1]	paraḥ punar pratyavatiṣṭhate nanu ca apuruṣa artha tvam bhūta niṣṭhe prasajyate yat khalu vākyam na puruṣam kvacid hita sādhane pravartayati ahita sādhanāt ca nivartayati kevalam siddham artham anvācaṣṭe tad apuruṣa artham apuruṣa artha tvāt ca unmatta pralāpa vadapramāṇam tathā ca prāyeṇa vedāntāḥ ucyate pramāṇasya na ca etāvat puruṣa artha eka niṣṭhatā api ca ajñānataḥ śokī duḥkhī jīvaḥ prakāśate tad nivṛttiḥ ca vijñānam puruṣa arthaḥ svayam matam kasmiṃścid arthe vijñāte kutūhalavatām nṛṇām ākulānām jñāna janma puruṣa artha tva saṃmatam akṣa ādau ca yathārūpa niṣṭhe na apuruṣa artha tā na ca pravṛtti niṣṭha tvam tathā asmin kena vāryate jñeyasya puruṣa artha tvam tatra ced atra tad samam puruṣa arthaḥ svayam brahma praśāntam vijarā ādikam atas tat tvam asi iti evam anuśiṣyāya śiṣyate 
[158,i^2]	para pravṛtteḥ aṅga tvam pratyakṣa ādeḥ matam yadi atra api sākṣāt karaṇa pravṛttau aṅgatā iṣya tām na tāvat niyogataḥ pramāṇasya puruṣa artha phala tā na khalu hita upādāna ahita hāne eva pramāṇa phale upekṣām api hi pramāṇa phalam pramāṇa vidaḥ ācakṣate na ca puruṣa artha tā pramāṇa lakṣaṇam pramāhetu tvam tu tasmāt na puruṣa artha abhāvena aprāmāṇyam api ca śokī aham duḥkhī aham dhana ādīni mama naṣṭāni iti viśuddha brahma ātmanaḥ jīvasya mithyājñānam etat nivṛtti rūpam ca viśuddha ānanda prakāśa brahma ātmata tva jñānam tat sva rūpeṇa eva puruṣa arthaḥ aniṣṭa nivṛtti rūpa tva āt iṣṭa āvirbhāvāt ca 
[158,i^3]	yadi api ca saṃskārāt tasya anuvṛttiḥ tathā api śābda jñānam anusaṃtanvataḥ viduṣaḥ na pūrvavat bhavati nivartate ca atyantāya dṛṣṭā ca jñāna utpatteḥ eva puruṣa artha tā kvacid kutūhala ākulitānām ajñāte arthe na hi tad jñānāt param anyadarthyate na ca pravṛtti nivṛtti viṣayasya eva puruṣa artha tā iti niyamaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni hi pramāṇāni na ca tāvat pravṛtti nivṛtti parāṇi siddha vastu viṣayāṇi na ca puruṣa artha tām jahati yadi matam pratyakṣa ādi jñeyam hi siddham vastu puruṣa arthaḥ salila ādiḥ tad upakārāt tatas pratyakṣa ādīnām puruṣa artha tā bhūta niṣṭhānām api 
[158,i^4_159,i]	atra api ca śabda prameyam svayam eva brahma puruṣa arthaḥ jarā ādi vividha aśiva upaśamāt parama ānanda prakāśa tvāt ca su prasannam atas eva tat tvam asi iti śvetaketu mukhena āśāsanīyāya puruṣāya śrutyā abhinnam upadiśyate abhinnam hi tad anuśāsanīyāt bhedena ca pratīyamānam na puruṣa arthaḥ tattve tādātmya jñāne ca tathā abhāvāt viśvāśivā upaśamāt parama śiva bhāvāt ca paripūrṇaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ āptaḥ bhavati yadi matam pratyakṣa ādīni api pravṛti aṅgāni eva pramite arthe hāna upādāna ādi lakṣaṇāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ tad mūla tvāt īdṛśam pravṛti aṅga tvam atra api asti eva śabdāt pramite brahmaṇi sākṣātkaraṇāya pravṛtteḥ iṣṭa tvāt iti eṣā vedānta tattva pravicaya catura prasphurat nyāya tejāḥ mārgam mukteḥ nirundhat nibiḍam api tamaḥ anādi nirdārayantī sadyas prakṣālayantī ghanam api jagatām tīrtha dustarka paṅkam vyākhyāta utkhāta viśvā śiva niratiśaya śreyase brahma siddhiḥ
